# ARCHITECTURE — bdp (Bad Doll Play)

## Source Overview

| Metric | Value |
|--------|-------|
| **Engine** | Unity (IL2CPP build, version inferred from DLLs — likely 2021.3+) |
| **Total project files** | 14,010 (229.05 MB) — from .stub |
| **Game scripts** | 30 `.cs` files in `Assembly-CSharp` |
| **Actual code files** | 28 (excluding auto-generated AssemblyInfo + MonoScriptTypes) |
| **Lines of game logic** | ~1,800 (excluding Lines.cs data) |
| **Localization data** | Lines.cs — 391.7 KB, 33 languages × 214 dialogue entries |
| **Scenes** | 13: Splash, Main, Scene1–Scene10, Exhibition |

### Folder Structure (Scripts)

```
Scripts/
  Assembly-CSharp/          ← game code (30 files)
  com.rlabrecque.steamworks.net/  ← Steamworks.NET (third-party, skip)
  netstandard/              ← runtime (skip)
  RTLTMPro/                 ← Right-to-Left TMP (third-party, skip)
  System/                   ← runtime (skip)
```

---

## Dependency Graph

### Domain Groupings

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  PLAYER CORE                                         │
│  PlayerMovement ← PlayerManager → PlayerInteract     │
│  Item (data-only)                                    │
└────────────────────┬────────────────────────────────┘
                     │ PlayerManager.instance
┌────────────────────▼────────────────────────────────┐
│  INTERACTION LAYER                                    │
│  InteractObject → PlayerManager.instance              │
│  Door → InteractObject                                │
│  TriggerCol / TriggerColLook / TriggerOnLook          │
└────────────────────┬────────────────────────────────┘
                     │
┌────────────────────▼────────────────────────────────┐
│  DIALOGUE & LOCALIZATION                              │
│  Lines (static data) ← Dialogue / Note / Spell        │
│  Dialogue → Lines, Resources.Load (audio)             │
│  Note → Lines, PlayerManager.instance                 │
│  Spell → Lines, Manager4.instance, PlayerManager      │
└────────────────────┬────────────────────────────────┘
                     │
┌────────────────────▼────────────────────────────────┐
│  SCENE MANAGERS (1 per scene, identical pattern)      │
│  Manager1..Manager10                                  │
│  All use: PlayableDirector, Dialogue, PlayerManager   │
│  All follow: singleton + eventIndex switch pattern    │
└────────────────────┬────────────────────────────────┘
                     │
┌────────────────────▼────────────────────────────────┐
│  UI & SETTINGS                                        │
│  Options → PlayerManager, PostProcessVolume           │
│  Main → SFX, SceneManager                             │
│  Credit → ScrollRect                                  │
│  Gallery → PlayerManager                              │
└────────────────────┬────────────────────────────────┘
                     │
┌────────────────────▼────────────────────────────────┐
│  EFFECTS & UTILITY                                    │
│  SFX → Resources.Load (audio)                         │
│  Fade → MeshRenderer                                  │
│  GraBlit → Material (post-process blit)               │
│  Splash → SceneManager                                │
└────────────────────┬────────────────────────────────┘
                     │
┌────────────────────▼────────────────────────────────┐
│  PLATFORM                                             │
│  SteamManager → Steamworks API (third-party)          │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

| Manager10 | SceneManager |
| Dialogue | Lines, Resources.Load |
| InteractObject | PlayerManager.instance |

## God Objects

| File | Lines | Responsibilities | Split Candidate? |
|------|-------|-----------------|-----------------|
| **Lines.cs** | ~10,000+ | Static 33×214 string array (all dialogue in all languages) | YES — extract to external JSON/CSV per language |
| **Manager2.cs** | ~407 | 24 event states, closet puzzles, radio puzzles, food puzzle, post-processing, cutscenes | YES — largest scene manager, 5+ subsystems |
| **Options.cs** | ~200 | Pause menu, language switching, brightness, post-processing filter, mouse sensitivity, font management | YES — UI + settings + fonts + PP |
| **Note.cs** | ~135 | Note reading UI + font management for 12+ languages | Moderate — font logic duplicated with Spell/Options |
| **Spell.cs** | ~110 | Spell reading UI + font management for 12+ languages | Moderate — font logic duplicated with Note/Options |

---

## Singleton Registry

| Singleton | Class | What It Owns | Who Reads It |
|-----------|-------|-------------|-------------|
| `PlayerManager.instance` | PlayerManager | Player movement lock/unlock, item inventory, camera, positioning | Manager1-9, InteractObject, Note, Spell, Options, Gallery |
| `Manager1.instance` | Manager1 | Scene 1 cutscene/dialogue sequencing | (only via UnityEvent in scene) |
| `Manager2.instance` | Manager2 | Scene 2 event sequencing (closets, radio, food) | (only via UnityEvent in scene) |
| `Manager3.instance` | Manager3 | Scene 3 event sequencing | (only via UnityEvent in scene) |
| `Manager4.instance` | Manager4 | Scene 4 event sequencing (hand/grab) | Spell.cs (direct call) |
| `Manager5.instance` | Manager5 | Scene 5 event sequencing (PP effects) | (only via UnityEvent in scene) |
| `Manager6.instance` | Manager6 | Scene 6 event sequencing | (only via UnityEvent in scene) |
| `Manager7.instance` | Manager7 | Scene 7 event sequencing (spell/closet) | (only via UnityEvent in scene) |
| `Manager8.instance` | Manager8 | Scene 8 event sequencing (doll/door) | (only via UnityEvent in scene) |
| `Manager9.instance` | Manager9 | Scene 9 event sequencing (final dialogue) | (only via UnityEvent in scene) |
| `SteamManager.s_instance` | SteamManager | Steam API lifecycle | (internal only) |

---

## Coupling Hotspots

### FindObjectOfType / GameObject.Find Calls
| Location | Call | Risk |
|----------|------|------|
| Options.Start() | `GameObject.Find("UICam")` | Fragile string lookup |
| Options.Start() | `GameObject.Find("PP")` | Fragile string lookup |
| Options.UpdateTextFont() | `GameObject.Find("Dialogue")` | Fragile string lookup |
| InteractObject.InvokeEvent() | `GameObject.Find("Warning")` | Fragile string lookup |
| Manager2.TriggerEvent() case 16 | `GameObject.Find("Player")` | Fragile string lookup |

### Static Instance Access (Cross-Domain)
- Every `Manager*.cs` accesses `PlayerManager.instance` (tight coupling)
- `Spell.cs` accesses `Manager4.instance.TriggerEvent()` (cross-scene coupling)
- `InteractObject` accesses `PlayerManager.instance` for item checks

### Resources.Load Calls (Implicit Dependencies)
| Caller | Resource Path |
|--------|--------------|
| Dialogue | `Sounds/Voice/{role}{1-3}` |
| SFX | `Sounds/SFX/{name}` |
| PlayerMovement | `Sounds/Footstep/Barefoot{1-5}` |
| PlayerManager | `Prefabs/{name}` |
| Manager1-9 | `Timeline/{scene}` |

---

## Event System

### Pattern: UnityEvent (Inspector-Wired)
- `InteractObject.action` — UnityEvent invoked on interaction
- `TriggerCol.action` — UnityEvent on collision/trigger enter
- `TriggerColLook.action` — UnityEvent on trigger + visibility
- `TriggerOnLook.action` — UnityEvent on becoming visible
- `Options.langChangedCallback` — UnityEvent on language change

### Pattern: Callback Delegates
- `Dialogue.StartDialogue(from, to, callback)` — UnityAction passed as completion callback
- All Manager*.cs use anonymous delegates for post-dialogue actions

### No Custom Event Bus
- No C# `event`/`Action` patterns found
- No custom EventManager or message bus
- All communication is direct singleton reference or UnityEvent wiring

---

## Data Flow

```
PlayerPrefs ──→ Options (language, mouse, brightness, filter)
                  ↓
Lines.cs (static) ──→ Dialogue.StartDialogue(from, to) ──→ RTLTextMeshPro
                  ↓
Resources.Load ──→ AudioClip (SFX/Voice), PlayableAsset (Timeline), GameObject (Prefabs)
                  ↓
[SerializeField] ──→ InteractObject, Animator, PostProcessVolume, PlayableDirector
                  ↓
Manager*.eventIndex (int) ──→ switch/case ──→ game state progression
                  ↓
SceneManager.LoadScene ──→ next scene
```

### State Management
- **Scene progression**: Linear Scene1 → Scene10, each with its own Manager singleton
- **Event index**: `int eventIndex` incremented per interaction, drives switch/case
- **Player state**: PlayerManager holds movement lock flags + current held item
- **Settings**: PlayerPrefs (language=int, mouse=float, brightness=float, filter=int)

---

## Inheritance Chains

| Chain | Worth Preserving? |
|-------|------------------|
| `MonoBehaviour` ← all scripts | Standard Unity pattern, preserve |
| No custom base classes | Nothing to flatten |
| No interfaces implemented | None exist |

The codebase is flat — no inheritance hierarchies, no interfaces. Everything inherits directly from `MonoBehaviour` except `Lines` (static class) and `Item` (data component).

# Estimate — bdp (Bad Doll Play)

## Methodology

Hours = File Count × Complexity Tier multiplier

| Tier | Description | Hours/File |
|------|-------------|-----------|
| T1 — Trivial | <30 lines, data-only or boilerplate | 0.25 |
| T2 — Simple | 30–100 lines, single responsibility | 0.5 |
| T3 — Medium | 100–200 lines, multiple concerns | 1.0 |
| T4 — Complex | 200+ lines, god object, many dependencies | 2.0 |
| T5 — Data Migration | External data extraction (Lines.cs) | 4.0 |

- Phase 3 is heaviest due to Lines.cs data migration (33 languages × 214 lines → JSON)
- Phase 5 is large due to 10 manager files + base class extraction
- Most individual files are small (T1–T2) — the project is architecturally simple but repetitive
- Lines.cs dominates file size but is pure data, not complex logic

# GOAL — bdp (Bad Doll Play)

## Project Identity

**Bad Doll Play (bdp)** — A first-person horror narrative game about a child named Ron, his doll, and a dark family secret. Linear 10-scene story with dialogue, item interactions, closet portals, and cutscenes. Supports 33 languages.

---

## Target Architecture

### Folder Structure

```
bdp/
├── _-PlayerSystem/
│   ├── W_PlayerMovement.cs
│   ├── Field_PlayerManager.cs
│   ├── W_PlayerInteract.cs
│   └── Field_Item.cs
├── _-InteractionSystem/
│   ├── W_InteractObject.cs
│   └── W_Door.cs
├── _-TriggerSystem/
│   ├── W_TriggerCol.cs
│   ├── W_TriggerColLook.cs
│   └── W_TriggerOnLook.cs
├── _-DialogueSystem/
│   ├── DataService_Localization.cs
│   ├── DataService_Font.cs
│   ├── W_Dialogue.cs
│   ├── W_Note.cs
│   ├── W_Spell.cs
│   └── W_Credit.cs
├── _-UISystem/
│   ├── W_Options.cs
│   └── W_MainMenu.cs
├── _-AudioSystem/
│   └── W_SFX.cs
├── _-SceneManagerSystem/
│   ├── BaseSceneManager.cs
│   ├── W_SceneManager_Intro.cs
│   ├── W_SceneManager_House.cs
│   ├── W_SceneManager_Cat.cs
│   ├── W_SceneManager_Void.cs
│   ├── W_SceneManager_RedFace.cs
│   ├── W_SceneManager_DollReunion.cs
│   ├── W_SceneManager_SpellDoor.cs
│   ├── W_SceneManager_FinalDoll.cs
│   ├── W_SceneManager_Revelation.cs
│   └── W_SceneManager_Ending.cs
├── _Standalone/
│   ├── W_Fade.cs
│   ├── W_GraBlit.cs
│   ├── W_Splash.cs
│   ├── W_Gallery.cs
│   └── W_SteamManager.cs
└── Data/
    └── Localization/
        ├── en.json
        ├── vi.json
        ├── zh.json
        └── ... (33 language files)
```

---

## Naming Conventions

| Prefix | Meaning | Example |
|--------|---------|---------|
| `W_` | MonoBehaviour worker (lives on a GameObject) | `W_PlayerMovement` |
| `Field_` | Singleton/manager that holds runtime state | `Field_PlayerManager` |
| `DataService_` | Pure C# service (no MonoBehaviour) | `DataService_Localization` |
| `SO_` | ScriptableObject data asset | `SO_SceneConfig` |
| `I` | Interface | `IPlayerFacade` |

---

## Class Responsibilities

### Single Responsibility Rules
1. **MonoBehaviour workers** (`W_`) handle ONE Unity concern: rendering, input, physics, or animation
2. **Field singletons** (`Field_`) hold runtime state and expose a clean API — no direct Unity input handling
3. **DataServices** contain pure logic testable without Unity — no `MonoBehaviour`, no `GameObject.Find`, no `Resources.Load`
4. **Interfaces** define communication contracts between systems — no system should reference another system's concrete class

### Forbidden Patterns
- ❌ `GameObject.Find("anything")` — inject via `[SerializeField]` or interface
- ❌ `Resources.Load` scattered everywhere — centralize in service or use addressables
- ❌ Hardcoded string data in C# files — use external JSON/CSV
- ❌ Copy-pasted font selection logic — extract to `DataService_Font`
- ❌ 10 identical Manager classes with no shared base — extract `BaseSceneManager`
- ❌ Static singleton access across systems — inject via interface or constructor

---

## Decoupling Patterns

### 1. Singleton → Interface Injection
**Before:** `PlayerManager.instance.LockAll()`
**After:** Scene managers receive `IPlayerFacade` via `[SerializeField]` or inject

### 2. Hardcoded Data → External Files
**Before:** `Lines.cs` — 391.7 KB static 2D string array
**After:** `DataService_Localization` loads JSON files per language at runtime

### 3. Duplicated Logic → Shared Service
**Before:** Font selection in Note.cs, Spell.cs, Options.cs, Dialogue.cs (4 copies)
**After:** `DataService_Font.GetFont(languageId)` returns `(TMP_FontAsset, float fontSize)`

### 4. God Manager → Base Class
**Before:** 10 identical Manager*.cs with copy-pasted PlayCutscene, TriggerEvent, singleton pattern
**After:** `BaseSceneManager` provides shared infrastructure; subclasses override event handling

### 5. String Scene Loading → Enum/Const
**Before:** `SceneManager.LoadScene("Scene2")`
**After:** `SceneManager.LoadScene(SceneId.Scene2)` with enum or const class

---

## Lifecycle Rules

### Scene Loading
1. Each scene has exactly ONE scene manager (`W_SceneManager_*`)
2. Scene manager sets up initial state in `Start()` (lock/unlock, arrange player)
3. Events progress via `TriggerEvent()` driven by UnityEvent from scene objects
4. Scene exits via `SceneManager.LoadScene` with fade-to-black

### Player State
1. `Field_PlayerManager` initializes in `Awake()` (singleton assignment)
2. Movement and interaction locked/unlocked per scene requirements
3. Items are instantiated as children of the camera, one at a time
4. Items destroyed on scene transition (not persisted)

### Dialogue Flow
1. Scene manager pauses PlayableDirector
2. Calls `Dialogue.StartDialogue(from, to, callback)`
3. Typewriter effect plays with voice blips
4. Player input advances/skips dialogue
5. Callback fires → typically resumes PlayableDirector

---

## C# Features & Patterns

### Use
- `switch` expressions (already used in Dialogue.GetRole)
- `?.` null-conditional operators (already used)
- `delegate` anonymous methods (already used for callbacks)
- Coroutines for timed sequences (established pattern)
- `[SerializeField]` for all inspector dependencies

### Avoid
- `async/await` (Unity coroutines are the established pattern here)
- Generic type parameters (project is simple enough not to need them)
- Reflection-based systems (keep it straightforward)

---

## Testing Strategy

### Phase 1 — Player Core
- Manual test: walk, look, sprint, pick up item, interact
- Verify lock/unlock states work correctly

### Phase 2 — Interaction & Triggers
- Test: required item gating, trigger enter events, visibility triggers
- Verify one-shot triggers don't re-fire

### Phase 3 — Dialogue & Localization
- Test: typewriter effect, skip, multi-line dialogue, RTL languages
- Verify all 33 language indices map to correct data
- Verify font switching per language

### Phase 4 — UI & Settings
- Test: pause menu toggle, language change persists, brightness/filter cycle
- Verify settings survive scene reload

### Phase 5 — Scene Managers
- Test each scene: full event sequence, cutscene pause/resume, scene transitions
- Verify linear progression Scene1→Scene10
- Manager2 needs extra attention (24 events, most complex scene)

### Phase 6 — Platform
- Test: Steam overlay, Steam init/shutdown
- Verify graceful degradation if Steam not running

---

| 3 | Dialogue & Localization | 5 | ★★★ Hard | 25% |
| 4 | UI, Settings & Effects | 7 | ★★☆ Medium | 15% |
| 5 | Scene Managers | 11 | ★★☆ Medium | 20% |
| 6 | Platform Integration | 1 | ★☆☆ Easy | 5% |

---

## Phase 1 — Player Core

**Depends on:** Nothing (foundation layer)

### File List
| File | Lines | Role |
|------|-------|------|
| PlayerMovement.cs | ~170 | First-person movement, mouse look, sprinting, footstep audio |
| PlayerManager.cs | ~100 | Singleton facade: lock/unlock movement, item inventory, camera positioning |
| PlayerInteract.cs | ~50 | Raycast interaction system, cursor icon toggle |
| Item.cs | ~5 | Data component: `string itemName` |

### What It Looks Like When Running
A first-person character walks around a 3D environment. The player can look with the mouse, move with WASD, sprint with Shift. A cursor icon appears when looking at interactable objects. The player can pick up and hold one item at a time.

### Key Patterns
- `PlayerManager.instance` singleton is the central facade
- Movement uses Rigidbody physics (`rb.velocity`)
- Items instantiated from `Resources/Prefabs/` and parented to camera
- Footstep audio loaded via `Resources.Load`

### Risks
- `PlayerManager` is accessed by nearly every other script in the project
- `Resources.Load` for footsteps and items (implicit coupling)

---

## Phase 2 — Interaction & Triggers

**Depends on:** Phase 1 (PlayerManager for item checks)

### File List
| File | Lines | Role |
|------|-------|------|
| InteractObject.cs | ~55 | Item-gated interaction with UnityEvent callbacks |
| Door.cs | ~22 | Animated door open via InteractObject |
| TriggerCol.cs | ~40 | Collider/trigger enter → fire UnityEvent (one-shot) |
| TriggerColLook.cs | ~45 | Trigger + visibility check → fire UnityEvent |
| TriggerOnLook.cs | ~12 | Visibility-based trigger (OnBecameVisible) |

### What It Looks Like When Running
Objects in the scene can be interacted with by pressing E or clicking. Some require holding a specific item. Trigger volumes fire events when the player enters them. Some triggers require the player to also be looking at an object.

### Key Patterns
- UnityEvent for all trigger/interaction callbacks (inspector-wired)
- `InteractObject` supports required items, event replacement at runtime
- `GameObject.Find("Warning")` in InteractObject — fragile

### Risks
- `InteractObject.InvokeEvent()` directly calls `PlayerManager.instance` — tight coupling
- String-based item matching (`requiredItem == "Meal"`)

---

## Phase 3 — Dialogue & Localization

**Depends on:** Phase 1 (PlayerManager for lock/unlock), Phase 2 (InteractObject for Note/Spell interaction)

### File List
| File | Lines | Role |
|------|-------|------|
| Lines.cs | ~10,000+ | Static 2D string array: 33 languages × 214 dialogue lines |
| Dialogue.cs | ~170 | Typewriter-effect dialogue display, RTL support, voice audio |
| Note.cs | ~135 | In-game note reading UI with per-language font selection |
| Spell.cs | ~110 | Spell text reading UI with per-language font selection |
| Credit.cs | ~20 | Credit scroll screen |

### What It Looks Like When Running
When dialogue triggers, a text box appears with a typewriter effect. Characters speak with voice blips. The player can skip by clicking/pressing Space. Notes and spells display full-screen text overlays. Text renders correctly in 33 languages including RTL (Arabic, Persian).

### Key Patterns
- `Lines.getLine(index)` returns localized string based on `PlayerPrefs.GetInt("language")`
- Dialogue lines use `|` separator: `"1|text"` where `1` = character role ID
- Font switching duplicated across Dialogue, Note, Spell, and Options (DRY violation)
- RTL support via RTLTMPro library

### Risks
- Lines.cs is 391.7 KB of hardcoded strings — unmaintainable, should be external data
- Font selection logic copy-pasted 4 times across Note, Spell, Options, Dialogue
- `Spell.cs` directly calls `Manager4.instance.TriggerEvent()` — cross-phase coupling

---

## Phase 4 — UI, Settings & Effects

**Depends on:** Phase 1 (PlayerManager for mouse sensitivity), Phase 3 (Options font callback)

### File List
| File | Lines | Role |
|------|-------|------|
| Options.cs | ~200 | Pause menu, language dropdown, brightness, post-process filter, mouse sens |
| Main.cs | ~85 | Main menu (Play, Options, social links, Gallery, Exit) |
| SFX.cs | ~30 | Audio clip player (play once, play loop, stop) |
| Fade.cs | ~20 | Animated mesh alpha fade |
| GraBlit.cs | ~25 | Multi-pass post-processing blit |
| Splash.cs | ~15 | Splash screen with 6s delay then load Main |
| Gallery.cs | ~15 | Exhibition scene — positions player |

### What It Looks Like When Running
The game boots to a splash screen, then the main menu. Options allow language selection (33 languages), brightness adjustment, mouse sensitivity, and post-processing filter cycling. During gameplay, ESC opens the pause menu. SFX plays one-shot or looping audio.

### Key Patterns
- `PlayerPrefs` for all settings persistence
- `GameObject.Find` for UI camera, PP volume, dialogue text (fragile)
- Post-processing filter cycling via `PostProcessProfile[]` array
- Keyboard shortcuts (1-5) for in-game settings adjustment

### Risks
- `Options` uses 3 `GameObject.Find` calls
- Language font logic duplicated from Phase 3

---

## Phase 5 — Scene Managers

**Depends on:** Phases 1–4 (all previous phases)

### File List
| File | Lines | Scene | Event Count |
|------|-------|-------|-------------|
| Manager1.cs | ~95 | Scene1 (Intro) | 10 events |
| Manager2.cs | ~407 | Scene2 (House exploration) | 24 events |
| Manager3.cs | ~100 | Scene3 (Cat encounter) | 7 events |
| Manager4.cs | ~95 | Scene4 (Dad's prison / Void) | 3 events |
| Manager5.cs | ~120 | Scene5 (RedFace encounter) | 12 events |
| Manager6.cs | ~100 | Scene6 (Doll reunion) | 6 events |
| Manager7.cs | ~100 | Scene7 (Spell door) | 5 events |
| Manager8.cs | ~180 | Scene8 (Final doll sequence) | 16 events |
| Manager9.cs | ~130 | Scene9 (Revelation cutscene) | 13 events |
| Manager10.cs | ~14 | Scene10 (Ending) | 1 event |
| (Splash/Gallery already in Phase 4) | | | |

### What It Looks Like When Running
Each scene runs a linear sequence of events: cutscenes play via Timeline, dialogue triggers at specific points, objects become interactable at the right moment, and the scene loads the next one when complete. The story progresses linearly from Scene1 to Scene10.

### Key Patterns
- **Identical architecture per manager**: singleton + `int eventIndex` + `switch/case TriggerEvent()`
- Timeline cutscenes via `PlayableDirector` (pause/resume/stop pattern)
- Dialogue inserted mid-cutscene via director.Pause() → dialogue → director.Resume()
- Scene transitions via `SceneManager.LoadScene` with black fade
- Each manager wires InteractObjects to advance `eventIndex`

### Risks
- 10 nearly identical manager classes with no shared base class
- Manager2 is a god object (24 events, 13 InteractObject references)
- Scene loading is string-based (`"Scene1"`, `"Scene2"`, etc.)

---

## Phase 6 — Platform Integration

**Depends on:** Nothing (standalone)

### File List
| File | Lines | Role |
|------|-------|------|
| SteamManager.cs | ~100 | Standard Steamworks.NET integration (init, shutdown, callbacks) |

### What It Looks Like When Running
Steam overlay works, achievements could be tracked (no achievement calls in game code). Steam API initializes on launch, shuts down on quit.

### Key Patterns
- Standard `SteamManager` boilerplate from Steamworks.NET
- `DontDestroyOnLoad` singleton
- AppId: 3205080

### Risks
- None significant — standard third-party integration

---

## Cross-Phase Modification Table

| If You Change... | You Must Also Check... |
|-----------------|----------------------|
| PlayerManager API | Manager1–9, InteractObject, Note, Spell, Options, Gallery |
| InteractObject API | Door, Manager2/3/4/6/7/8 (many [SerializeField] refs) |
| Dialogue API | Manager1–9 (all call StartDialogue) |
| Lines.cs data | Dialogue, Note, Spell (all call Lines.getLine) |
| Lines.cs language indices | Options, Note, Spell, Dialogue (all check PlayerPrefs language) |
| Options font logic | Note.UpdateTextFont, Spell.UpdateTextFont (duplicated logic) |
| PostProcessProfile setup | Options, Manager2, Manager5 |
| SFX API | Manager2/4/5/9, Main |
| SceneManager scene names | Manager1–10, Main, Splash (string-based loads) |
| PlayerPrefs keys | Options, Note, Spell, Dialogue, PlayerMovement |

## Scene Flow Diagram

```
Splash
  ↓ (6s delay)
Main (Menu)
  ↓ Play
Scene1 (Manager1) ──→ Scene2 (Manager2) ──→ Scene3 (Manager3)
  ↓                                            ↓
Scene4 (Manager4) ←────────────────────────────┘
  ↓
Scene5 (Manager5) ──→ Scene6 (Manager6) ──→ Scene7 (Manager7)
  ↓
Scene8 (Manager8) ──→ Scene9 (Manager9) ──→ Scene10 (Manager10)
  ↓
Main (back to menu)

Main → Exhibition (Gallery)
```

# StructureMap — bdp (Bad Doll Play)

## Phase 1 — Player Core

### System Folders
| Folder | Files | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| `_-PlayerSystem/` | PlayerMovement, PlayerManager, PlayerInteract, Item | 4 tightly coupled files: Manager orchestrates Movement + Interact, all share player state |

### DataService Candidates
| Candidate | Extractable Logic |
|-----------|------------------|
| `PlayerInventoryService` | Item add/remove/check logic from PlayerManager (pure C# — no MonoBehaviour needed) |

### Interface Candidates
| Interface | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `IPlayerFacade` | Decouple Manager scripts from direct PlayerManager.instance access — expose LockAll/UnlockAll/AddItem/RemoveItem |

### Naming Assignments
| Original | New Name | Prefix |
|----------|----------|--------|
| PlayerMovement | W_PlayerMovement | W (MonoBehaviour worker) |
| PlayerManager | Field_PlayerManager | Field (singleton facade) |
| PlayerInteract | W_PlayerInteract | W (MonoBehaviour worker) |
| Item | SO_Item or Field_Item | Stays as data component |

---

## Phase 2 — Interaction & Triggers

### System Folders
| Folder | Files | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| `_-InteractionSystem/` | InteractObject, Door | Interaction logic + door (uses InteractObject) |
| `_-TriggerSystem/` | TriggerCol, TriggerColLook, TriggerOnLook | 3 trigger variants, same pattern |

### DataService Candidates
| Candidate | Extractable Logic |
|-----------|------------------|
| `InteractionService` | Item requirement validation from InteractObject.InvokeEvent() — currently calls PlayerManager directly |

### Interface Candidates
| Interface | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `IInteractable` | Standardize interaction contract (currently only InteractObject, but could be extended) |
| `ITriggerHandler` | Unify trigger patterns — all 3 trigger classes share action + destroy + triggered pattern |

### Naming Assignments
| Original | New Name | Prefix |
|----------|----------|--------|
| InteractObject | W_InteractObject | W |
| Door | W_Door | W |
| TriggerCol | W_TriggerCol | W |
| TriggerColLook | W_TriggerColLook | W |
| TriggerOnLook | W_TriggerOnLook | W |

---

## Phase 3 — Dialogue & Localization

### System Folders
| Folder | Files | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| `_-DialogueSystem/` | Dialogue, Lines, Note, Spell, Credit | 5 files: all handle text display/localization |

### DataService Candidates
| Candidate | Extractable Logic |
|-----------|------------------|
| `LocalizationService` | Extract from Lines.cs — load language data from external JSON files instead of hardcoded 2D array. Provide `GetLine(index)` and `GetLanguageId()` |
| `FontService` | Extract duplicated font-selection logic from Note, Spell, Options, Dialogue into a single service that maps language ID → TMP_FontAsset + fontSize |

### Interface Candidates
| Interface | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `ILocalizable` | For any UI component that needs font/text updates on language change |
| `IReadableUI` | Shared contract for Note and Spell (both: show text → wait for input → close) |

### Naming Assignments
| Original | New Name | Prefix |
|----------|----------|--------|
| Lines | DataService_Localization | DataService (pure C#) |
| Dialogue | W_Dialogue | W |
| Note | W_Note | W |
| Spell | W_Spell | W |
| Credit | W_Credit | W |

---

| `SettingsService` | Extract PlayerPrefs read/write from Options into pure C# service. Centralize language, mouse, brightness, filter settings |

### Interface Candidates
| Interface | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `ISettingsProvider` | Decouple Options/PlayerMovement from direct PlayerPrefs access |

### Naming Assignments

## Cross-Phase Service Dependencies

```
Phase 1: PlayerCore
  └─ IPlayerFacade ←──────── Phase 2, 3, 4, 5

Phase 2: Interaction
  └─ IInteractable ←──────── Phase 5 (Managers wire InteractObjects)

Phase 3: Dialogue & Localization
  ├─ LocalizationService ←── Phase 3 (Dialogue, Note, Spell), Phase 4 (Options)
  └─ FontService ←────────── Phase 3 (Note, Spell), Phase 4 (Options)

Phase 4: UI & Settings
  ├─ SettingsService ←─────── Phase 1 (PlayerMovement mouse), Phase 4 (Options)
  └─ AudioService ←────────── Phase 1 (footsteps), Phase 3 (voice), Phase 4 (SFX), Phase 5 (music)

Phase 5: Scene Managers
  └─ CutsceneService ←─────── Phase 5 only (all Managers)
```

## Duplication Map

| Duplicated Logic | Found In | Extraction Target |
|-----------------|----------|------------------|
| Font selection (language → TMP_FontAsset + size) | Note, Spell, Options, Dialogue | FontService |
| `Resources.Load<AudioClip>("Sounds/...")` | SFX, Dialogue, PlayerMovement | AudioService |
| `Resources.Load<PlayableAsset>("Timeline/...")` | Manager1–9 (PlayCutscene method) | CutsceneService or base class |
| `PlayerManager.instance.LockAll/UnlockAll` | Manager1–9 | Base class method or ISceneManager |
| `director.Pause(); dialogue.StartDialogue(..., delegate { director.Resume(); });` | Manager1–9 (30+ occurrences) | Base class helper |
| PlayerPrefs read/write | Options, PlayerMovement, Dialogue, Note, Spell | SettingsService |
| `IStepInCloset` coroutine pattern | Manager2, Manager3, Manager6, Manager7 | Base class method |

<!-- ==== FILE: LEARN/bdp/SystemPortabilityMap.md ==== -->
# SystemPortabilityMap — bdp (Bad Doll Play)

## Classification

- **L0** — Project-specific, not reusable. Tightly coupled to bdp game logic, scenes, or story.
- **L1+** — Portable / reusable. Could be extracted to a shared library or used in another project with minimal changes.

---

## Per-System Classification

### Phase 1 — Player Core

| Script | Classification | Rationale |
|--------|---------------|-----------|
| PlayerMovement | **L1+** | Generic first-person controller — walkspeed, mouse look, sprint, rigidbody movement. Fully reusable. |
| PlayerManager | **L0** | Facade that combines movement + interact + items. API is generic but singleton wiring is project-specific. |
| PlayerInteract | **L1+** | Generic raycast interaction — detects InteractObject, shows cursor. Reusable in any first-person game. |
| Item | **L1+** | Trivial data component (`string itemName`). Fully reusable. |

### Phase 2 — Interaction & Triggers

| Script | Classification | Rationale |
|--------|---------------|-----------|
| InteractObject | **L1+** | Generic interaction point with required item + UnityEvent. Reusable pattern. |
| Door | **L1+** | Generic animated door. Reusable. |
| TriggerCol | **L1+** | Generic one-shot trigger event. Reusable. |
| TriggerColLook | **L1+** | Generic trigger + visibility event. Reusable. |
| TriggerOnLook | **L1+** | Generic visibility trigger. Reusable. |

### Phase 3 — Dialogue & Localization

| Script | Classification | Rationale |
|--------|---------------|-----------|
| Lines | **L0** | Hardcoded bdp dialogue in 33 languages. Completely project-specific data. |
| Dialogue | **L1+** (after refactor) | Typewriter dialogue system with RTL support. Core mechanic is reusable; currently coupled to Lines.cs. |
| Note | **L0** | Note UI tied to specific game items (fridge interaction). Font logic is extractable. |
| Spell | **L0** | Spell UI tied to Manager4.instance. Completely project-specific. |
| Credit | **L1+** | Generic credit scroll. Reusable. |

### Phase 4 — UI, Settings & Effects

| Script | Classification | Rationale |
|--------|---------------|-----------|
| Options | **L0** | Project-specific settings (language indices, filter profiles). Core logic (pause, brightness) could be L1+ after refactor. |
| Main | **L0** | bdp-specific main menu (hardcoded social URLs, scene names). |
| SFX | **L1+** | Generic audio player (play, loop, stop via Resources.Load). Reusable. |
| Fade | **L1+** | Generic mesh alpha fader. Reusable. |
| GraBlit | **L1+** | Generic multi-pass blit effect. Reusable. |
| Splash | **L0** | Hardcoded 1120×832 resolution, 6s delay. Project-specific. |
| Gallery | **L0** | bdp Exhibition scene startup. |

### Phase 5 — Scene Managers

| Script | Classification | Rationale |
|--------|---------------|-----------|
| Manager1–10 | **L0** | All contain hardcoded event sequences, dialogue line indices, scene names. 100% project-specific. |
| BaseSceneManager (proposed) | **L1+** | The shared pattern (singleton + eventIndex + PlayableDirector + dialogue integration) is reusable as a framework. |

### Phase 6 — Platform Integration

| Script | Classification | Rationale |
|--------|---------------|-----------|
| SteamManager | **L1+** | Standard Steamworks.NET boilerplate. Reusable across any Steam game. |

---

## Summary

| Classification | Count | Scripts |
|---------------|-------|---------|
| **L0** (project-specific) | 17 | Lines, Note, Spell, Options, Main, Splash, Gallery, Manager1–10 |
| **L1+** (portable) | 13 | PlayerMovement, PlayerInteract, Item, InteractObject, Door, TriggerCol, TriggerColLook, TriggerOnLook, Dialogue*, Credit, SFX, Fade, GraBlit, SteamManager |

*Dialogue becomes L1+ after decoupling from Lines.cs

### Portability Score: 39% L1+ (13/33 scripts)

The project's reusable core is the first-person controller, interaction system, trigger system, and audio utility. All story/scene logic is project-specific and accounts for the majority of files.

<!-- ==== FILE: LEARN/bdp/surfer.md ==== -->
# Surfer — bdp (Bad Doll Play)

## Prompt 1: Initial Source Analysis

**Date:** 2025-05-16
**Action:** Full source analysis of bdp project

### What Was Done
- Verified `MAIN-SOURCE/bdp/` contains Scripts/ and Assemblies/
- Read `entire-bdp.stub` — 14,010 files, 229.05 MB total project
- Identified game code in `Scripts/Assembly-CSharp/` — 30 .cs files
- Read every `.cs` file in Assembly-CSharp (all 30)
- Identified third-party code to skip: Steamworks.NET, RTLTMPro, System/, netstandard/
- Mapped full dependency graph, singleton registry, coupling hotspots

### Key Findings
- **Small codebase**: ~1,800 lines of game logic + 391.7 KB of localization data (Lines.cs)
- **Horror narrative game**: First-person, linear 10-scene story about a child, a doll, and family tragedy
- **33 languages** supported via hardcoded static 2D string array
- **10 identical scene managers** (Manager1–10) with no shared base class
- **Font selection logic duplicated 4 times** across Note, Spell, Options, Dialogue
- **5 `GameObject.Find` calls** — fragile string lookups
- **No custom event bus** — all communication via singletons + UnityEvent

### Documents Generated
1. `ARCHITECTURE.md` — Full source analysis, dependency graph, god objects, singletons, coupling, events, data flow
2. `PhaseMap.md` — 6 phases by dependency order with cross-phase mod tables
3. `StructureMap.md` — System folders, DataService candidates, interfaces, naming
4. `GOAL.md` — Architecture rules, naming conventions, decoupling patterns, testing strategy
5. `Estimate.md` — 34.5 hours total across 6 phases
6. `SystemPortabilityMap.md` — 39% L1+ portable, 61% L0 project-specific
7. `surfer.md` — This file

# ARCHITECTURE — Besiege (bsge)

## Source Overview

| Metric | Value |
|--------|-------|
| **Engine** | Unity 5.x (IL2CPP compatible) |
| **Total Project Files** | 25,193 |
| **Total Project Size** | 18.079 GB |
| **Game Code Files (.cs)** | ~2,456 (Assembly-CSharp) |
| **Third-Party SDK Files (.cs)** | ~2,383 (Assembly-CSharp-firstpass) |
| **DLL Assemblies** | 48 |
| **Asset Categories** | 10+ (Mesh, AudioClip, Texture2D, Shader, Material, Sprite, Prefab, Font, Cubemap, RenderTexture) |

### Folder Structure

```
bsge/
├── Assemblies/          # 48 compiled DLLs
├── Assets/              # ~22,000+ asset files (18 GB)
│   ├── AudioClip/       # ~400 audio files (ogg, wav)
│   ├── Mesh/            # ~2,000+ 3D models (glb)
│   ├── Texture2D/       # ~1,000+ textures (png)
│   ├── Shader/          # ~200+ compiled shaders
│   ├── Material/        # Hundreds of material definitions
│   ├── Sprite/          # UI sprites
│   ├── Font/            # 20+ font files (ttf, otf)
│   ├── Cubemap/         # ~40 cubemaps
│   ├── PrefabHierarchyObject/  # ~500+ prefab hierarchies
│   ├── RenderTexture/   # ~100+ render targets
│   └── Resources/       # Config, localization, templates
└── Scripts/
    ├── Assembly-CSharp/           # 2,456 game code files
    │   ├── AutoSave/              # Auto-save system
    │   ├── Besiege/               # Core utilities, networking, tooltips
    │   ├── BesiegeDlc/            # DLC management (6 files)
    │   ├── BlockMapperInternal/   # Block property widgets (7 files)
    │   ├── cakeslice/             # Outline rendering (6 files)
    │   ├── CodeAnimo/             # Animation/mesh generation
    │   ├── DynamicFogAndMist/     # Fog system (10 files)
    │   ├── GameAnalyticsSDK/      # Analytics
    │   ├── Interface/             # QuickSelect UI
    │   ├── InternalModding/       # Internal modding API
    │   ├── Localisation/          # Translation (4 files)
    │   ├── Modding/               # Public modding API (20+ files)
    │   ├── ModIO/                 # Mod.io UI
    │   ├── SRDebugger/            # Debug UI
    │   ├── SRF/                   # Service framework (8+ files)
    │   ├── VolumetricFogAndMist/  # Advanced fog effects
    │   └── XMLTypes/              # XML serialization
    ├── Assembly-CSharp-firstpass/ # 2,383 third-party SDK files
    │   ├── XGamingRuntime/        # Xbox SDK (~1,000 files)
    │   ├── PlayFab/               # Azure cloud (~500 files)
    │   ├── Steamworks/            # Steam SDK (~200 files)
    │   ├── ModIO/                 # Mod.io SDK (~150 files)
    │   ├── PartyXBLCSharpSDK/     # Xbox Live party (~200 files)
    │   ├── PartyCSharpSDK/        # Cross-platform party (~150 files)
    │   ├── NATTraversal/          # NAT traversal (~100 files)
    │   └── CSharpCompiler/        # IL2CPP support (~50 files)
    └── (other DLL-based script folders — no game logic)
```

---

## Dependency Graph

### Core Layer (no game dependencies)

```
SingleInstance<T> / SingleInstanceBase<T> / SingleInstanceFindOnly<T>
    ↑ used by all singletons
StaticSettings          — file paths, constants
BesiegeConfig           — serialized player prefs
XDataHolder / XData     — generic key-value data container
```

### Framework Layer (depends on Core)

```
StatMaster              → BesiegeConfig, StaticSettings
ReferenceMaster         → (pure event hub, 100+ static events)
PrefabMaster            → StatMaster (block/entity prefab registry)
STATLORD                → StatMaster (stats tracking)
SCREENLORD              → StatMaster (screen management)
LEVELLORD               → StatMaster (level completion tracking)
InputManager            → StatMaster (hotkey mapping)
```

### Data Layer (depends on Framework)

```
MapperType / MKey / MSlider / MToggle / MValue / MLimits / MLogic
    ↑ block property system (drives BlockMapper UI)
SaveableDataHolder      → MapperType, XDataHolder
MachineInfo             → XDataHolder, CLZF2 compression
XmlLoader / XmlSaver    → MachineInfo, BlockType, XData
```

### Block Layer (depends on Data)

```
BlockBehaviour          → SaveableDataHolder, BlockType, BlockJoint
    ├── BuildSurface    → BlockBehaviour (surface panels)
    ├── CanonBlock      → BlockBehaviour (cannons)
    ├── FlamethrowerController → BlockBehaviour
    ├── SteeringWheel   → BlockBehaviour
    ├── PropellorController → BlockBehaviour
    ├── GrabberBlock    → BlockBehaviour
    ├── SailBlock       → BlockBehaviour
    ├── TimedRocket     → BlockBehaviour
    ├── BuoyancyController → BlockBehaviour
    ├── WireController  → BlockBehaviour
    ├── SpringCode      → BlockBehaviour
    ├── BraceCode       → BlockBehaviour
    ├── SensorBlock     → BlockBehaviour
    ├── LogicGate       → BlockBehaviour
    └── (~90 block type implementations)
BlockJoint              → ConfigurableJoint/HingeJoint wrappers
BlockLink / BlockLinkManager → graph topology (nodes + edges)
BlockCluster            → connected component grouping
BlockMapper             → MapperType widgets → UI
BlockVisualController   → skins, glow, highlight rendering
AddPiece                → PrefabMaster, BlockBehaviour, ghost blocks
```

### Machine Layer (depends on Block)

```
Machine                 → BlockBehaviour[], BlockLinkManager, MachineAnalyzer
    └── ServerMachine   → Machine + networking (PlayerData, damage tracking)
MachineAnalyzer         → Machine, BlockCluster (async topology analysis)
MachineDamageController → Machine, BlockHealthBar
UndoSystem              → Machine, command pattern (9+ action types)
NodeController          → Machine, building grid
KeyInputController      → Machine, bit-packed input state
```

### Physics & Effects Layer (depends on Machine)

```
FireController          → BlockBehaviour (combustion, spread, water interaction)
ExplosionEffect         → Rigidbody, BlockHealthBar
WaterController         → BuoyancyController, static build/sim instances
TimeSlider              → FPS-based auto-timescale
BuildSurface            → mesh generation, aerodynamics, breaking
```

### AI Layer (depends on Physics)

```
EntityAI                → ITarget, Faction, AttackScript, KillingHandler
    ├── Targeting       → Machine.Active(), BlockBehaviour
    ├── Movement        → NavMesh-free physics locomotion
    ├── Combat          → AttackScript, range/melee
    └── Morale          → Faction loss tracking
AttackScript            → EntityAI (ray/trigger/capsule attacks)
ArcherAI                → ProjectilePhysArc (ballistic prediction)
KillingHandler          → IExplosionEffect (death, gibbing, suffocation)
Faction / FactionsController → EntityAI[] roster, loss calculation
FreighterAI             → balloon buoyancy, victory points
```

### Level Layer (depends on AI)

```
LevelEditor             → LevelEntity, EntityController, LevelGhostManager
LevelEntity             → NetworkBlock, ISelectable, GenericEntity
GenericEntity           → SaveableDataHolder, EntityLogic
    └── AIGenericEntity → GenericEntity + EntityAI properties
CustomLevel             → LevelEntity[], FrameBufferManager, logic execution
LevelPrefab             → entity template/metadata
WinCondition            → objective tracking, victory screen
LevelSelectController   → campaign map navigation
LevelEnvironmentManager → lighting, fog, water per-environment
LevelDataManager        → network frame serialization
```

### UI Layer (depends on Level)

```
UIManager               → canvas management
CanvasInputController   → input routing
BlockMapper             → MapperType → widget rendering
FileBrowserController   → machine/level file browsing
AdvancedBlockEditor     → extended block properties
AdvancedUIController    → options/settings UI
```

### Network Layer (cross-cutting)

```
BesiegeNetworkManager   → TransportNetworkManager wrapper
NetworkController       → frame compression, entity diffing
NetworkScene            → connection state machine (IP/Steam/PlayFab)
NetworkBlock            → per-block sync
ServerMachine           → Machine + network encoding/decoding
NetworkAuxAddPiece      → networked block placement (112 KB god object)
ProjectileManager       → pooled projectile sync
LevelDataManager        → level state serialization
```

### Modding Layer (depends on all)

```
ModEntryPoint (abstract) → mod lifecycle hooks
ModResources             → async asset loading
ModEvents / ModTriggers  → custom event system
ModNetworking            → custom RPC
ModKeys / ModConsole     → input/console extensions
ModSettings              → persistent mod config
Mods (static)            → mod registry
```

### Platform/DLC Layer (cross-cutting)

```
DlcManager               → DLC validation
SteamDlcProvider         → Steam-specific DLC
SteamManager             → Steam API wrapper
SteamWorkshopManager     → Workshop integration
AchievementManager       → achievement tracking
BesiegeEntryPoint        → bootstrap + CLI argument routing
```

## God Objects (>200 lines, 3+ responsibilities)

| File | Size | Responsibilities | Split Candidates |
|------|------|-----------------|------------------|
| **VolumetricFog.cs** | 140 KB | Fog rendering, density, noise, shadows, lighting | Third-party asset — skip |
| **NetworkAuxAddPiece.cs** | 113 KB | Block placement, networking, synchronization, validation, ghost blocks, multiplayer sync | NetworkBlockPlacer, BlockPlacementValidator, GhostBlockSync |
| **iTween.cs** | 111 KB | Animation engine (tweening, easing, callbacks) | Third-party — skip |
| **BuildSurface.cs** | 93 KB | Mesh generation, colliders, aerodynamics, breaking, materials, fire, tiling, drag | SurfaceMeshBuilder, SurfacePhysics, SurfaceAerodynamics, SurfaceBreaker |
| **Machine.cs** | 89 KB | Block management, simulation lifecycle, physics, undo integration, DLC tracking, connectivity | MachineSimulation, MachineBlockManager, MachineConnectivity |
| **EntityAI.cs** | 82 KB | AI state machine, targeting, movement, combat, morale, faction, death, physics | AIStateMachine, AITargeting, AIMovement, AICombat, AIMorale |
| **cInput.cs** | 68 KB | Custom input system (keys, axes, calibration, saving) | Third-party — skip |
| **ServerMachine.cs** | 61 KB | Machine + networking + encoding + damage + god modes | ServerMachineSync, MachineEncoder, ServerGodMode |
| **LevelEditor.cs** | 61 KB | Entity placement, selection, tools, simulation toggle, undo, events, file I/O | LevelEntityPlacer, LevelToolManager, LevelFileIO |
| **WaterController.cs** | 58 KB | Water physics, rendering, buoyancy zones, wave grid, fog, materials | WaterPhysics, WaterRenderer, WaterWaveGrid |
| **BlockBehaviour.cs** | ~50 KB | Block data, joints, visual state, simulation lifecycle, fire, saving | BlockData, BlockPhysics, BlockSimulation |
| **AddPiece.cs** | ~45 KB | Block placement, ghost blocks, symmetry, rotation, selection | BlockPlacer, GhostBlock, PlacementSymmetry |
| **StatMaster.cs** | ~40 KB | Global state, modes, player tracking, settings, tool management | GameState, ModeController, PlayerTracker |
| **BlockMapper.cs** | ~35 KB | Property UI generation, widget management, event routing | PropertyUIBuilder, WidgetManager |
| **ReferenceMaster.cs** | ~30 KB | 100+ static events for game state | Pure event hub — keep centralized |
| **CustomLevel.cs** | ~30 KB | Entity tracking, logic execution, network sync, variables | LevelEntityManager, LevelLogicRunner |

## Singleton Registry

| Singleton | Pattern | Owns | Read By |
|-----------|---------|------|---------|
| **StatMaster** | `SingleInstance<T>` | Global game state, modes, player refs | Nearly everything |
| **ReferenceMaster** | Static Instance | 100+ static events (central event bus) | Nearly everything |
| **PrefabMaster** | `SingleInstance<T>` | Block prefabs, level prefabs, skin prefabs | AddPiece, LevelEditor, BlockMapper |
| **AddPiece** | `SingleInstanceFindOnly<T>` | Block placement, ghost blocks, selection | Machine, BlockMapper, LevelEditor |
| **InputManager** | `SingleInstance<T>` | Hotkey bindings, input state | KeyInputController, BlockMapper |
| **MusicController** | `SingleInstance<T>` | Audio playback, crossfading, volume | LevelEnvironmentManager, UI |
| **WinCondition** | Static Instance | Objective tracking, win state | VictoryController, AI, levels |
| **CustomLevel** | Static Instance | Entity lists, logic frames, variables | LevelEditor, LevelEntity, network |
| **LevelEditor** | Static Instance | Entity tools, selection, settings | CustomLevel, LevelEntity, UI |
| **BesiegeNetworkManager** | Static Instance | Connection state, message routing | NetworkScene, ServerMachine, all net code |
| **FactionsController** | `SingleInstance<T>` | Faction registry, AI unit arrays | EntityAI, AttackScript |
| **AchievementManager** | `SingleInstance<T>` | Achievement state, triggers | Achievement trigger scripts |
| **DlcManager** | Static Instance | DLC status, validation | Block loading, machine loading, networking |
| **BlockSkinLoader** | `SingleInstance<T>` | Skin files, textures | BlockVisualController |
| **ProjectileManager** | Static Instance | Projectile pools, network sync | CanonBlock, CrossBowBlock, ArcherAI |
| **AdvancedBlockEditor** | Static Instance | Extended block editing UI | BlockMapper, AddPiece |
| **BMWidgetPool** | Static Instance | Mapper widget pooling | BlockMapper |
| **BlockGroundTool** | Static instance | Ground-plane snapping | AddPiece |

---

## Coupling Hotspots

### FindObjectOfType Calls (100+ instances)

Worst offenders:
- `FindObjectOfType<BlockTabController>()` — called from multiple UI scripts
- `FindObjectOfType<TransportNetworkManager>()` — network initialization
- `FindObjectOfType<WaterController>()` — water reference acquisition
- `FindObjectOfType<MachineToolController>()` — tool management
- `FindObjectOfType<OutlineEffect>()` — selection rendering
- `FindObjectOfType<BoundingBoxController>()` — bounds visualization

### Static Instance Access (cross-domain)

- `StatMaster.levelSimulating` — read by 50+ scripts
- `Machine.Active()` — read by AI, camera, victory, UI
- `ReferenceMaster.physicsGoalInstance` — read by entity/AI systems
- `WinCondition.Instance` — read by level entities, AI
- `CustomLevel.Instance` — read by editor, entities, network

### Direct Cross-Domain References

- **AI → Machine**: `Machine.Active()` for target tracking
- **Blocks → Camera**: `MouseOrbit`, `FixedCameraController` references
- **Level → Network**: tight coupling between `LevelEditor` ↔ `NetworkAuxAddPiece`
- **UI → Everything**: `BlockMapper` touches block, machine, input, undo systems
- **Platform → Core**: `SteamManager`, `DlcManager` scattered throughout

---

## Event System

### Primary Pattern: ReferenceMaster (Static Event Hub)

100+ static events covering:

**Configuration Events:**
- `onResolutionChange`, `onFovChange`, `onAudioSettingChange`
- `onLanguageChange`, `onGraphicsSettingChange`

**Game State Events:**
- `onLevelLoad`, `onLevelWin`, `onLevelComplete`
- `onMachineSimulation(Machine, bool)`, `onLevelSimulation(bool)`
- `onLocalMachineSimulation(bool)`

**Machine Events:**
- `onMachineModified(Machine)`, `onMachineChanged(Machine)`
- `onBlockPlaced(BlockBehaviour)`, `onDraggedBlockPlaced(BlockBehaviour)`
- `onPreSimulateMachine`, `ResetEditor`

**UI Events:**
- `hudHiddenChanged`, `Mode.ToolChanged`, `Mode.AeroDisplayChanged`

### Secondary Patterns

- **C# `Action<T>`**: Used on individual components (`Machine.onBatchOperationComplete`, `WinCondition.PreSetup`)
- **Custom delegates**: `CallBack`, `VoidDel`, `LevelSettingsChangedHandler`
- **UnityEvent**: Minimal usage — project prefers C# events
- **`SingleInstance<Events>.Instance`**: Block lifecycle events (`BlockInit`, `MachineSimulate`, `MachineStopSimulate`)

---

## Data Flow

```
[XML/Binary Files] → XmlLoader/MachineInfo.Decode()
    → MachineInfo (name, position, rotation, XData, blocks)
        → Machine.LoadMachineInfo()
            → BlockBehaviour[] (instantiated from PrefabMaster)
                → SaveableDataHolder.LoadState() (MapperType properties)
                    → BlockMapper → UI widgets

[Simulation Start]
    Machine.StartSimulation()
        → Clone all blocks → enable Rigidbody
        → BlockLinkManager.FindLinks() → BlockCluster[]
        → MachineAnalyzer (async topology)
        → KeyInputController (poll input) → bit-packed state
        → TimeSlider (auto-timescale from FPS)
        → Physics engine runs

[AI Runtime]
    EntityAI.Update()
        → TargetBlock = Machine.Active().SimulationBlocks[nearest]
        → SelectState() → Idle/Charge/Flee/Attack
        → AttackScript.Attack() → raycast/trigger → KillingHandler/BlockHealthBar

[Level Logic]
    CustomLevel logic frame
        → GenericEntity.logicData[] → EntityLogic.Execute()
        → Variables dictionary (string→float)
        → WinCondition.CheckObjective()

[Network Sync]
    Server: Machine → ServerMachine.Encode() → byte[]
        → NetworkController.WriteFrame() → compressed diff
        → BesiegeNetworkManager.Send()
    Client: byte[] → ServerMachine.Decode()
        → NetworkInterpolation → smooth transform updates
```

---

## Inheritance Chains

### Worth Preserving

```
MonoBehaviour
├── SingleInstance<T> / SingleInstanceBase<T> / SingleInstanceFindOnly<T>
│   ├── StatMaster
│   ├── PrefabMaster
│   ├── FactionsController
│   ├── AchievementManager
│   └── InputManager
├── SaveableDataHolder
│   ├── BlockBehaviour (base for all blocks)
│   │   ├── BuildSurface
│   │   ├── CanonBlock, FlamethrowerController, etc.
│   │   └── NetworkBlock
│   │       └── LevelEntity
│   └── GenericEntity (base for all entities)
│       ├── AIGenericEntity
│       ├── AIGenericEntityMultiLook
│       ├── BrushTerrainModifierEntity
│       └── (other entity types)
├── Machine
│   └── ServerMachine
├── ClickBehaviour
│   └── IslandController
└── PostEffectsBase
    ├── Bloom, BloomAndLensFlares
    ├── ColorCorrectionCurves/Lut
    ├── DepthOfField34/Scatter
    └── (other post-processing)
```

### Candidates for Flattening

- `EnemyAISimple` vs `EntityAI` — overlapping AI implementations
- `BreakOnForce` variants (7+ subclasses) — could use composition
- `TriggerSetJoint` variants (12+ subclasses) — could use strategy pattern
- `Undo*Action` classes (15+ variants) — could consolidate with generic undo

## Asset Inventory (from .stub)

### Audio (bsge/Assets/AudioClip/)
- ~400 files (ogg, wav)
- Categories: music tracks (8+), ambient loops (20+), combat SFX (50+), building SFX (30+), creature sounds (40+), environmental (30+), UI sounds (20+)
- Notable: Besiege_TitleScreen.ogg, SANDBOX.ogg, Ipsilon_Combat/Main.wav, Tolbrynd.ogg, Valfross_1/2.ogg

### 3D Models (bsge/Assets/Mesh/)
- ~2,000+ files (glb format)
- Categories: blocks, structures (castles, bridges, towers), creatures (knights, animals), vehicles (boats, airships), environmental (rocks, trees, cactus), weapons (cannons, catapults)
- Large combined meshes for level scenes (3-7 MB each, 100+ variants)

### Textures (bsge/Assets/Texture2D/)
- ~1,000+ files (png)
- Categories: diffuse maps, normal maps, UI icons, terrain textures, skybox gradients, effect textures

### Materials (bsge/Assets/Material/)
- Hundreds of material definitions
- Categories: block materials (wood, metal, stone), environment, water, effects, UI

### Shaders (bsge/Assets/Shader/)
- ~200+ compiled shader bytecode files
- Custom block shaders, water, fog, post-processing, UI

### Prefabs (bsge/Assets/PrefabHierarchyObject/)
- ~500+ prefab hierarchies (glb)
- Complete game objects with component data

### Scenes
- Campaign levels (Ipsilon, Tolbrynd, Valfross, Krolmar regions)
- Sandbox level
- Level editor
- Title screen / menus
- Multiplayer scenes

### Cubemaps (bsge/Assets/Cubemap/)
- ~40 cubemaps for reflections and skyboxes
- Desert, forest, fog, ocean, studio variants

### Fonts (bsge/Assets/Font/)
- 20+ font files (ttf, otf)
- Including Chinese/Cyrillic character sets
- Custom "Besiege Font" family

# Estimate — Besiege (bsge)

## Estimation Method

**Formula:** `Hours = FileCount × ComplexityTier × BaseHoursPerFile`

| Complexity Tier | Multiplier | Description |
|-----------------|-----------|-------------|
| Tier 1 (Simple) | 0.5h | Small files, enums, data containers, one-liners |
| Tier 2 (Moderate) | 1.0h | Standard MonoBehaviours, clear single responsibility |
| Tier 3 (Complex) | 2.0h | Multi-responsibility, event-heavy, 200-500 lines |
| Tier 4 (God Object) | 4.0h | >500 lines, 3+ responsibilities, deep coupling |
| Tier 5 (Extreme) | 8.0h | >1000 lines, network+physics+state, must split |

<!-- ==== FILE: LEARN/bsge/GOAL.md ==== -->
# GOAL — Besiege (bsge)

## Project Identity

- **Project Name:** Besiege
- **Engine:** Unity 5.x (C#, IL2CPP compatible)
- **Genre:** Physics-based building & destruction sandbox
- **Phases:** 14 (Core → Data → Block → Machine → Input → Mechanics → Physics → AI → Level → UI → Network → Modding → Platform → Audio)

---

## Target Architecture Rules

### 1. Folder Structure

```
bsge-reimpl/
├── _-CoreSingleton/        # SingleInstance<T> infrastructure
├── _-GameState/            # StatMaster, ReferenceMaster, *LORD
├── _-Config/               # BesiegeConfig, StaticSettings
├── _-PropertySystem/       # MapperType hierarchy (MKey, MSlider, etc.)
├── _-DataContainer/        # XDataHolder, typed wrappers
├── _-Serialization/        # XmlLoader, XmlSaver, MachineInfo
├── _-BlockSystem/          # BlockBehaviour, BlockType, BlockPrefab
├── _-BlockTopology/        # BlockLink, BlockCluster, BlockLinkManager
├── _-BlockVisual/          # BlockVisualController variants
├── _-JointSystem/          # GenericJointSystem, ConfigurableJoint extensions
├── _-MachineSystem/        # Machine, MachineAnalyzer, MachineDamageController
├── _-BuildTools/           # AddPiece, NodeController, transform tools
├── _-UndoSystem/           # UndoSystem, UndoAction variants
├── _-BlockMapper/          # BlockMapper, widget pool, property UI
├── _-InputSystem/          # InputManager, KeyInputController, key mapping
├── _-CameraSystem/         # MouseOrbit, CinematicCam, POVCam, etc.
├── _-WeaponBlocks/         # CanonBlock, CrossBow, Flamethrower, etc.
├── _-MotionBlocks/         # SteeringWheel, PropellorController, wheels
├── _-StructuralBlocks/     # BuildSurface, BraceCode, SpringCode
├── _-UtilityBlocks/        # GrabberBlock, SensorBlock, LogicGate
├── _-NavalBlocks/          # SailBlock, BuoyancyController, ballast
├── _-AerialBlocks/         # BalloonController, HotAirBalloon
├── _-DisplayBlocks/        # Altimeter, Anglometer, Speedometer
├── _-FireSystem/           # FireController, FireProperty, FireTrigger
├── _-ExplosionSystem/      # ExplosionEffect variants
├── _-WaterSystem/          # WaterController, buoyancy zones, waves
├── _-BreakingSystem/       # BreakOnForce variants, fracture
├── _-ParticleSystem/       # ParticleOnCollide, global particles
├── _-AICore/               # EntityAI, AttackScript, KillingHandler
├── _-AIFaction/            # Faction, FactionsController
├── _-AISpecialized/        # ArcherAI, turrets, siege
├── _-AIVehicle/            # FreighterAI, AirshipAI, ship AI
├── _-AICreature/           # BirdAI, FishAI, WhaleController
├── _-LevelEditor/          # LevelEditor, ghost, undo
├── _-LevelEntity/          # LevelEntity, LevelPrefab, controller
├── _-LevelLogic/           # GenericEntity, EntityLogic, triggers
├── _-LevelCore/            # CustomLevel, WinCondition, environments
├── _-Campaign/             # LevelSelect, islands, regions
├── _-EntityTools/          # Selection, transform, scale tools
├── _-UICore/               # UIManager, canvas input, screen switching
├── _-MenuSystem/           # Home menu, block menu, options
├── _-FileBrowser/          # File browsers (machine, level, skin)
├── _-TutorialSystem/       # Tutorial framework
├── _-InfoDisplay/          # Tooltips, console, info popups
├── _-NetworkCore/          # BesiegeNetworkManager, NetworkController
├── _-NetworkMachine/       # ServerMachine, NetworkBlock
├── _-NetworkSession/       # PlayerData, lobby, multiverse
├── _-ServerManagement/     # ServerConfig, hosting
├── _-NetworkSync/          # ProjectileManager, frame sync
├── _-ModAPI/               # ModEntryPoint, Mods, ModResources
├── _-ModContent/           # Internal modding, registration
├── _-ModWorkshop/          # Mod.io integration
├── _-DLCSystem/            # DlcManager, providers
├── _-SteamIntegration/     # SteamManager, workshop, achievements
├── _-AchievementSystem/    # AchievementManager, triggers
├── _-WorkshopSystem/       # WorkshopManager, platform-specific
├── _-AudioSystem/          # MusicController, sound effects
├── _-PostProcessing/       # Bloom, DOF, color correction, etc.
├── _-FogSystem/            # Global/dynamic/volumetric fog
├── _-WeatherEffects/       # Clouds, lightning, rain, wind
├── DataServices/           # Pure C# logic services (no MonoBehaviour)
├── Interfaces/             # Cross-system interfaces
├── SO/                     # ScriptableObject definitions
└── Enums/                  # Shared enums
```

### 2. Naming Conventions

| Prefix | Type | Example |
|--------|------|---------|
| `SO_` | ScriptableObject asset | `SO_BlockPrefab`, `SO_GameConfig` |
| `Field_` | Serialized data field | `Field_GameMode`, `Field_Health` |
| `W_` | Runtime wrapper | `W_MachineInfo`, `W_Faction` |
| `DS_` | DataService (pure C#) | `DS_MachineSerializer`, `DS_BallisticsCalculator` |
| `I` | Interface | `IBlock`, `IMachine`, `ITarget` |
| `_-` | System folder | `_-MachineSystem/`, `_-AICore/` |

### 3. Class Responsibilities

**MonoBehaviour classes:**
- Unity lifecycle only (Awake, Start, Update, OnDestroy)
- Delegate logic to DataServices
- Wire events in Start/OnEnable, unwire in OnDisable/OnDestroy
- No business logic in Update — call DataService methods

**DataService classes:**
- Pure C# (no MonoBehaviour inheritance)
- Stateless where possible, or explicitly manage state
- Testable without Unity runtime
- Injected via constructor or singleton registry

**ScriptableObject assets:**
- Configuration data only
- No runtime state
- Shared across instances via asset references

### 4. Decoupling Patterns

**Current Problem → Target Solution:**

| Current Pattern | Count | Target Pattern |
|-----------------|-------|---------------|
| `FindObjectOfType<T>()` | 100+ | Interface injection via singleton registry |
| `StatMaster.levelSimulating` (static read) | 50+ | `IGameState.IsSimulating` interface |
| `Machine.Active()` (static) | 30+ | `IMachineProvider.ActiveMachine` interface |
| `ReferenceMaster.onX` (static events) | 100+ | Keep centralized event bus (acceptable pattern) |
| `SingleInstance<T>.Instance` | 100+ | Keep singleton but add interface layer |
| Direct class references | 500+ | Interface-based communication for cross-system |

**Acceptable static access (keep as-is):**
- `ReferenceMaster` events — centralized event bus is a valid architecture
- `StatMaster` read-only state queries — game state is globally relevant
- `PrefabMaster` prefab lookups — asset registry is globally relevant

**Must decouple:**
- `FindObjectOfType` calls — replace with cached references or injection
- Cross-domain direct references (AI → Machine, Level → Network)
- God objects (>500 lines) — split into focused components + DataServices

### 5. Lifecycle Rules

**Build Mode → Simulation Mode Transition (critical path):**

```
1. Machine.StartSimulation()
2. Clone all BlockBehaviours (simulation copies)
3. Enable Rigidbody on clones
4. BlockLinkManager.FindLinks() → compute topology
5. MachineAnalyzer.Analyze() → async cluster analysis
6. KeyInputController.StartListening()
7. TimeSlider.Begin()
8. [Simulation runs]
9. Machine.EndSimulation()
10. Destroy simulation clones
11. Restore build mode state
```

**Entity Lifecycle (Level Editor):**
```
1. LevelEditor.AddEntity() → instantiate from LevelPrefab
2. GenericEntity.Init() → setup MapperType properties
3. LevelEntity.SetIdentifier() → assign unique ID
4. [Edit mode: move, rotate, scale, modify properties]
5. LevelEditor.ToggleSimulation(true) → clone for physics
6. EntityLogic.Execute() → run logic per frame
7. WinCondition.CheckObjective() → track victory
8. LevelEditor.ToggleSimulation(false) → restore
```

**Block Lifecycle:**
```
1. AddPiece.PlaceBlock() → instantiate from PrefabMaster
2. BlockBehaviour.OnPlaced() → initialize joints, visuals
3. SaveableDataHolder.SaveInitialData() → snapshot state
4. [Edit: BlockMapper shows properties, user modifies]
5. Machine.StartSimulation() → clone to simulation
6. BlockBehaviour.SimulateStart() → enable physics
7. [Simulation: physics, fire, damage]
8. Machine.EndSimulation() → destroy clone
```

### 6. C# Feature Guidelines

**Use:**
- `readonly` for fields set once
- `sealed` on classes not intended for inheritance
- Pattern matching for type checks
- String interpolation over concatenation
- `using` declarations for IDisposable
- Nullable reference types where supported
- `Dictionary<K,V>` over `Hashtable`
- `List<T>` over `ArrayList`

**Avoid:**
- `public` fields on MonoBehaviours (use `[SerializeField] private`)
- `FindObjectOfType` at runtime (cache in Awake/Start)
- Allocation in Update/FixedUpdate (pool objects)
- String concatenation in hot paths (use StringBuilder)
- `foreach` on non-generic collections in tight loops

**Existing patterns to preserve:**
- `SingleInstance<T>` singleton hierarchy — well-established
- `MapperType` property system — drives modding API
- `XDataHolder` serialization — machine format compatibility
- `ReferenceMaster` event bus — 100+ subscribers depend on it
- `SaveableDataHolder` base class — block/entity data persistence

### 7. Project-Specific Elements

**Block Types (90 variants):**
- Basic: wood, metal, panels, poles
- Mechanical: wheels, hinges, pistons, sliders, springs, cogs
- Weapons: cannons, bombs, rockets, flamethrowers, harpoons, crossbows
- Special: magnets, sensors, cameras, logic gates, build nodes, surfaces
- DLC: flying, scaling, steering, decoupler, metal ball, sails, buoyancy

**Factions (FactionEnum):**
- Ipsilon, Tolbrynd, Viking, PlayerUnit, Animal, Peasant, None, Krolmar, Seafarer

**Environments (LevelEnvironment):**
- Barren, Desert, Water, MountainTop, and more

**DLC Feature Flags:**
- Water mechanics (SailBlock, BuoyancyController, WaterController)
- Surface building (BuildSurface, BuildNodeBlock, BuildEdgeBlock)
- Additional blocks gated by `DlcManager.DlcType`

**Platform Targets:**
- Steam (primary)
- Xbox (XGamingRuntime)
- WeGame (Rail API)
- PlayFab cloud backend

### 8. Testing Strategy

**Unit Testable (DataServices):**
- `DS_MachineSerializer` — round-trip XML serialization
- `DS_BlockGraphService` — graph topology correctness
- `DS_BallisticsCalculator` — trajectory prediction
- `DS_DamageResolver` — damage type application
- `DS_MoraleCalculator` — faction loss computation
- `DS_NetworkCompressor` — compression correctness
- `DS_FireSpreadCalculator` — spread rules
- `DS_WaveSimulation` — wave grid math
- `DS_SurfaceMeshBuilder` — mesh generation

**Integration Testable (MonoBehaviour):**
- Machine build → simulate → end cycle
- Block placement → joint creation → topology
- Entity placement → logic execution → win condition
- Network encode → transmit → decode → interpolate

**Manual Test Scenarios:**
- Build machine with all block types, simulate
- Fire spread across connected wooden blocks
- AI faction battle (multiple teams)
- Water buoyancy with sails and rudder
- Level editor: create, test, save, reload
- Multiplayer: host, join, sync, chat, vote
- Mod loading: custom block appears and functions

### 9. Key Metrics

| Metric | Current | Target |
|--------|---------|--------|
| God objects (>500 lines) | ~15 | 0 (split into DataService + thin MonoBehaviour) |
| FindObjectOfType calls | 100+ | 0 (cached references or interface injection) |
| Public fields on MonoBehaviour | Hundreds | All `[SerializeField] private` |
| Untested business logic | ~100% | DataServices: 80%+ unit test coverage |
| Cross-domain direct references | Hundreds | Interface-only cross-system communication |
| Singleton pattern variants | 3 different | 1 unified pattern |

# PhaseMap — Besiege (bsge)

## Overview

| Total Game Code Files | ~2,456 |
|----------------------|--------|
| Total Phases | 14 |
| Estimated Total Weight | 100% |

> **Rule**: Each phase depends only on earlier phases, never forward.  
> **Third-party code** (iTween, VolumetricFog, cakeslice, SRF, SDKs) is excluded from phases — treated as external dependencies.

## Cross-Phase Modification Table

| Phase Modified | By Phase | Files Affected | Reason |
|---------------|----------|---------------|--------|
| Phase 3 (Block) | Phase 6 (Mechanics) | BlockBehaviour.cs | Each block type extends BlockBehaviour |
| Phase 3 (Block) | Phase 7 (Physics) | BlockHealthBar.cs | Fire/explosion damage hooks |
| Phase 4 (Machine) | Phase 11 (Network) | Machine.cs → ServerMachine.cs | Network subclass |
| Phase 4 (Machine) | Phase 8 (AI) | Machine.Active() | AI reads active machine for targeting |
| Phase 7 (Physics) | Phase 8 (AI) | FireController.cs | AI reacts to fire |
| Phase 8 (AI) | Phase 9 (Level) | AIGenericEntity.cs | Level editor exposes AI properties |
| Phase 9 (Level) | Phase 11 (Network) | LevelEntity.cs → NetworkBlock | Level entities are networked |
| Phase 1 (Core) | Phase 13 (Platform) | StatMaster.cs | Platform-specific state flags |
| Phase 4 (Machine) | Phase 12 (Modding) | BlockBehaviour.cs | Modding hooks into block lifecycle |
| Phase 9 (Level) | Phase 12 (Modding) | LevelPrefab.cs | Modded entity types |

<!-- ==== FILE: LEARN/bsge/StructureMap.md ==== -->
# StructureMap — Besiege (bsge)

## Overview

For each phase, this document specifies:
- Which scripts become `_-Systems/` folders (3+ tightly coupled files)
- DataService candidates (pure C# logic extractable from MonoBehaviours)
- Interface candidates (cross-system communication points)
- SO_ / Field_ / W prefix assignments

---

## Phase 1 — Core Framework

### Systems

**_-CoreSingleton/**
- `SingleInstance<T>`, `SingleInstanceBase<T>`, `SingleInstanceFindOnly<T>`
- Pure infrastructure — no domain logic

**_-GameState/**
- `StatMaster` → `Field_GameMode`, `Field_SimulationState`, `Field_ActivePlayer`
- `ReferenceMaster` → pure event hub (keep centralized)
- `STATLORD`, `SCREENLORD`, `LEVELLORD` → statistics/screen/level state

**_-Config/**
- `BesiegeConfig` → `SO_GameConfig` (audio, graphics, gameplay, network settings)
- `BesiegeConfigController` → config load/save
- `StaticSettings` → `SO_PathConfig` (file paths, constants)

### DataService Candidates

| Current | Proposed DataService | Why |
|---------|---------------------|-----|
| `BesiegeConfig` (MonoBehaviour) | `DS_ConfigService` | Pure data read/write — no Unity lifecycle needed |
| `StaticSettings` (static) | `DS_PathService` | Pure path computation — no MonoBehaviour |
| `CLZF2` (static) | `DS_CompressionService` | Pure data compression |
| `Arguments` (static) | `DS_ArgumentParser` | Pure CLI parsing |

### Interface Candidates

| Interface | Purpose | Implementors |
|-----------|---------|-------------|
| `IGameState` | Global state queries | `StatMaster` |
| `IEventBus` | Event pub/sub | `ReferenceMaster` |
| `IConfigProvider` | Settings access | `BesiegeConfig` |

### Prefix Assignments

| Prefix | Items |
|--------|-------|
| `SO_` | `SO_GameConfig`, `SO_PathConfig` |
| `Field_` | `Field_GameMode`, `Field_SimulationState`, `Field_ActivePlayer`, `Field_IsMultiplayer` |
| `W_` | (none — no wrappers at this level) |

---

## Phase 2 — Data & Serialization

### Systems

**_-PropertySystem/**
- `MapperType`, `MKey`, `MSlider`, `MToggle`, `MValue`, `MLimits`, `MLogic`, `MMenu`, `MText`, `MTeam`, `MVisual`, `MColourSlider`
- `SaveableDataHolder` → base class using MapperType

**_-DataContainer/**
- `XDataHolder`, `XData`, `XBoolean`, `XColor`, `XInteger`, `XIntegerArray`, `XSingle`, `XSingleArray`, `XString`, `XStringArray`, `XVector3`, `XDataUtil`

**_-Serialization/**
- `XmlLoader`, `XmlSaver`, `MachineInfo`, `MachineFormatConverter`
- `XMLTypes/` folder contents

### DataService Candidates

| Current | Proposed DataService | Why |
|---------|---------------------|-----|
| `XmlLoader` (static methods) | `DS_MachineSerializer` | Pure XML parsing — no Unity dependency |
| `XmlSaver` (static methods) | `DS_MachineSerializer` | Pure XML generation |
| `MachineInfo.Encode/Decode` | `DS_MachineEncoder` | Pure binary encoding |
| `MachineFormatConverter` | `DS_FormatConverter` | Pure version conversion |

### Interface Candidates

| Interface | Purpose | Implementors |
|-----------|---------|-------------|
| `ISerializable` | Save/load state | `SaveableDataHolder` |
| `IPropertyContainer` | MapperType collection | Block/entity implementations |

### Prefix Assignments

| Prefix | Items |
|--------|-------|
| `SO_` | (none — data containers are runtime) |
| `Field_` | All MapperType subclasses effectively act as fields |
| `W_` | `W_MachineData` (wraps MachineInfo for runtime) |

---

## Phase 3 — Block Foundation

### Systems

**_-BlockSystem/**
- `BlockBehaviour`, `BlockType`, `BlockInfo`, `MyBlockInfo`, `BlockPrefab`, `BlockPrefabContainer`
- `BlockTrigger`, `BlockDamageType`, `DamageType`

**_-BlockTopology/**
- `BlockJoint`, `BlockLink`, `BlockLinkManager`, `BlockCluster`, `BlockNode`
- Tightly coupled graph system — keep together

**_-BlockVisual/**
- `BlockVisualController`, `BlockVisualControllerExtended`, `BlockSkinnedVisualController`
- `BlockEventVisualController`, `FragmentVisualController`
- `BlockHealthBar`

**_-JointSystem/**
- `GenericJointSystem`, `BlockJoint`
- `ConfigurableJointExtensions`, `ConfigurableJointTargetAngle`
- `HingeJointFix`, `SolidHingeJoints`

### DataService Candidates

| Current | Proposed DataService | Why |
|---------|---------------------|-----|
| `BlockLinkManager` (graph logic) | `DS_BlockGraphService` | Graph topology is pure data — no rendering |
| `BlockCluster` (grouping) | `DS_ClusterService` | Connected component detection is pure algorithm |
| `GenericJointSystem` (creation) | `DS_JointFactory` | Joint creation rules are pure logic |

### Interface Candidates

| Interface | Purpose | Implementors |
|-----------|---------|-------------|
| `IBlock` | Block behavior contract | `BlockBehaviour` and all block types |
| `IBlockVisual` | Visual update contract | `BlockVisualController` variants |
| `IDamageable` | Damage reception | `BlockHealthBar`, `KillingHandler` |
| `IJointTarget` | Joint connection point | `BlockBehaviour` |

### Prefix Assignments

| Prefix | Items |
|--------|-------|
| `SO_` | `SO_BlockPrefab` (block template data) |
| `Field_` | `Field_BlockType`, `Field_Health`, `Field_Stress` |
| `W_` | `W_BlockState` (wraps runtime block state) |

---

## Phase 4 — Machine Core

### Systems

**_-MachineSystem/**
- `Machine`, `MachineAnalyzer`, `MachineDamageController`
- `MachineCenterOfMass`, `MachineHeight`, `MachineRotation`, `MachineGround`
- `MachineObjectTracker`, `MachineInfo` (runtime reference)

**_-BuildTools/**
- `AddPiece`, `MachineToolController`, `MachineTransformTool`, `MachineTranslateTool`
- `NodeController`, `NodeBuildingGridController`, `NodeBuildingGridBehaviour`

**_-UndoSystem/**
- `UndoSystem`, `UndoAction`, all `UndoAction*` variants (15+ files)
- `MultiUndoAction`

**_-BlockMapper/**
- `BlockMapper`, `BlockMapperInternal/` (7 widget files)
- `BMWidgetPool`, `OverviewBlockMapper`

### DataService Candidates

| Current | Proposed DataService | Why |
|---------|---------------------|-----|
| `MachineAnalyzer` (async analysis) | `DS_TopologyAnalyzer` | Graph analysis is pure algorithm |
| `Machine.FindLinks()` | `DS_LinkFinder` | Link computation is data-only |
| `MachineDamageController` | `DS_DamageCalculator` | Damage math is pure logic |
| `UndoSystem` (command pattern) | `DS_UndoHistory` | Undo stack is pure data structure |

### Interface Candidates

| Interface | Purpose | Implementors |
|-----------|---------|-------------|
| `IMachine` | Machine queries | `Machine`, `ServerMachine` |
| `IBuildTool` | Tool contract | Translate, Rotate, Scale, Mirror tools |
| `IUndoAction` | Undo command | All `UndoAction*` variants |
| `IAnalysisTarget` | Topology target | `Machine` |

### Prefix Assignments

| Prefix | Items |
|--------|-------|
| `SO_` | `SO_MachineConfig` (default settings) |
| `Field_` | `Field_MachineState`, `Field_BlockCount`, `Field_CenterOfMass` |
| `W_` | `W_MachineInfo` (wraps MachineInfo for runtime) |

---

## Phase 5 — Input & Camera

### Systems

**_-InputSystem/**
- `InputManager`, `KeyInputController`, `cInput`
- `KeyMapController`, `KeyMapButton`, `KeyMapModeButton`, `KeyMapIndividualButton`, `KeyMapTool`, `KeyMapMe`

- `CameraShake`, `CameraShaker`

### DataService Candidates

| Current | Proposed DataService | Why |
|---------|---------------------|-----|
| `KeyInputController` (bit-packing) | `DS_InputEncoder` | Bit-packed state is pure data |
| `GlobalDefaultKeyMaps` | `DS_DefaultBindings` | Pure data table |

### Interface Candidates

| Interface | Purpose | Implementors |
|-----------|---------|-------------|
| `ICameraMode` | Camera behavior | Orbit, Cinematic, POV, ThirdPerson |
| `IInputProvider` | Input source | `KeyInputController`, `NetKeyInputController` |

### Prefix Assignments

| Prefix | Items |
|--------|-------|
| `SO_` | `SO_InputBindings`, `SO_CameraConfig` |
| `Field_` | `Field_KeyState`, `Field_CameraPosition` |
| `W_` | (none) |

- `AltimeterBlock`, `AnglometerBlock`, `SpeedometerBlock`, `ColorLevelBlock`

### DataService Candidates

| Current | Proposed DataService | Why |
|---------|---------------------|-----|

| `BuildSurface` aerodynamics | `DS_AerodynamicsCalculator` | Drag computation is pure physics |
| `CanonBlock` trajectory | `DS_BallisticsCalculator` | Ballistic prediction is math |
| `SailBlock` wind | `DS_WindCalculator` | Wind force computation |

### Interface Candidates

| Interface | Purpose | Implementors |
|-----------|---------|-------------|
| `IWeaponBlock` | Firing contract | Canon, Crossbow, Flamethrower, Harpoon |
| `IMotorBlock` | Rotation control | Steering, Cog, Propellor, Wheel |
| `ISurfaceBlock` | Surface behavior | BuildSurface, BuildNode, BuildEdge |
| `INavalBlock` | Water interaction | Sail, Buoyancy, Ballast, Rudder |

### Prefix Assignments

| Prefix | Items |
|--------|-------|
| `SO_` | `SO_ProjectileConfig`, `SO_SurfaceMaterial`, `SO_WindConfig` |
| `Field_` | `Field_Ammo`, `Field_Force`, `Field_Fuel`, `Field_Speed` |
| `W_` | `W_ProjectileState`, `W_SurfaceState` |

## Phase 7 — Physics & Effects

### Systems

**_-FireSystem/**
- `FireController`, `FireProperty`, `FireTag`, `FireTrigger`
- `SimpleFireTrigger`, `ForgeEnableFire`

**_-ExplosionSystem/**
- `ExplosionEffect`, `ExplosionEffectAdv`, `SmallExplosion`
- `ShockwaveExplosion`, `BarrierExplosion`, `CannonBallExplosion`
- `BaloonExplosion`, `ExplosionListener`, `ExplosionMat`

**_-WaterSystem/**
- `WaterController`, `WaterBuoyancyZone`, `WaterZone`, `WaterZoneEntity`
- `WaterFogController`, `WaterFollowCam`, `WaterLod`
- `WaterSplashSimple`, `WaterSplashSimple1`, `WaterCausticsCamera`
- `WaveGridMover`, `WaveGridSplashSpawner`, `WaveSplashDetector`
