<!-- ==== FILE: LEARN/bsge/SystemPortabilityMap.md ==== -->
# SystemPortabilityMap — Besiege (bsge)

## Classification

- **L0** — Fully portable: Pure C# logic, no Unity dependencies, no external service calls. Can be extracted as standalone library.
- **L1** — Mostly portable: Uses Unity types (Vector3, Quaternion, Color) but no MonoBehaviour lifecycle. Needs thin Unity adapter.
- **L1+** — Partially portable: Uses MonoBehaviour but logic can be separated. Requires refactoring to extract DataService.
- **L2** — Unity-bound: Deep MonoBehaviour/Component dependency. Must remain in Unity project.

---

## Phase 1 — Core Framework

| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| SingleInstance infrastructure | L2 | MonoBehaviour-based, Unity lifecycle |
| StatMaster | L2 | MonoBehaviour singleton, deeply tied to Unity |
| ReferenceMaster | L1+ | Static events could be plain C# delegates; MonoBehaviour only for lifetime |
| STATLORD / SCREENLORD / LEVELLORD | L2 | MonoBehaviour with Unity scene access |
| StaticSettings | L0 | Pure static paths and constants |
| BesiegeConfig | L1 | Serializable data — needs file I/O adapter |
| CLZF2 compression | L0 | Pure C# compression algorithm |
| Arguments parser | L0 | Pure string parsing |
| Math utilities (MathUtil, Mathfx) | L1 | Uses Vector3/Quaternion but pure math |
| Extension methods | L0 | Pure C# |

## Phase 2 — Data & Serialization

| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| XDataHolder / XData / typed wrappers | L0 | Pure C# key-value store |
| MapperType hierarchy | L1 | Uses Unity types (Color, Vector3) but logic is pure |
| SaveableDataHolder | L1+ | MonoBehaviour base but save/load is pure data |
| XmlLoader | L0 | Pure XML parsing (System.Xml) |
| XmlSaver | L0 | Pure XML generation |
| MachineInfo encode/decode | L0 | Pure binary serialization |
| MachineFormatConverter | L0 | Pure version conversion logic |

## Phase 3 — Block Foundation

| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| BlockBehaviour | L2 | MonoBehaviour, joints, colliders, Unity lifecycle |
| BlockType enum | L0 | Pure enum |
| BlockLink / BlockLinkManager | L1 | Graph logic uses Unity joint references but algorithm is portable |
| BlockCluster | L0 | Pure connected-component algorithm |
| BlockJoint | L2 | Wraps Unity ConfigurableJoint/HingeJoint |
| GenericJointSystem | L2 | Creates Unity joints directly |
| BlockVisualController | L2 | Renderer, Material, Mesh — pure Unity |
| BlockHealthBar | L2 | Unity UI components |

## Phase 4 — Machine Core

| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| Machine | L2 | MonoBehaviour, manages Unity GameObjects/physics |
| MachineAnalyzer (topology) | L1 | Algorithm is portable; wraps Unity block references |
| MachineDamageController | L1+ | Damage math is pure; needs Unity block references |
| UndoSystem | L1 | Command pattern is pure; actions reference Unity objects |
| AddPiece | L2 | Instantiation, raycasting, ghost rendering — Unity-bound |
| BlockMapper | L2 | Unity UI generation |
| NodeController | L2 | Unity grid rendering |

## Phase 5 — Input & Camera

| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| InputManager | L2 | Unity Input system |
| KeyInputController (bit-packing) | L0 | Pure bit-pack encoding |
| cInput | L2 | Unity Input wrapper |
| MouseOrbit | L2 | Unity Camera/Transform |
| CinematicCam | L2 | Unity Camera paths |
| CameraShake | L2 | Unity Transform manipulation |

## Phase 6 — Block Mechanics

| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| All block implementations | L2 | MonoBehaviour with physics/rendering |
| Ballistics calculation | L1 | Pure math (trajectory prediction) |
| Aerodynamics calculation | L1 | Pure physics math (drag/lift) |
| Surface mesh generation | L1 | Geometry math; outputs Unity Mesh |
| Wind calculation | L1 | Pure force math |

## Phase 7 — Physics & Effects

| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| FireController | L2 | Unity colliders, particles, renderer |
| Fire spread logic | L1 | Rule-based spread could be pure algorithm |
| ExplosionEffect variants | L2 | Unity physics forces, particles |
| WaterController | L2 | Mesh generation, shaders, physics |
| Wave simulation math | L1 | Pure grid-based wave math |
| BreakOnForce variants | L2 | Unity joint/force detection |
| Structural integrity check | L0 | Pure force threshold comparison |
| TimeSlider | L1+ | FPS averaging is pure; timescale is Unity |

## Phase 8 — AI System

| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| EntityAI | L2 | MonoBehaviour, physics, raycasting |
| AI state evaluation logic | L1 | Decision tree is pure algorithm |
| Target selection | L1 | Distance/priority scoring is pure math |
| Morale calculation | L0 | Pure math (loss ratios) |
| AttackScript | L2 | Raycasting, collision, particles |
| Damage resolution | L0 | Pure damage type multiplication |
| Ballistic prediction (ArcherAI) | L1 | Pure physics math |
| Faction data | L0 | Pure data class |
| FactionsController | L1+ | Registry is pure; uses Unity for array management |
| KillingHandler | L2 | Materials, particles, ragdoll — Unity-bound |

## Phase 9 — Level System

| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| LevelEditor | L2 | Unity scene manipulation |
| LevelEntity | L2 | NetworkBlock → MonoBehaviour |
| GenericEntity | L2 | SaveableDataHolder → MonoBehaviour |
| CustomLevel | L2 | Unity scene management |
| LevelXMLLoader | L0 | Pure XML parsing |
| LevelXMLSaver | L0 | Pure XML generation |
| WinCondition (logic) | L1 | Objective counting is pure; display is Unity |
| LevelSettings | L0 | Pure data container |
| EntityLogic | L1+ | Logic execution could be pure; reads Unity state |

## Phase 10 — UI System

| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| All UI components | L2 | Unity Canvas/UI — inherently Unity-bound |
| Pagination logic | L0 | Pure math |
| Search filtering | L0 | Pure string matching |

## Phase 11 — Networking

| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| BesiegeNetworkManager | L2 | Wraps Unity networking |
| NetworkController frame compression | L0 | Pure byte-level encoding |
| NetworkCompression | L0 | Pure data compression |
| ServerMachine encode/decode | L0 | Pure binary serialization |
| FloatPacker | L0 | Pure float→byte conversion |
| NetworkInterpolation | L1 | Pure math interpolation; uses Unity types |
| ProjectileManager | L2 | Unity object pooling |
| NetworkScene | L2 | Unity scene + platform SDKs |

## Phase 12 — Modding API

| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| ModEntryPoint | L2 | MonoBehaviour lifecycle hooks |
| ModResources | L2 | Unity asset loading |
| ModSettings | L1 | File I/O with serialization |
| ModNetworking | L2 | Network layer dependent |
| Mods registry | L1 | Pure dictionary; needs Unity for loading |

## Phase 13 — Platform & DLC

| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| DLC validation logic | L0 | Pure enum checking |
| Achievement condition checks | L0 | Pure boolean evaluation |
| SteamManager | L2 | Platform SDK binding |
| Workshop managers | L2 | Platform SDK binding |
| AchievementManager | L2 | Platform SDK binding |

## Phase 14 — Audio & Visual Polish

| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| MusicController | L2 | Unity AudioSource |
| Crossfade math | L0 | Pure interpolation |
| Post-processing effects | L2 | Unity shader/rendering pipeline |
| Fog systems | L2 | Unity shader/rendering |

---

## Summary

| Level | Count | Description |
|-------|-------|-------------|
| **L0** | ~35 | Pure C# — directly extractable |
| **L1** | ~25 | Needs thin Unity type adapter |
| **L1+** | ~15 | Requires DataService extraction |
| **L2** | ~100+ | Unity-bound — stays in project |

### Highest-Value L0 Extractions

1. `DS_MachineSerializer` — XML save/load (XmlLoader + XmlSaver)
2. `DS_MachineEncoder` — Binary encode/decode (MachineInfo)
3. `DS_BlockGraphService` — Topology analysis (BlockCluster + link finding)
4. `DS_NetworkCompressor` — Frame compression (NetworkCompression + FloatPacker)
5. `DS_MoraleCalculator` — Faction loss math
6. `DS_DamageResolver` — Damage type multiplication
7. `DS_BallisticPredictor` — Trajectory math
8. `DS_CompressionService` — LZF compression (CLZF2)
9. `DS_InputEncoder` — Bit-packed key state
10. `DS_StructuralIntegrity` — Force threshold checks

<!-- ==== FILE: LEARN/bsge/surfer.md ==== -->
# surfer — Besiege (bsge)

## Prompt 1: Initial source analysis

**Date:** 2025-05-16

**Action:** Full project initialization and source analysis for Besiege (bsge).

**Source Scope:**
- 25,193 total project files (18.079 GB)
- 2,456 game code files in Assembly-CSharp
- 2,383 third-party SDK files in Assembly-CSharp-firstpass
- 48 compiled DLL assemblies

**Key Findings:**
- Game is Besiege — physics-based building & destruction sandbox
- Unity 5.x engine with IL2CPP support
- Multi-platform: Steam, Xbox (XGamingRuntime), WeGame (Rail), PlayFab cloud
- 90 block types, 9 factions, 14 identified phases
- Heavy singleton pattern (3 variants: SingleInstance, SingleInstanceBase, SingleInstanceFindOnly)
- Central event bus: ReferenceMaster with 100+ static events
- 100+ FindObjectOfType calls (coupling hotspot)
- 15 god objects (>500 lines) including Machine.cs (89KB), NetworkAuxAddPiece.cs (112KB), EntityAI.cs (82KB)
- Full modding API (ModEntryPoint, ModResources, ModNetworking)
- Water mechanics as DLC feature

**Documents Generated:**
1. ARCHITECTURE.md — dependency graph, singletons, coupling, events, data flow, inheritance, assets
2. PhaseMap.md — 14 phases with file lists, difficulty ratings, cross-phase modifications
3. StructureMap.md — 60 system folders, 45 DataService candidates, 48 interfaces
4. GOAL.md — target architecture rules, naming, lifecycle, testing strategy
5. Estimate.md — ~820h total (480h core + 340h overhead)
6. SystemPortabilityMap.md — L0/L1/L1+/L2 classification per system
7. surfer.md — this file

<!-- ==== FILE: LEARN/btycoon/ARCHITECTURE.md ==== -->
# ARCHITECTURE — btycoon (Bloody Bar Tycoon)

## Source Overview

| Metric | Value |
|--------|-------|
| **Engine** | Unity 2022.x (URP) |
| **Total .cs files** | 5,517 (includes third-party) |
| **Game code .cs files** | 2,546 (CTS.* assemblies) |
| **Third-party .cs files** | ~2,971 (Animancer, AstarPathfinding, PixelCrushers, EasySave3, Spine, XCharts, etc.) |
| **Total project files (from stub)** | 31,958 |
| **Total project size** | 4.988 GB |
| **Primary assembly** | CTS.BBT (2,134 files) |
| **Framework assembly** | CTS.Core (165 files) |

### Assembly Breakdown (Game Code)

| Assembly | Files | Purpose |
|----------|-------|---------|
| CTS.BBT | 2,134 | Main game logic — AI, machines, construction, quests, UI, finance, all gameplay |
| CTS.Core | 165 | Framework — DI container, pooling, FSM, events, base classes, world selector |
| CTS.UI | 77 | Panel system, canvas management, tooltips, cursor, palette/theming |
| CTS.Utilities | 70 | Time, collections, addressables, animation tracking, conditions |
| CTS.DevConsole | 51 | Developer console with 54 typed commands |
| CTS.TechTree | 13 | Research/technology tree system |
| CTS.ScriptableSettings | 13 | PlayerPrefs-based settings |
| CTS.StockInventory | 9 | Generic stack-based inventory system |
| CTS.Emotes.Runtime | 8 | Emote display system |
| CTS.InputGeneration | 3 | Input asset code generation |
| CTS.Report | 3 | Bug report system |
| Assembly-CSharp | 264 | ES3 save types (auto-generated), glue code, Spine/Dialogue bridges |

### Folder Structure (CTS.BBT)

```
CTS.BBT/
├── (root) ............... 116 files — Construction system, Quest, Steam, Options, Sound
├── CTS/ ................. 1,682 files — All game domain logic
│   ├── AI/ .............. 11 files — Pathfinding, movement, agent registry
│   ├── BBT/ ............. 70 files — Bar core: drinks, furniture, items, spawner, death
│   │   ├── AI/ .......... 152 files — Agent actions, FSMs, chores, autonomous behaviors
│   │   ├── Handlers/ .... 3 files — Financial charge/transaction enums
│   │   ├── TechTree/ .... 1 file
│   │   └── UI/ .......... 3 files
│   ├── DevConsole/ ...... 55 files — Console commands (agent, money, stock, etc.)
│   ├── Emotes/ .......... 3 files — Room-aware emote system
│   ├── Furnitures/ ...... 2 files — FurnitureBounds, FurniturePlacer
│   ├── GridSystem/ ...... 6 files — Furniture placement grid (separate from construction)
│   ├── Rendering/ ....... 4 files — Custom URP depth pass
│   ├── ScriptableSettings/ 3 files
│   ├── TechTree/ ........ 1 file
│   ├── UI/ .............. 3 files
│   └── Utilities/ ....... 5 files
├── Codice/CmdRunner/ .... 7 files — Build/CI tooling
├── NorskaLib/ ........... 4 files — Google Sheets import
└── Properties/ .......... 1 file
```

## Singleton Registry

### CTS.Core Singletons
| Singleton | Owns | Who Reads It |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `UpdateSpreader` | Central update loop + spread-update distribution | All IUpdatable/ISpreadUpdatable objects |
| `WorldSelector` | Raycast selection, multi-select, mode switching | ConstructionSystem, FurniturePlacer, AgentPanelGroup |

### CTS.BBT Singletons (MonoSingleton / CTSSingleton)
| Singleton | Owns | Who Reads It |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `ConstructionSystem` | Build/destroy/paint modes, grid operations | ConstructionGrid, FurniturePlacer, Prestige, UI panels |
| `BuildablePlacementSystem` | Door/window/arch placement | ConstructionSystem, ConstructionCell |
| `BuildingRoomsContainerManager` | Multi-floor room containers | ConstructionSystem, ConstructionGrid, RoomSelection |
| `SurfaceObjectPaintingSystem` | Wall/floor painting | ConstructionSystem, Prestige |
| `FurniturePlacer` | Furniture spawn, pickup, placement | BarFurnitures, FurnitureShop, WorldSelector |
| `BarFurnitures` | Furniture registry + lookup | Customer AI, Worker Chores, Machine actions |
| `AgentsPathfinding` | Async path calculation queue | AgentMovement, AgentAction |
| `AgentsMover` | Agent position/velocity tick | All moving agents |
| `CustomerSpawner` | Customer population control | LevelParameters, CalendarHandlers |
| `NameGeneratorManager` | Gendered name generation | Customer/Worker spawning |
| `InterimAgency` | Worker hiring UI + logic | AgentPanelGroup, WorkerParameters |
| `Prestige` | Prestige level calculations | UI, LevelParameters, FinancialLoaningContract |
| `FinancialLoaningManager` | Loan contracts | FinancialUI, CalendarHandlers |
| `FinancialMoneyStats` | Monthly income/expense tracking | FinancialUI, FinancialGraph |
| `FinancialGraph` | Financial chart data | FinancialMoneyStats, UI |
| `MusicMixManager` | Dynamic music system | BarStyleInfluence, LevelParameters |
| `TechTreeManager` | Research state tracking | TechTreeUI, MachineBase |
| `TechTreePoints` | Research point economy | TechTreeManager, MachineBase |
| `ChoreList` | Global worker chore registry | WorkerChoreAssigner, Machines |
| `ReportInterface` | Bug report UI | Options menu |
| `AgentPanelGroup` | Agent info panel | WorldSelector, Worker/Customer click |

### Static Class Singletons (no Instance)
| Class | Owns | Who Reads It |
|-------|------|-------------|
| `CustomerManager` | Customer lists (vampire/human) | CustomerSpawner, AI actions, Vigilance |
| `CharacterVisualManager` | Character visual data registries | Agent spawning |
| `Agents` | Agent hashset registry | AgentsMover, AI queries |
| `Workers` | Worker hashset registry | ChoreList, InterimAgency |

## Coupling Hotspots

### FindObjectOfType Calls
| File | Call | Risk |
|------|------|------|
| `BarFurnitures.Start()` | `FindObjectsOfType<Furniture>()` | Medium — runs once at start |

### Static Instance Access (MonoSingleton<T> pattern)
Used pervasively (~50+ singletons). Key coupling chains:
- `MonoSingleton<ConstructionSystem>` → accessed by 10+ classes
- `MonoSingleton<BuildablePlacementSystem>` → accessed by ConstructionGrid, ConstructionCell
- `MonoSingleton<AbsMoneyHandlerBridge>` → accessed by every purchase flow
- `MonoSingleton<CursorManager>` → accessed by ConstructionSystem, WorldSelector
- `MonoSingleton<WallSelectionManager>` → accessed by ConstructionGrid, ConstructionSystem

### Direct Cross-Domain References
| From | To | Type |
|------|----|------|
| Machine classes | ChoreList singleton | Create worker chores |
| ConstructionSystem | UI_ConstructionSystem, UI_DestructionMode, UI_PaintPanel | Direct singleton access |
| AgentSoundManager | 25+ action classes | Static event subscriptions |
| Prestige | 8+ systems | Static event subscriptions |
| Quest system | PixelCrushers.DialogueSystem | Deep integration (QuestLog, DialogueLua, ConversationPopup) |

---

## Event System

### Patterns Used
1. **C# `event Action<T>`** — Primary pattern. Both static (system broadcasts) and instance (component-scoped)
2. **CTSEvent / CTSEvent<T>** — CTS.Core wrapper with operator `+=`/`-=` overloads
3. **EventManager** (CTS.Core) — Static keyed event bus using `StringKey` + struct args
4. **PixelCrushers events** — Quest state changes via `QuestLog` callbacks

### Event Count Estimates
- **Static events declared**: ~150+ across all CTS assemblies
- **Instance events declared**: ~200+
- **Key broadcast events**: `CalendarHandlers.NewDay/NewMonth`, `MoneyHandler.MoneyAmountChanged`, `Agent.Died/Spawned/Despawned`, `ConstructionSystem.CellsBought`, `Prestige.PrestigeLevelChanged`

### Event Flow Examples

**Customer Orders a Drink:**
```
Customer.AutonomousActionCallWaiter
  → CustomerActionCallWaiter → creates CustomerOrder
  → GroupOrder.CreatePreparationChores()
  → WorkerChoreDrinkPreparation → added to ChoreList
  → WorkerChoreAssigner picks it up
  → WorkerActionGetDrinkFromPump/Storage
  → WorkerActionPutDrinkOnPlate
  → WorkerChorePlateDelivery
  → CustomerOrder.Status = Delivered
  → Customer.AutonomousActionDrink
  → AgentActionDrink → satisfaction modifiers
  → CustomerOrder.Pay() → MoneyHandler
```

**Machine Processing Victim:**
```
Player triggers ContextualActionSuckBlood/Hypnosis
  → WorkerActionLoadMachine → MachineBase.LoadVictim(Agent)
  → DOTween: LoadIn → Process → ProcessOut
  → MachineBase.VictimHarvested (static event)
  → BloodDistiller/BloodyShaker etc. generates StockItemSO
  → Stocks.BarStock updated → chore for unload
  → WorkerChoreUnloadMachine
  → MachineBase.FinalizeUnload() → ContextualStateDead or release
```

---

## Data Flow

### SO → Runtime → Manager → UI Pipeline

```
ScriptableObjects (data definitions)
    │
    ├── DrinkSO ──────────► Drink (Item, runtime) ──► OrderPlate ──► Table UI
    ├── FurnitureSO ──────► Furniture (runtime) ────► BarFurnitures registry ──► Agent panels
    ├── StockItemSO ──────► StockInventory ─────────► BBTStock ──► Stock UI
    ├── MapInfoSO ────────► MapSelection ───────────► ProfileManager ──► Map UI
    ├── PrestigeLevelsData ► Prestige singleton ────► Prestige UI
    ├── QuestSO ──────────► Quest (runtime) ────────► QuestLog (PixelCrushers) ──► Quest UI
    └── FinancialLoanSO ──► FinancialLoaningContract► FinancialLoaningManager ──► Finance UI
```

### Save/Load (EasySave3)
- ES3 auto-generates `ES3UserType_*` for ~100 classes
- `SaveManager` orchestrates save/load via `ES3File`
- `GameObjectSaver` per-object serialization
- Profile system: `ProfileManager` → `CareerProfile` / `FreemodeProfile`

---

## Inheritance Chains

### Worth Preserving
```
CTSBehaviour → CTSSingleton<T>      (DI lifecycle)
CTSBehaviour → FSM<T> → State<T>   (state machine)
AgentAction → AgentAction<T>        (typed agent binding)
  ├── CustomerAction                (customer-specific)
  ├── WorkerAction                  (worker-specific)
  │   └── WorkerChore               (chore system)
  ├── AgentHubAction                (multi-step orchestration)
  └── SimpleAgentAction             (one-shot)
Agent → Customer                    (sealed)
Agent → Worker                      (sealed)
FurnitureInteractor → MachineBase   (machine hierarchy)
  ├── BloodDistiller
  ├── BloodyArcade
  ├── BloodyExpresso
  ├── BloodyShaker
  ├── BloodySmoker
  ├── BloodyIceCrusher
  ├── BloodyRad
  ├── BloodyTeaBag
  └── BloodyWineBarrel
Quest → SecondaryQuest              (quest types)
Quest → CircumstantialQuest
QuestsManager → SecondaryQuestsManager
QuestsManager → CircumstantialQuestsManager
StockInventory<TStack,TData>        (generic inventory)
```

### Candidates for Flattening
```
ContextualAction<T> hierarchy — 14+ small subclasses could be data-driven
AutonomousAction* SO hierarchy — 13+ score-only SOs could merge patterns
ES3UserType_* — auto-generated, not maintained manually
```

# Estimate — btycoon (Bloody Bar Tycoon)

> Hours per phase based on file count × complexity tier.

## Complexity Tiers

| Tier | Multiplier | Description |
|------|-----------|-------------|
| **T1 — Simple** | 0.3 h/file | Data classes, enums, simple SOs, wrappers |
| **T2 — Standard** | 0.6 h/file | Standard MonoBehaviours, UI panels, handlers |
| **T3 — Complex** | 1.0 h/file | FSMs, action systems, AI, multi-step pipelines |
| **T4 — God Object** | 2.0 h/file | 400+ line files requiring decomposition |

---

## Phase Estimates

| Phase | Name | Files | Tier Mix | Hours | Notes |
|-------|------|-------|----------|-------|-------|
| 1 | Core Framework | 235 | 60% T2, 30% T3, 10% T1 | **162** | DI container is complex but well-structured |
| 2 | UI Framework | 90 | 70% T2, 20% T1, 10% T3 | **47** | Panel system + DOTween effects |
| 3 | Inventory & Stock | 25 | 50% T2, 30% T3, 20% T1 | **14** | Generic inventory is elegant |
| 4 | Construction & Rooms | 160 | 30% T3, 30% T4, 30% T2, 10% T1 | **152** | ConstructionGrid (1489L) + Cell (863L) are major |
| 5 | Furniture & Items | 90 | 50% T2, 30% T3, 20% T1 | **52** | FurnitureController (432L) needs care |
| 6 | Agent Core & Navigation | 120 | 40% T3, 30% T4, 20% T2, 10% T1 | **120** | Custom pathfinding + action framework |
| 7 | Customer AI & Drinks | 100 | 50% T3, 30% T2, 20% T1 | **72** | FSM + autonomous scoring + order pipeline |
| 8 | Worker AI & Chores | 80 | 50% T3, 30% T2, 20% T1 | **58** | Chore system + hub actions |
| 9 | Machine System | 60 | 40% T3, 30% T2, 20% T4, 10% T1 | **50** | 9 concrete machines share MachineBase pattern |
| 10 | Financial System | 35 | 50% T2, 30% T3, 20% T1 | **20** | Loan math + monthly processing |
| 11 | Prestige & Progression | 40 | 50% T3, 30% T2, 20% T1 | **28** | Multi-source accumulator + tech tree |
| 12 | Quest & Dialogue | 50 | 40% T3, 40% T2, 20% T1 | **30** | PixelCrushers integration adds complexity |
| 13 | Map, Menus & Meta | 120 | 40% T2, 30% T1, 20% T3, 10% T4 | **62** | Save system is critical path |

│   ├── IPerformable.cs
│   ├── IAutonomous.cs
│   ├── IBodyDisposalMachine.cs
│   └── ... (see StructureMap.md)
├── Enums/

│   ├── EConstructionMode.cs

│   ├── EAgentTag.cs
│   ├── ENeedType.cs

│   ├── TransactionType.cs
│   └── TransactionTag.cs
└── ThirdParty/
    └── (Animancer, A*, PixelCrushers, DOTween, EasySave3, Spine, FinalIK, etc.)
```

---

## 2. Naming Conventions

| Convention | Pattern | Example |
|------------|---------|---------|
| System folder | `_Name-System/` | `_Machine-System/` |
| ScriptableObject | `SO_Name` | `SO_Drink`, `SO_Furniture` |
| Interface | `IName` | `IMachine`, `IPoolable` |
| Enum | `EName` | `EBarStyle`, `EActionPriority` |
| DataService | `NameService` or `NameCalculator` | `PathfindingService`, `LoanCalculator` |
| Wrapper | `W_Name` | `W_Agent`, `W_Machine` |
| Field binding | `Field_Name` | `Field_Money`, `Field_Prestige` |
| Singleton | `*Singleton<T>` base | `CTSSingleton<T>`, `MonoSingleton<T>` |
| Event | `On*` / `*Changed` / `*Completed` | `OnBuildablePlaced`, `VictimHarvested` |
| Action class | `AgentAction*` / `CustomerAction*` / `WorkerAction*` / `WorkerChore*` | `WorkerChoreDrinkPreparation` |
| Autonomous SO | `AutonomousAction*` | `AutonomousActionFindSeat` |

---

## 3. Class Responsibilities

### MonoBehaviour Rules
1. MonoBehaviours handle **Unity lifecycle only**: Awake, OnEnable/Disable, Update, OnDestroy
2. Business logic lives in **DataServices** (pure C# classes, no MonoBehaviour)
3. MonoBehaviours **delegate** to DataServices for calculations
4. No `FindObjectOfType` except during initialization (and document why)
5. Prefer `[Inject]` via CTS DI over manual singleton access

### Singleton Rules
1. Use `CTSSingleton<T>` for systems needing DI injection
2. Use `MonoSingleton<T>` for simple singleton services
3. Use `static` classes only for stateless registries (`Agents`, `Workers`, `CustomerManager`)
4. Every singleton must document what it owns and who reads it
5. New singletons require justification — prefer dependency injection

### Event Rules
1. Use C# `event Action<T>` for component-to-component communication
2. Use `EventManager` (keyed bus) for cross-system broadcasts where decoupling is critical
3. **No direct cross-system calls** — use events or DI-injected interfaces
4. Static events must be unsubscribed in OnDisable/OnDestroy
5. Document event flow for complex pipelines (order, machine process, etc.)

---

## 4. Decoupling Patterns

### Current Coupling Issues
1. `MonoSingleton<T>.Instance` accessed directly from 50+ classes
2. `AgentSoundManager` subscribes to 37 events from 25+ action classes
3. `Prestige` subscribes to 8+ different system events
4. `ConstructionSystem` directly accesses UI singletons
5. Quest system deeply coupled to PixelCrushers API

### Target Patterns
1. **Event-driven**: Systems communicate via events, not direct calls
2. **Interface injection**: `[Inject]` interfaces instead of concrete singletons
3. **Mediator for sound**: `AgentSoundManager` uses a mediator pattern — agents publish sound events, mediator routes to audio
4. **Observer for prestige**: Systems fire generic `ValueChanged` events, Prestige subscribes
5. **Adapter for PixelCrushers**: Thin adapter layer between game quests and Dialogue System

---

## 5. Lifecycle Rules

### Initialization Order
1. `CTSFactory` scans scene → creates `TypeInjector` per type
2. `[DefaultExecutionOrder]` determines constructor call order
3. `[Constructor("MethodName")]` methods run before Awake
4. `[Inject]` fields populated after constructors
5. `Awake()` / `SingletonAwake()` runs after injection
6. `OnEnable()` subscribes to events
7. `Start()` for post-initialization logic

### Destruction Order
1. `OnDisable()` unsubscribes from events
2. `OnDestroy()` cleanup, pool return
3. Singletons use `SingletonDestroyed()` callback
4. `CTSSceneManager.BeingDestroyed` flag prevents stale references

### Agent Lifecycle
```
Pool.Pull() → Agent.Spawned → ContextualFSM.SetStateNormal()
  → AgentFSM starts (CustomerFSM/WorkerFSM)
  → Autonomous actions scored every SpreadUpdate
  → Actions queued in AgentActionPlayer
  → ...
  → Agent.Died / Agent.Despawned → Pool.Push()
```

---

## 6. C# Features & Patterns

### Required Patterns
- **Generic constraints** on DataServices: `where T : class`
- **Readonly structs** for data transfer: `PathCorner`, `BuyingData`, `CalendarCoord`
- **IDisposable** for pooled references: `PooledRef<T>`
- **Async/await** for Addressable loading (already used)
- **Value tuples** for multi-return methods (prefer over out params)

### Avoid
- `FindObjectOfType` at runtime (use registries/injection)
- Raw `string` comparison (use `StringKey` system)
- `MonoBehaviour` for pure data (use plain C# classes or structs)
- Nested coroutines deeper than 2 levels (use action queue instead)
- `public` fields on MonoBehaviours (use `[SerializeField] private` + property)

---

## 7. Testing Strategy

### Unit Testable (DataServices)
| Service | Test Focus |
|---------|-----------|
| `GridMathService` | Neighbor lookup, coordinate conversion, boundary checks |
| `WallGenerationService` | Wall auto-generation from cell configurations |
| `BuildCostCalculator` | Cost calculation accuracy |
| `PathfindingService` | Path corner optimization, distance calculations |
| `SatisfactionCalculator` | Modifier application, score bounds |
| `LoanCalculator` | Interest rates, installments, edge cases |
| `PrestigeCalculator` | Level thresholds, accumulator totals |
| `ChorePriorityResolver` | Priority ordering, room filtering |
| `OrderPipelineService` | Order state transitions |

### Integration Testable (Scene-based)
| System | Test Focus |
|--------|-----------|
| Construction | Grid generation → wall spawn → room detection |
| Agent Navigation | Path request → movement → arrival |
| Machine Pipeline | Load → process → unload → stock update |
| Order Pipeline | Customer order → worker prepare → deliver → pay |
| Save/Load | Save state → load state → verify integrity |

### Not Directly Testable
| System | Reason |
|--------|--------|
| DOTween sequences | Visual timing |
| Animancer animations | Animation clips |
| Spine portraits | 2D skeleton rendering |
| Audio mixing | Sound engine |

# PhaseMap — btycoon (Bloody Bar Tycoon)

> Each phase depends only on earlier phases, never forward.
> Files listed are from `CTS.*` assemblies (game code only).

---

## Phase 1 — Core Framework
**What It Looks Like When Running:** Nothing visible — pure infrastructure. Unit-testable without Unity scenes.

| Metric | Value |
|--------|-------|
| **File count** | ~235 |
| **Difficulty** | ★★☆☆☆ Medium |
| **Weight** | 8% |

### Assemblies
- **CTS.Core** (165 files) — Base classes, DI container, pooling, FSM, events, StringKey, world selector, update spreader
- **CTS.Utilities** (70 files) — Time, collections, addressables wrappers, animation tracking, conditions, materials

### Key Systems
- `CTSBehaviour` / `CTSSingleton<T>` / `MonoSingleton<T>` base hierarchy
- `CTSFactory` DI container (attribute-based `[Inject]`, `[Constructor]`, scopes)
- `Pooler` static pooling system (`PooledObject`, `PooledRef<T>`)
- `FSM<T>` + `State<T>` state machine
- `EventManager` keyed event bus + `CTSEvent<T>`
- `StringKey` / `StringKey<T>` interned ID system
- `UpdateSpreader` central update loop
- `WorldSelector` raycast selection
- `ILockable` / `Lock` / `LockToggle` reference-counted locking
- `GameTime` / `UnscaledGameTime` / `CooldownManager`
- `SerializableDictionary<K,V>`

### Dependencies
None (foundation layer)

---

### Key Systems
- Map world with selectable locations (career progression)
- EasySave3-based save/load with per-object serializers
- Game mode management (career vs freemode)
- Dynamic music mixing (13 themes × 4 layers)
- Steam achievement tracking
- Dev console with 54 commands
- Bug report system
- Twitch API integration

### Dependencies
Phase 1–12 (meta layer wraps everything)

---

## Cross-Phase Modification Table

| When Building Phase | Also Modify In |
|---------------------|----------------|
| Phase 4 (Construction) | Phase 11 (Prestige subscribes to construction events) |
| Phase 5 (Furniture) | Phase 11 (Prestige subscribes to furniture value changes) |
| Phase 6 (Agent Core) | Phase 13 (Save/load for agent data) |
| Phase 7 (Customer AI) | Phase 10 (Money from customer payments), Phase 11 (Reviews → Prestige) |
| Phase 8 (Worker AI) | Phase 10 (Worker salaries), Phase 9 (Machine chores) |
| Phase 9 (Machines) | Phase 3 (Stock output), Phase 11 (Tech tree points), Phase 10 (Body disposal credibility → vigilance) |
| Phase 10 (Financial) | Phase 11 (Loan unlock by prestige level) |
| Phase 12 (Quests) | Phase 10 (Quest rewards → money), Phase 11 (Quest rewards → prestige) |

---

# StructureMap — btycoon (Bloody Bar Tycoon)

> Internal structure per phase: system folders, DataService candidates, interfaces, naming conventions.

---

## Phase 1 — Core Framework

### System Folders (`_-Systems/`)

| System Folder | Scripts | Purpose |
|---------------|---------|---------|
| `_DI-System/` | `CTSFactory`, `TypeInjector`, `IInjector`, `IConstructor<T>`, `IConstruct<T…>`, scopes | Attribute-based dependency injection |
| `_Pool-System/` | `Pooler`, `PooledObject`, `PooledRef<T>`, `IPoolable`, `IPoolCallbackReceiver` | Object pooling |
| `_FSM-System/` | `FSM<T>`, `State<T>`, `BaseStateMachine<T>`, `FiniteMultiStateMachine<TEnum,T>`, `ScriptableMultiStateMachine`, `ScriptableState` | State machine variants |
| `_Event-System/` | `EventManager`, `CTSEvent`, `CTSEvent<T>` | Keyed event bus + instance events |
| `_Update-System/` | `UpdateSpreader`, `IUpdatable`, `ILateUpdatable`, `ISpreadUpdatable` | Central update distribution |
| `_Selection-System/` | `WorldSelector`, selection modes | Raycast-based world selection |

### DataService Candidates
| Candidate | Current Location | Extractable Logic |
|-----------|-----------------|-------------------|
| `StringKeyService` | `StringKey` / `StringKey<T>` | Interned ID creation/lookup — already pure C# |
| `LockService` | `ILockable` / `Lock` / `LockToggle` | Ref-counted locking — already pure C# |

### Interface Candidates
| Interface | Purpose | Consumers |
|-----------|---------|-----------|
| `IPoolable` | Pool lifecycle | All pooled objects |
| `ILockable` | Ref-counted enable/disable | UI controls, agents, systems |
| `IUpdatable` / `ISpreadUpdatable` | Tick registration | Agents, FSMs, managers |
| `IGive<T>` / `IReceive<T>` | Data flow contracts | Stock, items |

### Prefix Assignments
| Prefix | Type | Examples |
|--------|------|---------|
| (none) | Base classes keep original names | `CTSBehaviour`, `CTSSingleton<T>` |
| `SO_` | ScriptableObject data | (none in this phase) |
| `I` | Interfaces | `IPoolable`, `ILockable`, `IUpdatable` |

<!-- ==== FILE: LEARN/btycoon/SystemPortabilityMap.md ==== -->
# SystemPortabilityMap — btycoon (Bloody Bar Tycoon)

> Classifies every system by portability level.
> **L0** = game-agnostic (reusable as-is in other Unity projects).
> **L1+** = game-specific (references btycoon data, enums, or domain logic).

---

## L0 — Fully Portable (Engine/Framework)

| System | Assembly | Files | Notes |
|--------|----------|-------|-------|
| CTSFactory (DI Container) | CTS.Core | ~15 | Attribute-based scanning, zero game refs |
| CTSBehaviour / CTSSingleton | CTS.Core | ~5 | Base classes for all MonoBehaviours |
| StringKey / StringKey\<T\> | CTS.Core | ~4 | Interned uint ID system |
| Pooler / PooledObject / PooledRef | CTS.Core | ~6 | Generic object pooling |
| FSM\<T\> / State\<T\> | CTS.Core | ~4 | Simple generic FSM |
| FiniteMultiStateMachine | CTS.Core | ~3 | Multi-state FSM |
| ScriptableMultiStateMachine | CTS.Core | ~5 | Scriptable-driven FSM |
| EventManager (keyed bus) | CTS.Core | ~3 | String-keyed event bus |
| CTSEvent\<T\> | CTS.Core | ~2 | Operator-overloaded event |
| UpdateSpreader | CTS.Core | ~2 | Distributes Update across frames |
| CTS.Utilities extensions | CTS.Utilities | ~70 | Math, collections, reflection helpers |
| Panel system (PanelBase) | CTS.UI | ~12 | Generic UI panel open/close/animate |
| ScriptableSettings | CTS.ScriptableSettings | ~13 | SO-based config framework |
| DevConsole | CTS.DevConsole | ~51 | In-game dev console + commands |
| InputGeneration | CTS.InputGeneration | ~3 | Input abstraction layer |
| Report system | CTS.Report | ~3 | Generic report interface |
| Emotes runtime | CTS.Emotes.Runtime | ~8 | Generic emote display system |

**Total L0: ~209 files**

---

## L1 — Lightly Game-Specific (Needs Thin Adapter)

| System | Assembly | Files | Coupling Point | Adapter Needed |
|--------|----------|-------|---------------|---------------|
| StockInventory | CTS.StockInventory | ~9 | References `SO_StockItem`, generic otherwise | Replace SO type |
| TechTree | CTS.TechTree | ~13 | References `SO_TechTreeTechnology`, otherwise generic | Replace SO type |
| CTSSceneManager | CTS.Core | ~3 | Knows about btycoon scene names | Abstract scene list |
| Cursor system | CTS.Core | ~4 | References construction-specific cursor states | Parameterize states |

**Total L1: ~29 files**

---

## L2+ — Game-Specific (Btycoon Domain Logic)

### Construction Domain (Phase 4)
| System | Files | Key Coupling |
|--------|-------|-------------|
| ConstructionGrid / Cell | ~40 | Grid math + EBarStyle + wall rules |
| WallSystem | ~25 | Wall auto-generation, door placement |
| RoomBuilding / Detection | ~20 | Room detection algorithm tied to grid |
| BuildablePlacement | ~30 | EConstructionMode, snapping rules |
| SurfaceObjectPainting | ~15 | Furniture surface placement |
| Elevator system | ~10 | Multi-floor grid linking |

### Agent Domain (Phases 6-8)
| System | Files | Key Coupling |
|--------|-------|-------------|
| Agent core / spawning | ~30 | EAgentTag, ENeedType, EGender |
| AgentActionPlayer / Actions | ~50 | Action priority queue + coroutines |
| CustomerFSM / autonomous | ~40 | Customer scoring + seat finding |
| WorkerFSM / chores | ~35 | Chore priority + hub actions |
| ContextualFSM | ~15 | Life-state machine |
| Agent components (carry, need, visual) | ~25 | Deep coupling to agent data |
| AgentSoundManager | ~5 | 37 event subscriptions |

### Machine Domain (Phase 9)
| System | Files | Key Coupling |
|--------|-------|-------------|
| MachineBase + 9 machines | ~30 | DOTween sequences, stock items |
| Station system | ~15 | Worker↔machine interaction |
| Body disposal machines | ~10 | Crime system integration |

### Economy Domain (Phases 10-11)
| System | Files | Key Coupling |
|--------|-------|-------------|
| Financial (money, loans, stats) | ~20 | TransactionType, ChargeTypes |
| Prestige + accumulator | ~15 | Multi-source event aggregation |
| Calendar system | ~10 | Monthly/weekly processing |

### Furniture & Items (Phase 5)
| System | Files | Key Coupling |
|--------|-------|-------------|
| FurnitureController + variants | ~40 | SO_Furniture, EBarStyle filtering |

| Trap system | ~15 | Crime/body disposal integration |

### Quest & Content (Phase 12)
| System | Files | Key Coupling |
|--------|-------|-------------|
| Quest system | ~25 | PixelCrushers Dialogue System API |
| Dialogue integration | ~15 | Ink + PixelCrushers bridge |
| Named characters | ~10 | Hardcoded character data |

### Meta Systems (Phase 13)
| System | Files | Key Coupling |
|--------|-------|-------------|
| Save/Load (ES3) | ~30 | EasySave3 + all serialized state |
| Map system | ~20 | World selection, unlocking |
| Main menu / settings | ~20 | Steam integration |
| Music mixing | ~15 | MusicMixManager + bar ambiance |
| Camera system | ~10 | Construction/play mode switching |
| UI panels (game-specific) | ~65 | All domain panels |
| Achievement system | ~10 | Steam achievements |

**Total L2+: ~2,308 files**

---

## Summary

| Level | Files | % | Reusability |
|-------|-------|---|-------------|
| **L0** (Portable) | ~209 | 8% | Drop-in to any Unity project |
| **L1** (Adapter needed) | ~29 | 1% | Reusable with thin adapter |
| **L2+** (Game-specific) | ~2,308 | 91% | btycoon domain logic |
| **Total** | ~2,546 | 100% | |

> The CTS framework (L0) is a solid, reusable Unity toolkit. The game logic (L2+) is deeply domain-specific as expected for a tycoon game.

<!-- ==== FILE: LEARN/btycoon/surfer.md ==== -->
# surfer — btycoon (Bloody Bar Tycoon)

> Tracks every analysis prompt and its outcome for this project.

---

## Prompt 1: Initial Source Analysis (`init`)

**Date**: 2025  
**Scope**: Full project initialization  
**Input**: MAIN-SOURCE/btycoon/ (2,546 game .cs files, 11 assemblies, 31,958 total project files)

### What was done
1. Read entire project stub (31,963 lines) — identified asset-only folders to skip
2. Read ALL 2,546 game code .cs files via batched subagent exploration
3. Mapped full dependency graph across all 11 CTS.* assemblies
4. Identified god objects (14 files > 400 lines)
5. Catalogued ~25+ singletons, ~150+ static events, ~200+ instance events
6. Mapped DI container (CTSFactory), 3 FSM systems, pooling, StringKey IDs

### Documents Generated
| Document | Status |
|----------|--------|
| ARCHITECTURE.md | ✅ Created |
| PhaseMap.md | ✅ Created (13 phases) |
| StructureMap.md | ✅ Created |
| GOAL.md | ✅ Created |

| SystemPortabilityMap.md | ✅ Created (L0: 209 files, L2+: 2,308 files) |
| surfer.md | ✅ Created |

### Key Findings
- **Engine**: Unity 2022.x + URP
- **DI**: Custom CTSFactory with [Inject], [Constructor], [InjectScope] attributes
- **Dominant pattern**: C# events (not UnityEvents, not message bus)
- **Agent architecture**: Dual FSM (behavior + life-state) with priority action queue
- **Biggest risk**: ConstructionGrid (1,489 lines) — core god object
- **Third-party**: Animancer, A* Pathfinding, PixelCrushers, DOTween Pro, EasySave3, Spine, Final IK, Steamworks.NET
- **L0 reusable framework**: ~209 files (8%) — CTSFactory, FSMs, Pooler, StringKey, UpdateSpreader, Panel system, DevConsole

# ARCHITECTURE — fwr (The Farmer Was Replaced)

## Source Overview

| Metric | Value |
|--------|-------|
| **Total game code .cs files** | ~200 |
| **Core assembly** | 112 files (main game logic) |
| **Utils assembly** | 84 game files + 21 LeanTween files (third-party) |
| **Assembly-CSharp** | 2 game files + 1 auto-generated |
| **Engine** | Unity 6 (6000.x), URP, C# 9.0, .NET Framework 4.0 |
| **Total stub files** | 14,962 (235.67 MB) |

### Folder Structure
```
fwr/
├── Assemblies/          # Engine + third-party DLLs (skip)
├── Assets/              # Audio, Meshes, Textures, Fonts, Shaders, Sprites, Prefabs, Scenes
├── Scripts/
│   ├── Assembly-CSharp/ # AchievementSO.cs, CreateItemTextures.cs
│   ├── Core/            # ★ Main game logic (112 .cs files)
│   ├── Utils/           # Framework + Py types + options + LeanTween
│   ├── com.rlabrecque.steamworks.net/  # Third-party: Steamworks
│   ├── FMODUnity/       # Third-party: FMOD audio middleware
│   ├── FMODUnityResonance/  # Third-party: FMOD resonance
│   ├── System/          # .NET system stubs
│   └── netstandard/     # .NET standard stubs
```

### Game Concept
"The Farmer Was Replaced" is a **programming automation game** where the player writes Python-like code to control drones that farm crops on a grid. The game includes a custom Python interpreter (tokenizer → parser → AST → execution), grid-based farm simulation, research/unlock progression, leaderboards, and Steam integration.

---

## Dependency Graph

### Domain Groups

#### 1. Interpreter Domain (Tokenizer → Parser → AST → Execution)
```
Tokenizer → TokenStream → Token, TokenType
Parser → TokenStream, All AST Nodes, CodeWindow, Farm (keywords)
Node (abstract) → ProgramState, Execution, CodeWindow, BoxedNodeParams
  ├── BinaryExprNode, ComparisonNode, UnaryExprNode
  ├── AssignmentNode, ValueNode, LiteralNode
  ├── CallNode, FunctionNode, DefNode
  ├── BranchNode, ForNode, ImportNode
  ├── SequenceNode, ListNode, SetNode, DictNode, TupleNode
  ├── BracketNode, ReturnNode, BreakNode, ContinueNode, PassNode, NoOpNode
  └── Control flow: BreakStatement, ContinueStatement, ReturnStatement (exceptions)
Execution → Simulation, ProgramState, BuiltinFunctions, Farm, Drone, all Py types
ProgramState → Scope, Node, Execution, ModuleState, PyDroneHandle
Scope → FunctionNode, IPyObject, ResourceManager (SO lookups)
BuiltinFunctions (static) → Simulation, Execution, ProgramState, all Py types, Farm, ItemBlock
```

#### 2. Py Type System (Utils/)
```
IPyObject (root interface)
├── IPySequence : IPyObject, IReadOnlyList, IPyIndexable
├── IPyNameSpace : IPyObject
├── IPyIndexable
│
├── PyNumber (double wrapper) ← PyBool : PyNumber
├── PyString : IPySequence
├── PyList : IList, IPySequence
├── PyDict : ICollection, IPyIndexable
├── PySet : ICollection
├── PyTuple : IPySequence (immutable)
├── PyRange : IPySequence (lazy)
├── PyNone (singleton)
├── PyModule : IPyNameSpace
├── PyConstBag : IPyNameSpace
├── PyFunction : IPyObject (holds AST or native delegate)
├── PyObjectBox (mutable value wrapper for dict values)
├── PyDroneHandle : IPyObject (drone entity reference)
├── PyGridDirection : IPyObject (GridDirection wrapper)
├── PyUnassigned (sentinel)
├── PyCollectionEnumerator
└── InternalPySequence : IPySequence (internal arg wrapper)
```

#### 3. Simulation Domain
```
MainSim (SINGLETON) → Simulation, Execution, Farm, CodeWindow, Workspace, Saver
  └── Spawns background Thread for SimulationLoop
Simulation → Farm, Execution, Duration, TimerManager
Farm → GridManager, Drone[], ItemBlock, UnlockSO map
GridManager → FarmObject map, PumpkinController, water/cactus arrays
FarmObject (base) → FarmObjectSO, Simulation, GridManager, Duration, ItemBlock
  ├── Growable : FarmObject → growth timer, yield, fertilize, companion
  │   ├── Cactus : Growable
  │   ├── Sunflower : Growable
  │   ├── Pumpkin : Growable → PumpkinController
  │   ├── TreePlant : Growable
  │   └── Apple : Growable (snake game)
  ├── HedgePlant : FarmObject (maze walls)
  │   └── Treasure : HedgePlant (maze reward)
  ├── BushPlant : Growable (maze generator)
  ├── Dinosaur : FarmObject (snake game)
  ├── DeadPumpkin : FarmObject
  ├── Ground : FarmObject
  │   └── Soil : Ground
  └── Hat (plain class) → HatSO, Simulation, Drone
      └── DinosaurHat : Hat (snake game hat)
Drone → Simulation, Hat, GridManager, FarmObject interactions
PumpkinController → GridManager, Pumpkin merging logic
```

#### 4. UI Domain
```
Workspace : MonoBehaviour → CodeWindow[], DocsWindow[], Window[], ContainerScaler
  ├── CodeWindow : MonoBehaviour, ITooltipHandler → Parser, CodeInputField, CodeCompleter, BlinkManager
  ├── DocsWindow : MonoBehaviour → MarkdownText
  ├── Window : MonoBehaviour (draggable, dockable panels)
  ├── SearchBox : MonoBehaviour → CodeWindow, DocsWindow
  └── CodeCompleter : MonoBehaviour → CodeOption[]
Menu : MonoBehaviour → Saver, SaveChooser, OptionMenu
SaveChooser : MonoBehaviour → SaveOption[], Saver, WarningPopup
ResearchMenu : MonoBehaviour → UnlockBox[], UnlockSO tree
Tooltip : MonoBehaviour → TooltipInfo, MarkdownText
WarningPopup : MonoBehaviour → ColoredButton (modal dialog)
HatPopup (SINGLETON) → MarkdownText
Inventory : MonoBehaviour → ItemUI[], ItemBlock
ItemUI : MonoBehaviour, ITooltipHandler → ItemSO
LeaderboardManager : MonoBehaviour → Leaderboard
Leaderboard : MonoBehaviour → LeaderboardEntry, SteamLeaderboard
```

#### 5. Settings & Options
```
OptionHolder (static) → OptionSO[], file-backed persistence
  fires: OnOptionChanged
OptionSO : ScriptableObject (base)
  ├── CycleOptionSO → CycleOptionUI
  ├── DropdownOptionSO → DropdownOptionUI
  ├── SliderOptionSO → SliderOptionUI
  └── KeyBindOptionSO → KeyBindOptionUI
OptionUI : MonoBehaviour, ITooltipHandler (base)

#### 6. Audio & VFX

FMODSoundManager (static) → SoundReferencesSO, FMOD API
VFXManager : MonoBehaviour (SINGLETON) → IVisualEffect pool
  ├── ParticleEffect : IVisualEffect

  └── PrintSign : IVisualEffect

#### 7. Persistence
```
Saver (static) → SaveGame, OldSaveGame, MainSim, Workspace, CodeWindow, FileSystemWatcher
SaveGame → ItemBlock, Pair<string,string>
SaveChooser → SaveOption, Saver
```

#### 8. Theme & Localization
```
ThemeManager : MonoBehaviour (SINGLETON) → ColorTheme[]
  fires: OnThemeChanged
ColorTheme : ScriptableObject — full UI color palette
Localizer → OptionHolder (language setting), file-based string tables
TMPTextLocalizer → Localizer auto-binding for TMP text
```

#### 9. Data Assets (ScriptableObjects)
```
FarmObjectSO : ScriptableObject, IPyObject — farm entity definitions
ItemSO : ScriptableObject, IPyObject — item definitions
UnlockSO : ScriptableObject — research tree node data
HatSO : ScriptableObject, IPyObject — cosmetic hat data
LeaderboardSO : ScriptableObject, IPyObject — leaderboard config

AchievementSO : ScriptableObject — achievement display data
TradeSO : ScriptableObject, IPyObject — trade/recipe data
SoundReferencesSO : ScriptableObject — FMOD event references
```

## God Objects

| File | Lines | Responsibilities | Split Candidates |
|------|-------|-----------------|------------------|
| **BuiltinFunctions.cs** | ~900 | 49 game-callable functions, 5 collection methods, unlock registry, item conversion | Split by domain: FarmActions, QueryFunctions, DroneActions, CollectionMethods |
| **Parser.cs** | ~1100 | Full recursive-descent parser, operator precedence, block parsing, expression parsing | Reasonably cohesive for a parser, but could extract ExpressionParser |
| **CodeWindow.cs** | ~1070 | Code editing, execution control, parse caching, undo/redo tracking, search highlight, tooltip, UI layout | Split: CodeEditor (text), ExecutionController, CodeWindowUI |
| **Execution.cs** | ~700 | Main execution loop, side effect dispatch (30+ cases), drone scheduling, breakpoints | Extract SideEffectDispatcher from ApplySideEffect |
| **MainSim.cs** | ~780 | Singleton hub, sim thread management, leaderboard orchestration, UI event coordination, tooltip, hat unlocks | Extract LeaderboardController, SimThread management |
| **Saver.cs** | ~320 | Save/load progress, save/load code files, file watcher, backup, old save migration | Reasonably cohesive but mixes two save domains |

## Singleton Registry

| Singleton | Type | What It Owns | Who Reads It |
|-----------|------|-------------|--------------|
| **MainSim.Inst** | MonoBehaviour | Simulation, Execution, Farm, inventory, unlocks, workspace refs, leaderboard state | Nearly everything — 40+ classes access it |
| **HatPopup.Inst** | MonoBehaviour | Hat unlock popup UI | MainSim (enqueues hat popups) |
| **ThemeManager** | MonoBehaviour (implicit singleton) | ColorTheme[], current theme | All UI classes subscribe to OnThemeChanged |
| **SoundManager** | MonoBehaviour (implicit singleton) | FMOD sound dispatch queue | MainSim, Drone, UnlockBox, PiggyBank |
| **VFXManager** | MonoBehaviour (implicit singleton) | VFX pool and throttling | MainSim, FarmObject, Growable |
| **TimerManager** | MonoBehaviour (implicit singleton) | Sorted delayed callback list | Tooltip, Simulation (via Farm.sim) |

### Static Classes Acting as Singletons
| Class | Purpose | Accessed By |
|-------|---------|------------|
| **ResourceManager** | SO registry (all FarmObjects, Items, Unlocks, Hats, Leaderboards) | ~30 classes |
| **BuiltinFunctions** | Python builtin function/method registry | Execution, CodeWindow, MarkdownText, Scope |
| **Achievements** | Steam achievement/stat tracking, golden hat unlocks | ~15 classes |
| **Saver** | Save/load game state to disk | MainSim, Menu, SaveChooser |
| **OptionHolder** | Persistent options with change events | ~20 classes |
| **CodeUtilities** | Syntax highlighting, error formatting | ~25 classes |
| **Helper** | Number formatting, rich-text, hashing | ~15 classes |
| **Localizer** | Localized string lookup | ~20 classes |
| **FMODSoundManager** | FMOD event playback wrapper | SoundManager, Drone |
| **Logger** | Output log buffer for in-game console | Node, ProgramState, MainSim |
| **StringIds** | Item name↔id mapping | ItemBlock, Achievements, Farm |
| **Tokenizer** | Lexer (stateless) | CodeWindow, Parser |
| **TooltipUtils** | Tooltip text generation | CodeWindow, UnlockBox, Scope |

## Coupling Hotspots

### FindObjectOfType Calls
**None found** — the codebase avoids FindObjectOfType entirely. All references flow through:
- `MainSim.Inst` singleton
- Direct serialized references ([SerializeField])
- Static class access

### Direct Cross-Domain References
| From | To | Coupling Type |
|------|----|--------------|
| AST Nodes → CodeWindow | Every node stores a `CodeWindow` reference (via BoxedNodeParams) | Tight: interpreter knows about UI |
| Execution → Farm, GridManager, Drone | Side effect dispatch directly manipulates game state | Tight: interpreter reaches into simulation |
| BuiltinFunctions → Simulation, Farm | Static functions directly call simulation APIs | Tight: builtins coupled to game state |
| Saver → Workspace, Window, CodeWindow | Serialization directly reads UI layout state | Tight: persistence knows about UI hierarchy |
| Scope → ResourceManager | Variable lookup falls back to SO name matching | Medium: interpreter coupled to data layer |
| ResearchMenu → MainSim.Inst | Direct singleton access for unlock state | Medium: standard Unity pattern |

### Static Instance Access
`MainSim.Inst` is accessed by **40+ classes** across all domains. It is the primary coupling vector in the codebase.

---

## Event System

### C# Events (Action/delegates)
| Event | Owner | Subscribers |
|-------|-------|------------|
| `OptionHolder.OnOptionChanged` | OptionHolder (static) | Saver, Workspace, ResearchMenu, OptionMenu, UIScaler, ResolutionOptionUpdater, FMODSoundManager, WarningPopup |
| `ThemeManager.Inst.OnThemeChanged` | ThemeManager | CodeWindow, ResearchMenu, ItemUI, UnlockBox, CodeOption, ErrorMessage, OptionUI subclasses, SpoilerWarning |
| `Logger.OnOutputChanged` | Logger (static) | OutputText |

### Unity Events (from UI components)
| Component | Events Used |
|-----------|------------|
| CodeInputField | onTextInserted, onTextMeshUpdated, onEndEdit, onCarretMoved, onBackSpace, onSelect, onTextSelection |
| ColoredButton | OnClick |
| Various buttons/sliders | Unity's onClick, onValueChanged |

### No Custom Event Bus
The project does not use a central event bus. Communication is through:
1. Direct method calls via `MainSim.Inst`
2. C# events on static classes
3. Thread synchronization via `lock(lockSimulation)`
4. ConcurrentQueue for cross-thread communication (hat unlocks, code changes)

---

## Data Flow

```
ScriptableObjects (FarmObjectSO, ItemSO, UnlockSO, HatSO, LeaderboardSO)
    ↓ loaded by ResourceManager.LoadAll()
Runtime Instances (FarmObject, Drone, Hat, ItemBlock)
    ↓ created by Farm/GridManager/Simulation
Manager Layer (MainSim → Simulation → Execution)
    ↓ reads/writes via thread-safe wrappers
UI Layer (Workspace → CodeWindow, ResearchMenu → UnlockBox, Inventory → ItemUI)
    ↓ user actions flow back via
Code Execution (CodeWindow → Parser → Execution → SideEffects → Farm)
    ↓ persistence via
Saver → SaveGame JSON → disk
```

### Threading Model
- **Main thread**: Unity Update loop, UI, rendering (FarmRenderer, BlinkManager)
- **Background thread**: `MainSim.SimulationLoop()` — tight loop calling `Simulation.RunNextStep()`
- **Synchronization**: `lock(lockSimulation)`, `volatile` fields, `ConcurrentDictionary`, `ConcurrentQueue`
- **Cross-thread**: Queued effects (sounds, VFX, blinks, hat popups) accumulated during sim, applied in Update

---

## Inheritance Chains

### Worth Preserving
```
FarmObject
├── Growable (growth timer, yield, fertilize, companion logic)
│   ├── Cactus, Sunflower, Pumpkin, TreePlant, Apple, BushPlant
├── HedgePlant (maze walls)
│   └── Treasure (maze reward)
├── Dinosaur (snake game entity)
├── DeadPumpkin
└── Ground
    └── Soil

Hat → DinosaurHat (only one specialization)

Node (abstract AST base)
└── 20+ concrete node types (well-structured AST hierarchy)

OptionSO → CycleOptionSO, DropdownOptionSO, SliderOptionSO, KeyBindOptionSO
OptionUI → CycleOptionUI, DropdownOptionUI, SliderOptionUI, KeyBindOptionUI

IPyObject hierarchy (well-designed type system)
```

### Candidates for Flattening
- `Hat → DinosaurHat`: Only one specialization; could use composition
- `HedgePlant → Treasure`: Treasure has very different behavior from HedgePlant

# Estimate — fwr (The Farmer Was Replaced)

## Methodology
Hours = file count × complexity tier multiplier

| Tier | Multiplier | Description |
|------|-----------|-------------|
| T1 | 0.25 hr | Enums, data structs, simple SOs, interfaces |
| T2 | 0.5 hr | Small classes <100 lines, pure data containers |
| T3 | 1.0 hr | Medium classes 100–300 lines, moderate logic |
| T4 | 2.0 hr | Large classes 300–600 lines, complex logic |
| T5 | 4.0 hr | God objects 600+ lines, heavy refactoring needed |

---

## Total Estimate

| Phase | Files | Hours | Cumulative |
|-------|-------|-------|------------|
| 0 — Foundation Types & Data | 42 | 17.0 | 17.0 |
| 1 — Python Type System | 23 | 14.25 | 31.25 |
| 2 — Interpreter Core | 32 | 29.5 | 60.75 |
| 3 — Farm Simulation | 22 | 19.0 | 79.75 |
| 4 — Game Bridge | 5 | 11.5 | 91.25 |
| 5 — UI Framework & Code Editor | 28 | 25.5 | 116.75 |
| 6 — Game UI & Menus | 20 | 14.5 | 131.25 |
| 7 — Persistence & Steam | 14 | 9.0 | 140.25 |
| 8 — Audio, VFX & Rendering | 14 | 9.0 | 149.25 |
| **TOTAL** | **~200** | **149.25 hr** | |

### Risk Factors
- **Threading complexity** (+15%): Background sim thread with lock-based synchronization adds refactoring risk in Phase 4
- **Interpreter correctness** (+10%): AST node behavior must be preserved exactly — any regression breaks user code
- **God object splitting** (+10%): MainSim, Execution, BuiltinFunctions, CodeWindow are deeply coupled

### Adjusted Estimate
**149.25 × 1.12 (avg risk) ≈ 167 hours**

# GOAL — fwr (The Farmer Was Replaced)

## Target Architecture

### Project Identity
- **Project Name**: The Farmer Was Replaced (fwr)
- **Engine**: Unity 6 (6000.x), URP, C# 9.0
- **Phases**: 9 phases (0–8)
- **Systems**: 22 identified systems

---

## Folder Structure

```
fwr/
├── _-PyTypes/                    # Phase 1: Complete Python type system
├── _-Tokenizer/                  # Phase 2: Lexer
├── _-Parser/                     # Phase 2: Recursive-descent parser
├── _-ASTNodes/                   # Phase 2: Syntax tree node hierarchy
│   ├── Expressions/
│   ├── Statements/
│   └── Collections/
├── _-Runtime/                    # Phase 2: Interpreter runtime state
├── _-FarmCore/                   # Phase 3: Simulation engine
├── _-FarmEntities/               # Phase 3: Farm object hierarchy
│   ├── Crops/
│   ├── Maze/
│   ├── Special/
│   └── Ground/
├── _-Hats/                       # Phase 3: Hat system
├── _-GameBridge/                 # Phase 4: Execution ↔ Simulation
├── _-Workspace/                  # Phase 5: Window management
├── _-CodeEditor/                 # Phase 5: Code editing UI
├── _-DocsViewer/                 # Phase 5: Documentation browser
├── _-Tooltips/                   # Phase 5: Tooltip system
├── _-Options/                    # Phase 5: Settings UI
├── _-Theme/                      # Phase 5: Theme & localization
├── _-ResearchUI/                 # Phase 6: Research tree UI
├── _-InventoryUI/                # Phase 6: Inventory display
├── _-LeaderboardUI/              # Phase 6: Leaderboard UI
├── _-Menus/                      # Phase 6: Menu system
├── _-Persistence/                # Phase 7: Save/load
├── _-Steam/                      # Phase 7: Steam integration
├── _-Audio/                      # Phase 8: Sound system
├── _-VFX/                        # Phase 8: Visual effects
└── Standalone/                   # Files not in any system
```

---

## Naming Conventions

### Class Prefixes
| Prefix | Meaning | Example |
|--------|---------|---------|
| `SO_` | ScriptableObject data asset | `SO_FarmObject`, `SO_Item`, `SO_Unlock` |
| `Field_` | Serialized field wrapper | `Field_Duration`, `Field_ItemBlock` |
| `W_` | Runtime wrapper around SO data | `W_FarmObject` (wraps SO_FarmObject at runtime) |

### File Naming
- **Systems**: `_-SystemName/` prefix with dash
- **Interfaces**: `I` prefix (`IPyObject`, `IFarmEntity`, `ISideEffectHandler`)
- **Enums**: PascalCase without prefix (`GridDirection`, `SoundEffectType`, `VFXType`)
- **Static utilities**: PascalCase (`Helper`, `CodeUtilities`, `StringIds`)
- **Data structs**: PascalCase (`Duration`, `ItemBlock`, `VFXCall`)

---

## Class Responsibilities

### Single Responsibility Targets

| Current | Problem | Target |
|---------|---------|--------|
| `MainSim` (780 lines) | Singleton hub doing 8+ things | Split: `MainSim` (singleton access only), `SimThreadManager`, `LeaderboardController`, `HoverTooltipProvider` |
| `Execution` (700 lines) | Execution loop + 30+ side effect cases | Split: `Execution` (loop only), `SideEffectDispatcher` (dispatch table) |
| `BuiltinFunctions` (900 lines) | 49 functions + 5 methods in one class | Group by domain: `FarmBuiltins`, `DroneBuiltins`, `QueryBuiltins`, `CollectionBuiltins`, `SystemBuiltins` |
| `CodeWindow` (1070 lines) | Editor + execution control + undo + search | Split: `CodeWindow` (editing), `ExecutionController` (play/stop/step), `CodeSearchHighlighter` |
| `Saver` (320 lines) | Save game + save code + file watcher | Split: `GameSaver`, `CodeFileSaver`, `CodeFileWatcher` |

### Class Size Targets
- **Max lines per class**: 300 (soft limit), 500 (hard limit)
- **Max public methods**: 10 per class
- **Max SerializeField**: 8 per MonoBehaviour

---

## Decoupling Patterns

### 1. Replace MainSim.Inst Direct Access
**Current**: 40+ classes access `MainSim.Inst` for everything
**Target**: Inject dependencies via constructor or [SerializeField]

```csharp
// BEFORE
var unlocks = MainSim.Inst.GetUnlocks();

// AFTER (constructor injection for non-MonoBehaviour)
class ResearchMenu {
    private readonly IUnlockProvider _unlocks;
    public ResearchMenu(IUnlockProvider unlocks) { _unlocks = unlocks; }
}

// AFTER (SerializeField for MonoBehaviour)
[SerializeField] private UnlockProvider _unlocks;
```

### 2. Side Effect Dispatch Table
**Current**: 300-line switch statement in `Execution.ApplySideEffect()`
**Target**: Dictionary-based dispatch with `ISideEffectHandler` interface

```csharp
interface ISideEffectHandler {
    SideEffect Type { get; }
    double Apply(int droneId, Simulation sim, ProgramState state);
}

// Registration
Dictionary<SideEffect, ISideEffectHandler> handlers = new();
```

### 3. Decouple AST from UI
**Current**: Every AST Node holds a `CodeWindow` reference via `BoxedNodeParams`
**Target**: AST nodes hold source location info only; UI binding happens at execution layer

```csharp
// BEFORE (in BoxedNodeParams)
public CodeWindow codeWindow;

// AFTER
public int fileId;  // index into a file registry
public int startIndex;
public int endIndex;
```

### 4. Event-Based Cross-Domain Communication
**Current**: Direct method calls across domains
**Target**: Use existing C# event pattern more broadly

```csharp
// New events to add
public static event Action<string, int> OnUnlockChanged;    // unlock name, level
public static event Action<int, double> OnItemCollected;     // item id, amount
public static event Action<SideEffect> OnSideEffectApplied;  // for UI/audio reactions
```

---

## Lifecycle Rules

### MonoBehaviour Lifecycle
1. **Awake**: Singleton init, cache Camera.main
2. **OnEnable**: Subscribe to events (ThemeManager.OnThemeChanged, OptionHolder.OnOptionChanged)
3. **Start**: One-time setup, spawn background threads
4. **Update**: Process queued effects, update animations, input handling
5. **OnDisable**: Unsubscribe from events
6. **OnDestroy**: Set disposed flags, cleanup threads

### Thread Safety Rules
1. Simulation runs on background thread — never touch Unity API from sim thread
2. Use `lock(lockSimulation)` for all shared state access
3. Queue effects (sound, VFX, blink, hat popup) via `ConcurrentQueue` — apply in Update
4. Use `volatile` for simple boolean flags (`disposed`, `dirty`)
5. All SO data is read-only at runtime — safe to read from any thread

### Initialization Order
```
Phase 0 data → ResourceManager.LoadAll() → Localizer.Init()
→ ThemeManager.Init() → OptionHolder.Load()
→ MainSim.Awake() (singleton) → MainSim.Start() (sim thread)
→ Menu.Play() → Saver.Load() → MainSim.SetupSim()
```

---

## C# Features Used

### Current Usage
- C# 9.0 language features
- `ConcurrentDictionary`, `ConcurrentQueue` for thread safety
- `volatile` for boolean flags
- `lock` for critical sections
- Pattern matching in switch statements
- Tuple decomposition
- Extension methods (GridDirectionMethods, RectExtensions)
- Static classes for utility functions
- `FileSystemWatcher` for hot-reload (code files, themes)

### Avoid
- `FindObjectOfType` — already not used, keep it that way
- `SendMessage` / `BroadcastMessage` — use direct calls or events
- `GameObject.Find` — use serialized references
- Coroutines for game logic — use Duration-based timers (Simulation.StartTimer)
- `async/await` in Unity — stick with thread + lock pattern already in use

---

## Testing Strategy

### Unit Testable (Pure C#)
- **Phase 1**: All Py types — arithmetic, comparison, deep copy, hashing, iteration
- **Phase 2**: Tokenizer, Parser, AST node execution (with mock Scope)
- **Phase 3**: GridManager operations, Farm unlock logic, Growable math
- **Phase 0**: Duration arithmetic, ItemBlock operations, RangeSet, Deque

### Integration Testable (with mock interfaces)
- **Phase 4**: Execution loop with ISideEffectHandler mocks
- **Phase 4**: BuiltinFunctions with mock Simulation
- **Phase 3**: PumpkinController with mock GridManager

### UI Testable (requires Unity)
- **Phase 5-6**: Window docking, search, tooltip positioning
- **Phase 7**: Save/load round-trip
- **Phase 8**: VFX pooling

### Priority Test Targets
1. Python interpreter correctness (Tokenizer → Parser → Execution)
2. Scope variable resolution and constant evaluation
3. Farm growth calculations and yield formulas
4. ItemBlock arithmetic and serialization round-trip
5. Save/load backward compatibility

---

## Project-Specific Notes

### Tags Found in Source
From TagManager.json (via stub): Standard Unity tags only

### Layers Found in Source
Standard Unity layers

### Project-Specific Enums
| Enum | Values | Used By |
|------|--------|---------|
| `SideEffect` | 39 values | Execution dispatch |
| `TokenType` | 40 values | Lexer/Parser |
| `GridDirection` | N/E/S/W (4) | All grid operations |
| `SoundEffectType` | 20 values | Audio system |
| `VFXType` | 9 values | VFX system |
| `LeaderboardType` | 4 values | Leaderboard categorization |
| `MultiUnlockDescrMode` | 5 values | Unlock UI display |
| `OptionValueType` | 4 values | Settings type system |

### Key Game Mechanics
1. **Python interpreter**: Custom tokenizer → parser → AST → execution with 49 builtin functions
2. **Grid farming**: 2D wrapped grid with crops, maze generation, dinosaur snake game
3. **Drone system**: Multiple drones executing code in parallel with priority queue scheduling
4. **Unlock tree**: Research progression unlocking keywords, features, farm sizes
5. **Leaderboard**: Timed farming runs with seed-based deterministic simulation
6. **Hat cosmetics**: 20+ hats with gameplay effects (DinosaurHat spawns snake game)
7. **Multi-threading**: Background sim thread for continuous execution

### Utility Extensions
- `GridDirectionMethods` — Vector2Int conversion, rotation, angle
- `RectExtensions` — Intersection, Area
- `Helper` — Number formatting, rich-text stripping, SHA256
- `CodeUtilities` — Syntax highlighting, error formatting, localized names

# PhaseMap — fwr (The Farmer Was Replaced)

## Phase Overview

| Phase | Name | Files | Weight % | Difficulty | Depends On |
|-------|------|-------|----------|------------|------------|
| 0 | Foundation Types & Data | 42 | 12% | ★★☆☆☆ | — |
| 1 | Python Type System | 23 | 10% | ★★★☆☆ | Phase 0 |
| 2 | Interpreter Core | 32 | 22% | ★★★★★ | Phase 0, 1 |
| 3 | Farm Simulation | 22 | 18% | ★★★★☆ | Phase 0, 1 |

**Total: ~200 game code files**

## Phase 0 — Foundation Types & Data (42 files)

### Purpose
Pure data types, interfaces, enums, ScriptableObjects, and utility classes with zero game logic. Everything else builds on these.

### File List

**Enums & Constants**
- `GridDirection.cs` — N/E/S/W cardinal enum
- `GridDirectionMethods.cs` — extension methods (vector, rotate, reverse)
- `SoundEffectType.cs` — 20 SFX type enum
- `VFXType.cs` — 9 VFX type enum
- `TokenType.cs` — 40 lexer token types
- `SideEffect.cs` — 39 side-effect action enum
- `LeaderboardType.cs` — none/simulation/reset/farm_resources
- `MultiUnlockDescrMode.cs` — unlock description mode enum
- `OptionValueType.cs` — Unknown/String/Float/KeyCombination
- `ModuleState.cs` — per-module interpreter state container

**Data Structures**
- `Duration.cs` — nanosecond-precision time struct
- `ItemBlock.cs` — double-array inventory container
- `Deque.cs` — generic circular-buffer double-ended queue
- `RangeSet.cs` — non-overlapping integer interval set
- `Pair.cs` — generic key-value pair
- `SerializableItem.cs` — serializable name+double pair
- `SFO.cs` — serialized farm object position+data
- `Token.cs` — lexer token (type, value, startIndex)
- `VFXCall.cs` — VFX request struct
- `KeyCombination.cs` — KeyCode + modifier struct
- `TooltipInfo.cs` — tooltip display data
- `LeaderboardEntryData.cs` — player name + score + rank
- `BoxedNodeParams.cs` — shared AST node params container
- `StringIds.cs` — global item name↔id registry (static)
- `SaveGame.cs` — save data format
- `OldSaveGame.cs` — legacy save data format

**Interfaces**
- `IPyObject.cs` — root Py type interface
- `IPySequence.cs` — ordered sequence interface
- `IPyIndexable.cs` — index/slice access interface
- `IPyNameSpace.cs` — attribute lookup interface
- `ITooltipHandler.cs` — tooltip provider interface
- `IVisualEffect.cs` — VFX play/color/text interface

**ScriptableObjects (Data Assets)**
- `FarmObjectSO.cs` — farm entity definitions
- `ItemSO.cs` — item definitions
- `UnlockSO.cs` — research tree node data
- `HatSO.cs` — cosmetic hat data
- `LeaderboardSO.cs` — leaderboard config
- `DroneSO.cs` — drone animation/audio data
- `TradeSO.cs` — trade/recipe data
- `AchievementSO.cs` — achievement display data
- `OptionSO.cs` — settings option base
- `SoundReferencesSO.cs` — FMOD event references
- `ColorTheme.cs` — UI color theme asset

### What It Looks Like When Running
Nothing visible — these are data definitions and pure types. They compile but produce no behavior on their own.

---

## Phase 1 — Python Type System (23 files)

### Purpose
Complete runtime type system for the embedded Python-like language. All Py* types, collections, enumerators, and control flow exceptions.

### File List
- `PyNumber.cs` — double wrapper
- `PyBool.cs` — boolean as 0/1 (extends PyNumber)
- `PyString.cs` — string as char-sequence
- `PyList.cs` — mutable list
- `PyDict.cs` — dictionary
- `PySet.cs` — hash set
- `PyTuple.cs` — immutable tuple
- `PyRange.cs` — lazy numeric range
- `PyNone.cs` — null sentinel (singleton)
- `PyModule.cs` — named attribute namespace
- `PyConstBag.cs` — read-only constant namespace
- `PyObjectBox.cs` — mutable value wrapper
- `PyDroneHandle.cs` — drone entity reference
- `PyGridDirection.cs` — GridDirection enum wrapper
- `PyFunction.cs` — function object (AST or native)
- `PyCollectionEnumerator.cs` — safe collection enumerator
- `PyUnassigned.cs` — unassigned variable sentinel
- `InternalPySequence.cs` — internal arg wrapper
- `ExecuteException.cs` — runtime error with source range
- `BreakStatement.cs` — break control flow exception
- `ContinueStatement.cs` — continue control flow exception
- `ReturnStatement.cs` — return control flow exception
- `ParseException.cs` — parser error with source range

### What It Looks Like When Running
Still invisible — these are runtime representations of Python values. They support equality, deep copy, iteration, indexing, and string conversion.

---

## Phase 2 — Interpreter Core (32 files)

### Purpose
Complete Python-like language interpreter: tokenizer, parser, AST nodes, scope management. Can parse and build syntax trees but cannot execute game actions (those require Phase 4).

### File List

**Tokenizer**
- `Tokenizer.cs` — static lexer, produces TokenStream
- `TokenStream.cs` — indexed token list with consume/peek
- `Token.cs` (Phase 0)

**Parser**
- `Parser.cs` — recursive-descent parser, operator precedence

**AST Nodes**
- `Node.cs` — abstract base with Execute(), CheckDependencies(), DeepCopy()
- `BinaryExprNode.cs` — binary operators (+, -, *, /, etc.)
- `ComparisonNode.cs` — comparison/membership (==, <, in, etc.)
- `UnaryExprNode.cs` — unary operators (not, +, -)
- `AssignmentNode.cs` — assignment with destructuring
- `ValueNode.cs` — variable lookup
- `LiteralNode.cs` — constant value
- `CallNode.cs` — function call dispatch
- `FunctionNode.cs` — function execution with scope push
- `DefNode.cs` — function definition (def statement)
- `BranchNode.cs` — if/elif/else branching
- `ForNode.cs` — for-loop over iterables
- `ImportNode.cs` — module import
- `SequenceNode.cs` — sequential expression evaluation
- `ListNode.cs` — list literal [...]
- `SetNode.cs` — set literal {...}
- `DictNode.cs` — dict literal {k:v, ...}
- `TupleNode.cs` — tuple literal (a, b, ...)
- `BracketNode.cs` — parenthesized expression
- `ReturnNode.cs` — return statement
- `BreakNode.cs` — break statement
- `ContinueNode.cs` — continue statement
- `PassNode.cs` — pass (no-op)
- `NoOpNode.cs` — empty node

**Runtime State**
- `Scope.cs` — variable scope with eval/const support
- `ProgramState.cs` — per-execution stack, op counting, drone handle
- `Program.cs` — parsed AST container (tree, vars, modules)
- `BuiltinFunctions.cs` — 49 builtin functions + 5 methods registry

### What It Looks Like When Running
Can tokenize source code, parse into AST, and execute pure expressions (math, string ops, list comprehensions). But game-side effects (harvest, plant, move) return placeholder values — they require the simulation bridge.

---

## Phase 3 — Farm Simulation (22 files)

### Purpose
Grid-based farm world: entities, growth timers, item economy, drone movement, unlocks, research tree. Runs independently of the interpreter for testing.

### File List

**Core Simulation**
- `Simulation.cs` — simulation tick orchestrator, timer management
- `Farm.cs` — farm state: drones, items, unlocks, keyword tracking
- `GridManager.cs` — 2D grid of entities/grounds, water decay, world resize
- `Drone.cs` — drone entity: movement, actions, animation state
- `PumpkinController.cs` — pumpkin merging logic

**Farm Objects (Entities)**
- `FarmObject.cs` — base entity class with animation, yield, harvest
- `Growable.cs` — base growing crop with fertilizer, companion bonus
- `Cactus.cs` — cactus growth stages, neighbor-aware
- `Sunflower.cs` — numbered flower, 8× yield if highest among ≥10
- `Pumpkin.cs` — pumpkin with death chance, merging into giants
- `TreePlant.cs` — tree, slower per adjacent tree
- `Apple.cs` — snake-game apple
- `BushPlant.cs` — maze generator using DFS
- `HedgePlant.cs` — maze wall with directional walls
- `Treasure.cs` — maze reward, repositions
- `Dinosaur.cs` — snake-game segment
- `DeadPumpkin.cs` — non-harvestable dead pumpkin
- `Ground.cs` — base ground type
- `Soil.cs` — ground with water-dependent mesh

**Hats**
- `Hat.cs` — base hat with OnMove/OnEquip/OnUnequip
- `DinosaurHat.cs` — snake-game hat, spawns dinosaur segments

### What It Looks Like When Running
A grid world populates with grass/soil, drones can be positioned, crops can be planted and grown via timer ticks, items can be collected. No code execution yet — just the simulation sandbox.

---

## Phase 4 — Game Bridge (Execution ↔ Simulation) (5 files)

### Purpose
Connects the interpreter to the simulation. Contains the main game loop, side effect dispatch, and the central singleton that orchestrates everything.

### File List
- `Execution.cs` — execution loop, op budgeting, side effect dispatch (30+ cases)
- `MainSim.cs` — **SINGLETON** hub: sim thread, leaderboard orchestration, UI event coordination
- `Achievements.cs` — Steam stats/achievements, golden hat unlocks
- `ResourceManager.cs` — SO registry loader (all game data)
- `Logger.cs` — output log buffer for in-game print()

### What It Looks Like When Running
**The full game loop**: Player code executes on background thread → side effects are dispatched → farm state changes → items collected → achievements tracked → UI updated on main thread. Leaderboard runs can be triggered. This is where the entire game comes alive.

---

Workspace system, code editor, documentation viewer, tooltip system, options UI, theme management. The "IDE" portion of the game.

**Workspace & Windows**

**Tooltip System**

- `KeyBindOptionSO.cs` + `KeyBindOptionUI.cs` — key binding

**Theme & Localization**
- `ThemeManager.cs` — theme hot-reload with FileSystemWatcher
- `Localizer.cs` — file-based localization

### What It Looks Like When Running
A functional code IDE: multiple code editor windows that can be dragged/docked/minimized, syntax highlighting, autocomplete, breakpoints, documentation browser, search, options menu, theme switching. Everything except actual code execution.
