<!-- ==== FILE: LEARN/noimnot/SystemPortabilityMap.md ==== -->
# SystemPortabilityMap — noimnot

## Classification

- **L0** — Project-specific. Cannot be reused without significant modification.
- **L1+** — Portable/generic. Could be extracted as a reusable library or shared across projects.

---

## Per-System Classification

| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| **_-CoreServices** | L1+ | Generic updater, view provider factory, DI installers — reusable pattern |
| **_-DataSystem** | L1+ | IDataStorage abstraction, ASavableData pattern, AesCrypter — fully generic |
| **_-SaveDataSystem** | L0 | All save data classes are noimnot-specific (RoomsSaveData, CatSaveData, etc.) |
| **_-SoundSystem** | L1+ | Sound service, source management, music cycling — generic audio framework |
| **_-SettingsSystem** | L1+ | Settings manager pattern with ASettingsInstance/ASettingsData — reusable |
| **_-ArabicSupportSystem** | L1+ | RTL text processing — standalone, project-independent |
| **_-ControlsViewerSystem** | L1+ | Gamepad/keyboard control display — generic input visualization |
| **_-PlayerSystem** | L0 | noimnot-specific player controller, footstep logic, movement model |
| **_-WatcherSystem** | L0 | EWatcherState states are game-specific (InDialog, InCloseup, etc.) |
| **_-CursorSystem** | L1+ | Cursor controller with cause-based locking — generic pattern |
| **_-MarkerSystem** | L0 | Markers are scene-specific UI anchor points |
| **_-RoomsSystem** | L0 | 7 specific room types, room object views — deeply game-specific |
| **_-WindowsSystem** | L0 | Window views showing 13-day progression — game-specific |
| **_-TriggerObjectsSystem** | L1+ | Abstract trigger zone pattern — reusable with different trigger types |
| **_-RaycastSystem** | L1+ | Generic 2D/UI raycast interaction system |
| **_-CharacterSystem** | L0 | Character types, emotion sprites, visit tracking — game-specific |
| **_-DialogSystem** | L0 | 55+ game-specific events, Yarn integration tailored to noimnot narrative |
| **_-CloseUpsSystem** | L0 | Phone, radio, fridge — all game-specific interactive objects |
| **_-ConsumablesSystem** | L0 | Beer, cigarettes, kombucha, mushroom — game-specific items |
| **_-NotepadSystem** | L1+ | Generic notepad controller pattern |
| **_-EventsSystem** | L0 | Game-specific events (CharacterDingDong, GrowingBelly) |
| **_-DayNightSystem** | L1+ | Day/night cycle controller — reusable with different configurations |
| **_-DreamSystem** | L0 | Mushroom dream sequences — game-specific |
| **_-EffectsSystem** | L1+ | Effects controller with fog data — generic visual effects framework |
| **_-CatSystem** | L0 | Cat AI, positions, animations — game-specific pet system |
| **_-BalancerSystem** | L1+ | Generic float/color/random balance value system — fully reusable |
| **_-EndingsSystem** | L0 | 13 game-specific ending paths |
| **_-CutscenesSystem** | L1+ | Cutscene data provider pattern — reusable with different content |
| **_-HUDSystem** | L0 | Game-specific HUD with raycast hint icons |
| **_-MainMenuSystem** | L0 | Game-specific main menu with face animation |
| **_-PauseSystem** | L1+ | Generic pause controller with mock implementation |
| **_-TitlesSystem** | L1+ | Generic title fade/scroll system |
| **_-SteamSystem** | L1+ | Steam manager, achievements, cloud save — reusable Steam wrapper |
| **SPACE_UTIL** | L1+ | Pure C# utilities — fully reusable |

---

## Summary

| Level | Count | Percentage |
|-------|-------|------------|
| **L0 (Project-specific)** | 18 systems | 53% |
| **L1+ (Portable)** | 16 systems | 47% |

### Most Portable Systems (extract first)
1. `SPACE_UTIL` — zero dependencies, pure C#
2. `_-DataSystem` — generic persistence framework
3. `_-SoundSystem` — generic audio pipeline
4. `_-SettingsSystem` — generic settings pattern
5. `_-ArabicSupportSystem` — standalone text processing
6. `_-BalancerSystem` — generic balance values
7. `_-CursorSystem` — generic cursor management
8. `_-RaycastSystem` — generic interaction detection
9. `_-SteamSystem` — generic Steam integration
10. `_-PauseSystem` — generic pause/resume

<!-- ==== FILE: LEARN/noimnot/surfer.md ==== -->
# surfer — noimnot

## Prompt 1: Initial source analysis

**Date:** 2025-05-16

### What was done
- Verified `MAIN-SOURCE/noimnot/` exists with `Assemblies/` and `Scripts/` folders
- Read `MAIN-SOURCE/entire-noimnot.stub` — 15,214 files, 1.471 GB total project
- Identified Assembly-CSharp as main game code (585 .cs files, all decompiled from 519.5 KB DLL)
- Read all 585 .cs files and extracted complete class inventory
- Mapped full dependency graph across 14 domains
- Identified 4 singletons, 55+ dialog events, 150+ interfaces, 40+ enums

### Documents generated
1. `ARCHITECTURE.md` — Source overview, dependency graph, god objects, singletons, coupling hotspots, event system, data flow, inheritance chains, external packages, asset inventory
2. `PhaseMap.md` — 14 phases (0–13) with file lists, difficulty ratings, weight percentages, cross-phase modification table
3. `StructureMap.md` — Per-phase system folders, DataService candidates, interface candidates, SO_/Field_/W prefix assignments
4. `GOAL.md` — Architecture rules, folder structure, naming conventions, class responsibilities, decoupling patterns, lifecycle, testing strategy, project-specific enums
5. `Estimate.md` — 406 total hours across 14 phases, complexity tier methodology
6. `SystemPortabilityMap.md` — 18 L0 systems (53%), 16 L1+ systems (47%)
7. `surfer.md` — This file

### Key findings
- Game is an interactive horror visual novel ("Not I'm Not" / "Fake People")
- Zenject DI + YarnSpinner dialogue engine + Steamworks.NET
- Dialog system is the heaviest coupling point (55+ events in IDialogManager)
- Well-architected with interface-driven communication and provider pattern
- Very few singletons — DI used properly throughout
- Arabic RTL support deeply integrated
- 13 unique ending paths
- Source is decompiled — variable names and comments lost

<!-- ==== FILE: LEARN/npcfr/ARCHITECTURE.md ==== -->
# ARCHITECTURE — npcfr

## Source Overview

| Metric | Value |
|--------|-------|
| **Project** | npcfr (NPC Factory / People-Playground-style sandbox) |
| **Engine** | Unity 6+ (URP), C#, IL2CPP build |
| **Source Origin** | ILSpy decompilation from `Assembly-CSharp.dll` |
| **Obfuscation** | Heavy — most class/method names are 2–3 letter codes |
| **Total .cs files (game code)** | ~800+ in `Assembly-CSharp/` |
| **Named folders** | 21 (retain original structure) |
| **Obfuscated root files** | ~650+ (single/double-letter `.cs` files) |
| **Total stub entries** | 9,750 files / 110.92 MB |
| **DI Framework** | Zenject (53 `[Inject]` points, 33 Installer files) |

### Folder Structure (Assembly-CSharp)

```
Assembly-CSharp/
├── ActiveRagdoll/          (9)  — physics-based character controller & muscles
├── Audio/                  (3)  — ambient audio, single-shot sources
├── BloodSplatters/         (1)  — particle emitter for blood decals
├── Components/             (9)  — reusable MonoBehaviours (particles, audio, rigidbodies)
├── Core/                   (3)  — MeshData handler
├── Data/                   (11) — ScriptableObjects (icons, player inventory, camera shake)
├── Effectors/              (5)  — LVA effector system
├── Infrastructure/         (63) — Zenject installers, scene services, project services
│   ├── Project/            (42) — project-level DI (registrations, prefabs, SFX handlers)
│   └── Scenes/             (21) — scene-level DI (toolbar, camera, inputs, UI, creatures)
├── Kinemation/             (16) — recoil animation, spring systems, camera shake
├── LVA/                    (54) — Living Virtual Agents (creatures, limbs, organs, puppeteers)
│   ├── Core/               (2)  — enums (LVAEffectorFeedbackType)
│   ├── Creatures/           (3)  — abstract Creature<TNode>, implementations
│   ├── Limbs/              (23) — AbstractLimb, LimbPhysics, LimbDismemberment, variants
│   ├── Organs/             (4)  — organ system
│   ├── Puppeteers/         (17) — HumanoidPuppeteer, IK, bone mapping, move control
│   └── NodesHierarchy/     (2)  — node graph
├── Map/                    (3)  — Spinner environment objects
├── Player/                 (33) — player controller
│   ├── Appearances/        (11) — God mode appearance, camera, body physics
│   ├── Cam/                (3)  — camera shake service
│   ├── Control/            (3)  — player control logic
│   ├── GameplayInput/      (5)  — button actions, mouse/keyboard input
│   ├── GodInventoryItems/  (4)  — HumanSpawnerGII, Glock17GII
│   └── Toolbar/            (5)  — toolbar model, service, populator
├── QuickOutline/           (2)  — mesh outline effect
├── Spawnables/             (11) — runtime-spawned objects
│   ├── Bullets/            (3)  — PistolBullet, Shell
│   ├── Misc/               (3)  — HumanSpawner
│   └── Weapons/            (5)  — Glock17, muzzle particles, shell ejection
├── Sugar/                  (1)  — syntactic sugar helpers
├── TEST/                   (4)  — test scripts
├── Tests/                  (5)  — unit/performance tests
├── TripledoseLibs/         (9)  — internal library (collections, infrastructure)
├── VFX/                    (4)  — blood drain, blood loss particles
├── Views/                  (27) — UI layer
│   ├── ContextMenu/        (6)  — radial/context menu
│   ├── Generic/            (7)  — PopupWindow, base view classes
│   ├── Hints/              (3)  — hint bar (MK variant)
│   ├── Pause/              (5)  — pause menu
│   └── Toolbar/            (5)  — toolbar UI slots
├── VoxelMeshGeneration/    (15) — voxel body mesh system
│   ├── Chunks/             (1)  — VoxelMeshChunkData
│   ├── DataBuilding/       (3)  — VoxelMeshData builder
│   ├── Separation/         (2)  — mesh separation (dismemberment)
│   ├── Tools/              (3)  — morphs
│   └── Tests/              (2)  — voxel tests
└── [~650 obfuscated .cs files at root]
```

## Dependency Graph

### Core Hierarchy (deobfuscated role names)

```
bgb (MonoBehaviour base — unknown original name)
 └── g  (Lifecycle managed entity — Awake/Start/Enable/Disable/Destroy events)
      └── bcx  (Parameterized entity — parameters, behaviors, effectors, external params)
           └── bcz<TParam, TBehavior>  (Generic creature component)
                ├── AbstractLimb  (via bcz<zq, AbstractLimb.wv>)
                └── [other creature parts]
```

### Domain Dependencies

| From | To | Nature |
|------|----|--------|
| **LVA.Creatures** | `bam`, `bcx`, `vf`, `wk`, `bim`, Zenject | Creature base → entity system |
| **LVA.Limbs** | `bcz`, `zq`, `VoxelMesh`, `SeparatedMeshData`, `LimbPhysics` | Limb → voxel body, physics |
| **LVA.Puppeteers** | `bml`, `bmb`, `IKReferences`, `HumanoidPuppeteerStaticData` | Humanoid IK, bone mapping |
| **VoxelMeshGeneration** | Unity.Burst, Unity.Collections, Unity.Mathematics | High-perf voxel processing |
| **Player** | `jg` (InputActions), Zenject, Views, Spawnables | Input → toolbar → inventory → spawn |
| **Infrastructure** | Zenject.MonoInstaller, all domain services | DI wiring |
| **Views** | Zenject, Data SOs | UI binds via DI, reads data |
| **Spawnables** | Zenject, LVA, VFX, Components | Weapons/bullets depend on creature system |
| **Kinemation** | Unity.Mathematics, MonoBehaviour | Standalone recoil/spring system |
| **ActiveRagdoll** | MonoBehaviour, Physics | Standalone physics controller |

### Key Obfuscated Class Roles

| Class | Lines | Role |
|-------|-------|------|
| `fo` | 1420 | **Utility god-class** — math, coroutines, timers, collection helpers |
| `fp` | 336 | **Extension methods** — float/Vector/Quaternion/NativeContainer extensions |
| `bcx` | 940 | **Entity base** — parameters, behaviors, effectors (LVA entity framework) |
| `g` | 231 | **Lifecycle entity** — Awake/Start/OnEnable/OnDisable/OnDestroy wrapper |
| `jg` | 381 | **Input action map** — Player + UI actions (Unity Input System) |
| `dm` | 367 | **VoxelMesh separator** — processes voxel separation for dismemberment |
| `yh` | 334 | **Limb damage handler** — voxel-level limb destruction logic |
| `rd` | 371 | **IK height controller** — humanoid pose/height transitions |
| `cn` | 198 | **Voxel flood-fill** — separation algorithms |
| `ir` | 363 | **Perf test** — hash set benchmark MonoBehaviour |
| `bam` | ~unknown | **Creature MonoBehaviour** — base for Creature<TNode> |

|------|-------|------------------|
| `fo.cs` | 1420 | Math utils, coroutine helpers, timer system, collection ops, audio helpers, particle control, easing |
| `bcx.cs` | 940 | Entity parameters, behavior management, effector signals, external params, lifecycle |
| `fp.cs` | 336 | Float extensions, Vector extensions, Quaternion extensions, NativeContainer extensions, list shuffling |
| `VoxelMesh.cs` | 561 | Voxel data, chunk management, mesh building (Burst), morph application, event dispatch |
| `jg.cs` | 381 | Player input actions, UI input actions, control scheme management |
| `dm.cs` | 367 | Separation coroutines, mesh data filtering, chunk coordinate tracking |
| `yh.cs` | 334 | Damage detection, voxel weight tracking, limb separation events, physics integration |

## Singleton Registry

| Location | Pattern | What It Owns |
|----------|---------|--------------|
| `l.cs` | `static Instance` | Unknown (single singleton in entire codebase) |

**Note:** This project is remarkably singleton-free. All service access goes through Zenject `[Inject]`.

## Coupling Hotspots

### FindObjectOfType
**None found.** Clean DI architecture.

### Zenject [Inject] Points (53 total)
Heavy users:
- **Infrastructure installers** (21 files) — scene/project wiring
- **LVA domain** (7 files) — Creature, AbstractLimb, LimbPhysics, Puppeteers
- **Player domain** (7 files) — Appearances, Camera, Toolbar, GodInventoryItems
- **Spawnables** (6 files) — Glock17, PistolBullet, HumanSpawner
- **Views** (6 files) — ContextMenu, Hints, Pause, Toolbar views

### Static Instance Access
Only 1 file (`l.cs`) uses static Instance pattern.

### Cross-Domain Direct References
- **Spawnables → LVA**: Weapons reference creature damage system
- **Player → Spawnables**: Toolbar/GodInventory items reference spawnable prefabs
- **Views → Player**: Toolbar views bind to toolbar service
- **VoxelMeshGeneration → LVA.Limbs**: AbstractLimb uses SeparatedMeshData

---

## Event System

### Patterns Used
1. **C# `Action` / `Action<T>`** — Primary pattern (324 matches across 120 files)
2. **`event Action<T>`** — Standard C# event accessors on entity lifecycle (`g.cs`: pcl/pcm/pcn/pco/pcp events)
3. **No UnityEvent usage detected** in game code
4. **No custom event bus** — direct subscription model

### Key Event Chains
- `g` entity lifecycle → `Action<g>` events (created, started, enabled, disabled, destroyed)
- `VoxelMesh` → `Action<hz<int3, Voxel>>` voxel change events
- `VoxelMesh` → `Action<el>` chunk update events
- `bcx` entity → `Action sql` parameter change event
- Limb system → separation/destruction callbacks

---

## Data Flow

```
ScriptableObjects (SO) → SerializedData
    ├── SerializedIconData
    ├── SerializedObjectDescriptor
    ├── SerializedGodInventoryCategoryData
    ├── SerializedGIIRegistrationData
    ├── FPSCameraShake
    ├── RecoilAnimData
    └── ButtonActionData

Registration Installers → Zenject Bindings
    ├── RegistrationsInstaller (prefabs, mods)
    ├── GodInventoryItemsRegistrationInstaller
    ├── LVAEntitiesRegistrationInstaller
    ├── SpawnablesRegistrationInstaller
    └── ParticlesRegistrationInstaller

Scene Installers → Runtime Services
    ├── CoreSceneServicesInstaller
    ├── PlayerInputsInstaller
    ├── ButtonsActionsInstaller
    ├── ToolbarInstaller
    ├── CameraServiceInstaller
    └── SandboxUIInstaller

Runtime: Service → MonoBehaviour → Events
    Player Input (jg) → Player Control → Toolbar → GodInventoryItem → Spawnable
    Creature (bam) → Limbs (AbstractLimb) → VoxelMesh → Separation → Physics
```

---

## Inheritance Chains

### Entity System (preserve)
```
bgb → g → bcx → bcz<TParam, TBehavior> → AbstractLimb / Creature<TNode>
```

### Limb Behaviors (preserve)
```
bcx.bcw (abstract behavior) → AbstractLimb.wv → concrete limb behaviors (yh, vm<yi>, etc.)
```

### Installer Hierarchy (preserve)
```
MonoInstaller → cjj → RegistrationsInstaller, CoreSceneServicesInstaller, etc.
```

### Worth Flattening
- `fo.cs` / `fp.cs` — utility classes should be split by domain (math, collections, audio, particles)
- Obfuscated single-letter classes with <50 lines — many are tiny enums, structs, or delegates that can be grouped

# Estimate — npcfr

## Hours per Phase

| # | Phase | Files | Complexity | Hours | Notes |
|---|-------|-------|------------|-------|-------|
| 1 | Core Utilities & Extensions | ~25 | Low | 6–8 | Split fo.cs god-object, rename all methods |
| 2 | Data Layer (SOs & Structs) | ~20 | Low | 4–6 | Straightforward data containers, rename fields |
| 3 | TripledoseLibs | ~9 | Low | 3–4 | Collection wrappers, preserve NativeContainer APIs |
| 4 | VoxelMesh Engine | ~25 | High | 18–24 | Burst jobs, NativeArray math, coroutine rebuilds |
| 5 | Entity Framework | ~80 | High | 24–32 | Deep abstract hierarchy, 80+ obfuscated files |
| 6 | LVA Core | ~60 | High | 20–28 | Creature/Limb graph, VoxelMesh integration |
| 7 | ActiveRagdoll & Puppeteers | ~30 | High | 14–18 | Physics, IK, bone mapping |
| 8 | Infrastructure & DI | ~65 | Medium | 12–16 | Zenject installers, service bindings |
| 9 | Player System | ~35 | Medium | 10–14 | Input, toolbar, appearances |
| 10 | Spawnables & Weapons | ~15 | Medium | 6–8 | Weapon logic, spawn pipeline |
| 11 | Views & UI | ~30 | Medium | 8–10 | UI controllers, context menu |
| 12 | Audio, VFX & Components | ~15 | Low | 4–6 | Standalone MonoBehaviours |
| 13 | Integration & Wiring | ~5 | Medium | 6–8 | Cross-phase testing, scene setup |
| | **TOTAL** | **~414** | | **135–182** | |

## Complexity Tiers

| Tier | Multiplier | Criteria |
|------|-----------|----------|
| **Low** | 0.25 hr/file | Data containers, enums, simple MonoBehaviours |
| **Medium** | 0.4 hr/file | Service logic, DI wiring, standard patterns |
| **High** | 0.6 hr/file | Burst jobs, physics, deep abstractions, NativeContainer management |

## Risk Factors

- **Obfuscation overhead**: +30% time for naming reconstruction across all phases
- **Entity framework (P5)**: Highest risk — 80+ files forming a complex abstract hierarchy. May need multiple passes.
- **VoxelMesh (P4)**: Burst-compiled code may have edge cases not visible in decompiled stubs
- **Cross-phase integration (P13)**: Zenject binding order and scene loading sequence

<!-- ==== FILE: LEARN/npcfr/GOAL.md ==== -->
# GOAL — npcfr

## Target Architecture Rules

### 1. Folder Structure

```
npcfr-reimpl/
├── _-Systems/           ← folders containing 3+ tightly coupled scripts
│   ├── VoxelMeshCore/
│   ├── EntityCore/
│   ├── LimbSystem/
│   ├── etc.
├── DataServices/        ← pure C# classes (no MonoBehaviour) with extractable logic
├── Interfaces/          ← cross-system communication contracts
├── SO_/                 ← ScriptableObject assets
├── Field_/              ← serializable data structs
├── W_/                  ← runtime wrappers around SO_ data
├── Enums/
├── Tests/
└── [Phase folders as needed]
```

### 2. Naming Conventions

| Element | Convention | Example |
|---------|-----------|---------|
| ScriptableObject | `SO_` prefix | `SO_IconData` |
| Data struct | `Field_` prefix | `Field_Voxel`, `Field_SpringData` |
| Runtime wrapper | `W_` prefix | `W_ToolbarSlot` |
| Interface | `I_` prefix | `I_Creature`, `I_Limb` |
| System folder | `_-Systems/[Name]/` | `_-Systems/VoxelMeshCore/` |
| Service (pure C#) | `[Name]DataService` | `LimbDamageDataService` |
| MonoBehaviour | PascalCase, no prefix | `VoxelMesh`, `AbstractLimb` |
| Enum | PascalCase | `LVAEffectorFeedbackType`, `TimerTimeType` |

### 3. Class Responsibilities

- **MonoBehaviour**: Only Unity lifecycle + serialized references. Delegates logic to DataServices.
- **DataService**: Pure C# class. Testable without Unity. Receives data, returns results.
- **ScriptableObject**: Immutable configuration. Never mutated at runtime.
- **Wrapper (W_)**: Mutable runtime copy of SO_ data. Owned by a single manager.
- **Interface**: Defines communication contract between systems. Never concrete class references across system boundaries.

### 4. Decoupling Patterns

#### Cross-System Communication
- Systems communicate **only** through interfaces
- No direct class references across `_-Systems/` folder boundaries
- Zenject binds interfaces to implementations in Installers

#### Event Pattern
- Use `Action` / `Action<T>` for events (matches source style)
- Event owners declare events; subscribers inject the owning interface
- No global event bus — direct injection only

#### Dependency Direction
- Each phase depends only on earlier phases (see PhaseMap)
- No circular dependencies between `_-Systems/` folders
- Utility code (P1) has zero dependencies

### 5. Lifecycle Management

- **Entity lifecycle** preserved: `bgb → g → bcx → bcz → concrete`
- Virtual hooks: `cxh/cxi/cxj/cxk/cxl` (Init/Start/Enable/Disable/Destroy)
- Behavior system: `bcw.gsu()` (Init), `bcw.gqo()` (Tick), `bcw.hls()` (Cleanup)
- Zenject `[Inject]` for constructor injection on MonoBehaviours

### 6. C# Features

- **Burst-compatible structs** for VoxelMesh (Voxels, Voxel) — must remain blittable
- **NativeArray/NativeHashSet/NativeList** for voxel operations — must manage allocation/disposal
- **IEquatable<T>** on value types used in NativeContainers
- **IteratorStateMachine (coroutines)** for async mesh operations
- **Extension methods** in dedicated static classes (fp.cs pattern)
- **Generics** on entity framework (bcz<TParam, TBehavior>)

### 7. Project-Specific Details

| Item | Value |
|------|-------|
| **Project Name** | npcfr |
| **Phase Count** | 13 |
| **DI Framework** | Zenject |
| **Render Pipeline** | URP (Universal Render Pipeline) |
| **Physics** | 3D Physics (Rigidbody, Collider, PhysicsMaterial) |
| **Input** | Unity Input System (New) via `jg` wrapper |
| **Custom Shaders** | TripledosePixelShader, NoiseHologram, Liquid, VHSUI |
| **Key Plugin** | Amazing Assets Advanced Dissolve (limb separation VFX) |

### 8. Tags & Layers (from source)

#### Physics Materials Found
- Default, DefaultFriction, FZeroFriction
- SlidePhysicMaterial, SlipperyFloorPhysicMaterial
- SpinnerPhysicMaterial, TestDumper

#### SFX Type Enums
- `ImpactSFXType` — bullet impacts, body hits, foot steps
- `ToolsSFXType` — tool use sounds
- `WeaponSFXType` — gun fire, casing
- `WhooshSFXType` — weapon aim whooshes

#### Input Actions (from jg.cs)
- **Player Map**: 16 actions (move, look, fire, aim, scroll, toolbar slots, pause, etc.)
- **UI Map**: 10 actions (navigate, submit, cancel, point, click, scroll, etc.)
- **Control Schemes**: 5 (likely Keyboard+Mouse, Gamepad, etc.)

### 9. Testing Strategy

- **Unit tests** for DataServices (pure C# — no Unity dependency)
- **Integration tests** for VoxelMesh operations (NativeContainer allocation)
- **Performance tests** already exist (`ir.cs` — hash set benchmarks, `VoxelMeshGeneration/Tests/`)
- **Phase validation**: each phase should compile and run independently up to its "What It Looks Like When Running" description
- **Regression**: preserve existing test infrastructure in `TEST/` and `Tests/`

### 10. Utility Extensions

#### SPACE_UTIL (from fo.cs) — Split Targets
| Category | Methods |
|----------|---------|
| **Math** | Approximately-equal (float, float3, Vector3), angle conversion, clamping, remapping |
| **Quaternion** | Pitch/yaw/roll extraction, clamped rotation, flatten |
| **Vector** | Flatten, signed angle, distance helpers |
| **Coroutine** | Timer (lerp + callback), delay, sequential coroutine runner |
| **Collection** | AddRange for HashSet/ICollection, NativeContainer dispose helpers |
| **Audio** | AudioSource play/stop helpers |
| **Particle** | ParticleSystem play/stop wrappers |
| **Transform** | Reset local/world, destroy children |
| **Easing** | DOTween Ease evaluation wrappers |
| **String** | Random string generation, string manipulation |

#### Extension Methods (from fp.cs) — Keep Grouped
- Float extensions (approximately, clamp, remap, ceil, floor, sign)
- Vector3/Vector3Int extensions (flatten, scale, approximately)
- Quaternion extensions (flatten, pitch extraction)
- NativeContainer extensions (dispose safety, set operations)
- List/Collection extensions (shuffle, insert-or-replace, find-with-index)
- Color extensions (to Vector3)
- ParticleSystem extensions (play/stop toggle)

## Phase 1 — Core Utilities & Extensions

### Files
- `fo.cs` — static utility class (math, coroutines, timers, collections, audio, particles)
- `fp.cs` — extension methods (float, Vector, Quaternion, NativeContainer, List)
- `cn.cs` — voxel flood-fill/separation static utilities
- Selected small obfuscated files: math helpers, enums, delegates (~20 files)

### What It Looks Like When Running
Nothing visible — pure utility code. All other phases depend on these helpers.

### Difficulty: Easy
Straightforward static methods. Obfuscation makes naming hard but logic is simple math/collection ops.

---

## Phase 2 — Data Layer (SOs & Structs)

### Files
- `Data/Icons/SerializedIconData.cs`
- `Data/Objects/SerializedObjectDescriptor.cs`
- `Data/Player/CameraShake/FPSCameraShake.cs`
- `Data/Player/Inventory/God/Categories/SerializedGodInventoryCategoryData.cs`
- `Data/Player/Inventory/God/Items/SerializedGIIRegistrationData.cs`
- `Data/CustomTypes/` (5 files)
- `Kinemation/Recoilly/Runtime/RecoilAnimData.cs`
- `Player/GameplayInput/ButtonsActions/ButtonActionData.cs`
- Selected obfuscated structs/enums: `bdb`, `bda`, `bbu`, `bcm`, `bcj`, `bdd`, `bjs`, etc.

### What It Looks Like When Running
No runtime behavior — these are data containers serialized in the Inspector.

### Difficulty: Easy
ScriptableObjects and plain structs. Deobfuscation naming is the only challenge.

---

## Phase 3 — TripledoseLibs (Internal Library)

### Files
- `TripledoseLibs/` (9 files)
- `TripledoseLibs/Collections/` — FastDictionary, NativeHashMapWrapper, ReadOnlyNativeHashSet
- `TripledoseLibs/Infrastructure/Setup/ProjectServicesInstaller.cs`
- Related obfuscated types: `ig<T>`, `hx<TKey,TValue>`, `hz<TKey,TValue>`, `em<T>`

### What It Looks Like When Running
Background data structures used by VoxelMesh and entity systems. No visible effect.

### Difficulty: Easy
Standard collection wrappers. Some use Unity.Collections Native types.

---

## Phase 4 — VoxelMesh Engine

### Files
- `VoxelMeshGeneration/VoxelMesh.cs` — core MonoBehaviour (Voxels struct, Voxel struct, chunk management)
- `VoxelMeshGeneration/RGBAtlasColor.cs`
- `VoxelMeshGeneration/VoxelFaceNormalSbyte.cs`
- `VoxelMeshGeneration/VoxelFaceVerticesIndexes.cs`
- `VoxelMeshGeneration/Chunks/VoxelMeshChunkData.cs`
- `VoxelMeshGeneration/DataBuilding/` (3 files — VoxelMeshData builder)
- `VoxelMeshGeneration/Separation/` (2 files — separation module)
- `VoxelMeshGeneration/Tools/` (3 files — VoxelMorphData)
- `VoxelMeshGeneration/Tests/` (2 files)
- `dm.cs` — VoxelMesh separator coroutine handler
- Related obfuscated: `er`, `ej`, `ek`, `el`, `cr`, `cc`, `cq`, `dq`

### What It Looks Like When Running
Voxel meshes render as chunked 3D pixel bodies. Chunks rebuild dynamically when voxels are modified (shot, cut, separated). Separation creates independent physics objects from detached voxel groups.

### Difficulty: Hard
Burst-compiled jobs, NativeArray/NativeHashSet math, coroutine-based async mesh rebuilding. Core to the entire game.

---

## Phase 5 — Entity Framework (g / bcx / bcz)

### Files
- `bgb` base class
- `g.cs` — lifecycle entity (Awake/Start/OnEnable/OnDisable/OnDestroy wrapper with events)
- `bcx.cs` — parameterized entity (nested classes: bcn, bco, bcp, bcq, bcr, bcs, bct, bcv, bcw)
- `bcz` — generic entity component
- Interface files: `bca`, `bcb`, `bce`, `bcf`, `bcg`, `bci`, `bch`, `bcd`
- Parameter types: `bdb`, `bda`, `bbu`, `bcm`, `bcj`, `bdd`
- Behavior base: `bcx.bcw`
- ~60 additional obfuscated files forming the entity parameter/behavior/effector framework

### What It Looks Like When Running
Invisible framework. Manages entity lifecycle, parameter binding, behavior execution, and effector signal routing.

### Difficulty: Hard
Deep abstract hierarchy, heavily obfuscated. Generic type constraints, dictionary-based parameter tracking, nested class architecture.

---

## Phase 6 — LVA Core (Creatures, Limbs, Organs)

### Files
- `LVA/Core/LVAEffectorFeedbackType.cs`
- `LVA/Core/` (2 files)
- `LVA/Creatures/Creature.cs` — abstract `Creature<TNode> : bam`
- `LVA/Creatures/Implementations/AutomaticCctvCamera.cs`
- `LVA/Limbs/AbstractLimb.cs` — base limb with nested `wv` behavior
- `LVA/Limbs/LimbPhysics.cs`
- `LVA/Limbs/LimbDismembermentModule.cs`
- `LVA/Limbs/References/LimbReferencesPrivate.cs`
- `LVA/Limbs/Variants/` (limb implementations)
- `LVA/Limbs/Systems/` (node systems)
- `LVA/Organs/` (4 files)
- `LVA/NodesHierarchy/` (2 files)
- `LVA/DebugTools/` (2 files)
- `LVA/TestCreatureInitializer.cs`
- `yh.cs` — limb damage/voxel handler
- `bam` — creature MonoBehaviour base
- Related obfuscated: `zq`, `zf`, `zk`, `vf`, `vd`, `vm<T>`, `ug`, `rx`, `bab`, `wx`, `wy`, `xc`, `ber`

### What It Looks Like When Running
Humanoid NPCs with voxel bodies. Each body part is a limb with its own VoxelMesh. Damage removes voxels, triggers gore VFX. When enough voxels are destroyed, limbs separate as independent physics objects. Limbs have physical joints and can be dismembered.

### Difficulty: Hard
Complex creature component graph. Limb ↔ VoxelMesh ↔ Physics interaction. Multiple abstract layers.

---

## Phase 7 — ActiveRagdoll & Puppeteers

### Files
- `ActiveRagdoll/Scripts/PuppetMaster.cs`
- `ActiveRagdoll/Scripts/LegacyCharacterController.cs`
- `ActiveRagdoll/Scripts/LegacyMuscle.cs`
- `ActiveRagdoll/Scripts/Pelvis.cs`
- `ActiveRagdoll/Scripts/FootFrictionControl.cs`
- `ActiveRagdoll/Scripts/PhysicalBodyPart.cs`
- `ActiveRagdoll/Scripts/PuppetFollowCamera.cs`
- `ActiveRagdoll/Scripts/IgnoreCollision.cs`
- `ActiveRagdoll/Tools/TimeScaler.cs`
- `LVA/Puppeteers/Humanoid/` (all 17 files)
  - `HumanoidPuppeteerReferences.cs`
  - `HumanoidPuppeteerBoneMapHandler.cs`
  - `HumanoidPuppeteerStaticData.cs`
  - `HumanoidMoveControl.cs`
  - `COMTransformControl.cs`
  - `MeshEnableManagement.cs`
  - `HumanoidPuppeteerRuntimeData.cs`
  - `IKReferences.cs`
- `rd.cs` — IK height/pose controller
- `Kinemation/` (16 files — recoil, springs, camera shake)
- Related: `bml`, `bmb`, `HumanGroupHandler`

### What It Looks Like When Running
NPCs walk, stand, fall with active ragdoll physics. Muscles drive joints toward target poses. PuppetMaster orchestrates bone tracking. IK handles foot placement and height transitions.

### Difficulty: Hard
Physics-heavy, lots of Transform/Rigidbody manipulation, IK solving, bone mapping.

---

## Phase 8 — Infrastructure & DI

### Files
- `Infrastructure/Project/Installers/` (9 files)
  - `RegistrationsInstaller.cs`
  - `GodInventoryItemsRegistrationInstaller.cs`
  - `LVAEntitiesRegistrationInstaller.cs`
  - `SpawnablesRegistrationInstaller.cs`
  - `ParticlesRegistrationInstaller.cs`
  - SFX type enums (Impact, Tools, Weapon, Whoosh)
- `Infrastructure/Project/Registration/` (30 files)
  - `PrefabsRegistration.cs`
  - `AudioRegistrationInstaller.cs`
  - `UIRegistrationInstaller.cs`
- `Infrastructure/Project/Services/` (3 files — LoadingCurtain)
- `Infrastructure/Scenes/` (21 files)
  - `CoreSceneServicesInstaller.cs`
  - `ButtonsActionsInstaller.cs`
  - `CameraServiceInstaller.cs`
  - `PlayerInputsInstaller.cs`
  - `ToolbarInstaller.cs`
  - `MKButtonsActionsInstaller.cs`
  - `PlayerAppearanceInstaller.cs`
  - `ParticlesInstaller.cs`
  - Material converters (Dissolve, Liquid, LitOpaque, LitTransparent)
  - `Sandbox/Installers/` (scene-specific DI)
  - `Sandbox/Services/` (creatures, UI context menu)

### What It Looks Like When Running
Bootstrap scene loads → ProjectContext installs project-wide services → Sandbox scene loads → Scene installers wire creature services, UI, input. Loading curtain shows between scenes.

### Difficulty: Medium
Zenject wiring. Requires understanding of all services being bound.

---

## Phase 9 — Player System

### Files
- `Player/Control/` (3 files)
- `Player/GameplayInput/` (5 files — jg InputActions, ButtonActions, MKButtonActionData)
- `Player/GeneralInput/` (2 files)
- `Player/Appearances/God/` (11 files)

  - `HumanSpawnerGII.cs`
  - `Glock17GodInventoryItem.cs`
- `jg.cs` — Input action wrapper

### What It Looks Like When Running
First-person god-mode player. Free camera, toolbar at bottom with inventory items (human spawner, gun). Click to use active item. Camera shake on actions. Mouse/keyboard input mapped through Unity Input System.

### Difficulty: Medium
Input → action → toolbar → item pipeline. Zenject-injected services.

---

## Phase 10 — Spawnables & Weapons

### Files
- `Spawnables/Bullets/PistolBullet.cs`
- `Spawnables/Bullets/Shell.cs`
- `Spawnables/Misc/HumanSpawner.cs`

### What It Looks Like When Running
Player fires Glock17 → muzzle flash + smoke particles → bullet spawns with physics → bullet hits creature → voxel damage → blood VFX → shell casing ejects with physics.

Human spawner throws → spawn VFX → humanoid NPC appears with full ragdoll body.

### Difficulty: Medium
Particle systems, physics raycasts, Zenject factory injection.

Toolbar UI at bottom showing inventory slots with icons. Context menu on right-click for creature manipulation. Hint bar shows controls. Pause menu with settings. Loading curtain between scenes.

### Difficulty: Medium
Standard Unity UI with Zenject injection. Some custom window/popup architecture.

Ambient space atmosphere audio. Footstep sounds. Gore splat SFX on impacts. Blood particle trails from wounds. Muzzle flash particles. Spinner environment hazards.

Standalone MonoBehaviours with straightforward audio/particle logic.

### Files

- Final cross-phase integration testing

### What It Looks Like When Running
Full game: Bootstrap → Loading → Sandbox scene with terrain, NPC spawning, weapon use, voxel destruction, ragdoll physics, UI.

### Difficulty: Medium
Final wiring and testing across all phases.

---

## Cross-Phase Modification Table

| Phase | Modifies Earlier Phase | Nature |
|-------|----------------------|--------|
| P4 (VoxelMesh) | P3 (TripledoseLibs) | Uses ReadOnlyNativeHashSet, NativeHashMapWrapper |
| P5 (Entity) | P1 (Utils) | Entity lifecycle calls utility methods |
| P6 (LVA) | P4, P5 | Limbs own VoxelMesh instances, extend entity framework |
| P7 (Ragdoll) | P6 | Puppeteers reference limb/creature types |
| P8 (Infra) | P2, P5–P7 | Installers bind all domain types into Zenject |
| P9 (Player) | P8 | Player services injected via scene installers |
| P10 (Spawnables) | P6, P8, P9 | Weapons interact with creature damage via DI |
| P11 (Views) | P8, P9 | UI binds to toolbar/input services |
| P12 (Audio/VFX) | P8 | Audio services registered in DI |
| P13 (Integration) | All | Wiring verification |

<!-- ==== FILE: LEARN/npcfr/StructureMap.md ==== -->
# StructureMap — npcfr

## Naming Conventions

| Prefix | Meaning |
|--------|---------|
| `SO_` | ScriptableObject asset |
| `Field_` | Serializable data struct (no logic) |
| `W_` | Wrapper / runtime-mutable container around SO_ data |
| `I_` | Interface for cross-system communication |
| `_-Systems/` | Folder containing 3+ tightly coupled scripts |

---

## Phase 1 — Core Utilities & Extensions

### Structure
```
Phase01_CoreUtils/
├── SPACE_UTIL.cs              ← fo.cs (split from god-object)
│   Static math, coroutine, timer, easing helpers
├── SPACE_UTIL_Ext.cs          ← fp.cs
│   Extension methods (float, Vector, Quaternion, NativeContainer)
├── VoxelGridUtils.cs          ← cn.cs
│   Voxel flood-fill and separation static algorithms
└── Enums/
    ├── TimerTimeType.cs       ← from fo.cs nested enum
    └── [~15 small enum/delegate files from obfuscated root]
```

### DataService Candidates
- `fo.cs` → `MathService` (pure static, no extraction needed — just split)
- `fp.cs` → stays as extension methods class

### Interface Candidates
None — utility layer has no cross-system communication.

---

## Phase 2 — Data Layer

### Structure
```
Phase02_Data/
├── SO_IconData.cs                     ← SerializedIconData
├── SO_ObjectDescriptor.cs             ← SerializedObjectDescriptor
├── SO_GodInventoryCategory.cs         ← SerializedGodInventoryCategoryData
├── SO_GIIRegistration.cs              ← SerializedGIIRegistrationData
├── SO_FPSCameraShake.cs               ← FPSCameraShake
├── SO_RecoilAnimData.cs               ← RecoilAnimData
├── SO_ButtonActionData.cs             ← ButtonActionData
├── Field_MKButtonActionData.cs        ← MKButtonActionData
├── Field_ToolbarModelSlotData.cs      ← ToolbarModelSlotData
└── CustomTypes/
    └── [5 files from Data/CustomTypes/]
```

### Interface Candidates
None — pure data.

---

## Phase 3 — TripledoseLibs

### Structure
```
Phase03_TripledoseLibs/
├── Collections/
│   ├── FastDictionary.cs
│   ├── NativeHashMapWrapper.cs
│   ├── ReadOnlyNativeHashSet.cs
│   └── [related obfuscated: ig<T>, hx<K,V>, hz<K,V>, em<T>]
└── Infrastructure/
    └── ProjectServicesInstaller.cs
```

### DataService Candidates
All collection types are already pure C# — no extraction needed.

---

## Phase 4 — VoxelMesh Engine

### Structure
```
Phase04_VoxelMesh/
├── _-Systems/
│   └── VoxelMeshCore/               ← 3+ tightly coupled
│       ├── VoxelMesh.cs              ← VoxelMesh MonoBehaviour
│       ├── VoxelMeshData.cs          ← DataBuilding
│       ├── Field_Voxel.cs            ← VoxelMesh.Voxel struct
│       ├── Field_Voxels.cs           ← VoxelMesh.Voxels struct (Burst)
│       └── RGBAtlasColor.cs
├── _-Systems/
│   └── VoxelChunks/                  ← 3+ tightly coupled
│       ├── Field_VoxelMeshChunkData.cs
│       ├── ChunkRenderer.cs          ← ej (obfuscated)
│       └── ChunkBuilder.cs           ← er (obfuscated)
├── _-Systems/
│   └── VoxelSeparation/              ← 3+ tightly coupled
│       ├── VoxelMeshSeparationModule.cs
│       ├── Field_SeparatedMeshData.cs
│       └── VoxelSeparator.cs         ← dm.cs
├── Tools/
│   ├── Field_VoxelMorphData.cs
│   └── VoxelFaceNormalSbyte.cs
│   └── VoxelFaceVerticesIndexes.cs
└── Tests/
```

### DataService Candidates
- `cn.cs` (VoxelGridUtils) → already static, stays in P1
- Separation logic in `dm.cs` → `VoxelSeparationDataService` (pure C# coroutine logic extractable from MonoBehaviour)

### Interface Candidates
- `I_VoxelMeshEvents` — VoxelMesh change/chunk events (currently raw Action delegates)
- `I_VoxelSeparationCallback` — separation completion callback

---

## Phase 5 — Entity Framework

### Structure
```
Phase05_EntityFramework/
├── _-Systems/
│   └── EntityCore/                   ← 5+ tightly coupled
│       ├── EntityBase.cs             ← bgb
│       ├── ManagedEntity.cs          ← g.cs (lifecycle)
│       ├── ParameterizedEntity.cs    ← bcx.cs
│       ├── GenericEntityComponent.cs ← bcz<T,B>
│       └── I_EntityLifecycle.cs      ← events from g.cs
├── _-Systems/
│   └── EntityParameters/             ← 4+ tightly coupled
│       ├── ParameterRegistry.cs      ← bcx.bcr
│       ├── ParameterBinding.cs       ← bcx.bcp
│       ├── ExternalParameters.cs     ← bcx.bcs
│       └── I_ParameterAccess.cs      ← bcb, bcg, bce interfaces
├── _-Systems/
│   └── EntityBehaviors/              ← 3+ tightly coupled
│       ├── BehaviorManager.cs        ← bcx.bcv
│       ├── AbstractBehavior.cs       ← bcx.bcw
│       └── I_BehaviorAccess.cs       ← bca, bci, bch interfaces
├── Effectors/
│   └── [5 files from Effectors/]
├── Types/
│   ├── Field_ParameterKey.cs         ← bbu
│   ├── Field_ParameterValue.cs       ← bcm
│   ├── Field_ParameterDef.cs         ← bdb, bda
│   └── [~30 small type files]
└── Signals/
    ├── EntityActivationLock.cs       ← bcx.bcn
    └── EffectorSignalHelper.cs       ← bcx.bco
```

### DataService Candidates
- Parameter resolution logic (bcx.bcp methods) → `ParameterResolutionService` (pure C#)
- External parameter tracking (bcx.bcs) → `ExternalParameterService` (pure C#)

### Interface Candidates
- `I_EntityLifecycle` — created/started/enabled/disabled/destroyed events
- `I_ParameterAccess` — read-only parameter query (bcb/bcg)
- `I_ParameterBinding` — read-write parameter binding (bcf)
- `I_BehaviorAccess` — behavior query (bca/bci)
- `I_BehaviorControl` — behavior enable/disable (bch)

---

<!-- ==== FILE: LEARN/npcfr/SystemPortabilityMap.md ==== -->
# SystemPortabilityMap — npcfr

## Portability Classification

### L0 — Self-Contained (can be copied as-is into new project)

| System | Files | Dependencies | Notes |
|--------|-------|--------------|-------|
| Core Math Utils (fo.cs split) | ~10 | Unity.Mathematics, DOTween | Pure static, no scene references |
| Extension Methods (fp.cs) | 1 | Unity.Collections, Unity.Mathematics | Pure extensions |
| TripledoseLibs/Collections | ~5 | Unity.Collections | NativeContainer wrappers |
| RGBAtlasColor | 1 | None | Simple color struct |
| VoxelFace types | 2 | None | Simple structs |
| QuickOutline | 2 | None | Standalone mesh outline |
| TimeScaler | 1 | None | Time.timeScale wrapper |
| Data SOs (all 7) | 7 | None | Pure ScriptableObjects |
| Kinemation/Recoilly | ~16 | Unity.Mathematics | Standalone spring/recoil system |
| SingleShotAudioSource | 1 | None | Simple audio helper |
| LerpSound | 1 | None | Audio fade component |
| RandomActivator | 1 | None | Random enable/disable |
| ParticlesGroupMono | ~5 | None | Particle system controller |

### L1+ — Requires Adaptation (has cross-system deps)

| System | Files | Key Dependencies | Adaptation Needed |
|--------|-------|-----------------|-------------------|
| VoxelMesh Engine | ~25 | TripledoseLibs, Burst, RGBAtlas | Extract chunk builder interface |
| VoxelSeparation | ~5 | VoxelMesh, NativeContainers | Tight coupling to VoxelMesh.Voxels |
| Entity Framework (g/bcx/bcz) | ~80 | Zenject, custom types | Core framework — must be rebuilt or fully ported |
| LVA Creatures | ~10 | Entity Framework, Zenject | Depends on full entity system |
| LVA Limbs | ~25 | VoxelMesh, Entity Framework, Physics | Cross-cuts VoxelMesh + Entity |
| LVA Puppeteers | ~17 | Limbs, Physics, IK | Deep integration with bone hierarchy |
| ActiveRagdoll | ~9 | Physics, PuppetMaster | Cross-references between muscle/pelvis/controller |
| Infrastructure/DI | ~65 | Zenject, all domain types | Project-specific wiring |
| Player System | ~35 | Input System, Zenject, Views | Input → Toolbar → Inventory pipeline |
| Spawnables | ~15 | Zenject, LVA, VFX | Factory-pattern spawning |
| Views/UI | ~30 | Zenject, Player services | UI binds to services |
| Audio services | ~5 | Zenject | Service layer over AudioSource |
| Blood VFX | ~5 | Zenject, Physics | Particle + decal system |
| Map/Spinner | ~3 | Physics, Player events | Environment hazard |

## Portability Summary

| Level | Systems | Files | % of Codebase |
|-------|---------|-------|---------------|
| **L0** (self-contained) | 13 | ~53 | ~13% |
| **L1+** (needs adaptation) | 14 | ~361 | ~87% |

The high L1+ ratio is expected for a tightly integrated game codebase using Zenject DI throughout.

<!-- ==== FILE: LEARN/npcfr/surfer.md ==== -->
# surfer — npcfr

## Prompt 1: Initial Source Analysis

**Date**: 2025-05-16
**Action**: Full `/init` workflow

### What Was Done
1. Identified project `npcfr` in `MAIN-SOURCE/`
2. Read `entire-npcfr.stub` (9,750 files / 110.92 MB) for full asset inventory
3. Explored `Scripts/Assembly-CSharp/` folder (1094 items, ~800+ .cs files)
4. Read the 10 largest files by size to identify god-objects and framework classes
5. Scanned all named subfolders (21 domain folders with original naming)
6. Searched for architectural patterns:
   - 169 MonoBehaviour classes
   - 53 [Inject] usage points (Zenject DI)
   - 7 ScriptableObject classes
   - 33 Installer files
   - 324 Action/event matches across 120 files
   - 1 singleton (l.cs)
   - 0 FindObjectOfType calls
7. Read key domain files: Creature, AbstractLimb, VoxelMesh, entity framework (g, bcx)
8. Mapped dependency graph and inheritance chains

### Documents Generated
- `ARCHITECTURE.md` — full architecture analysis
- `PhaseMap.md` — 13 phases with dependency ordering
- `StructureMap.md` — per-phase internal structure with systems/interfaces/DataServices
- `GOAL.md` — target architecture rules and conventions
- `Estimate.md` — hours per phase (135–182 total)
- `SystemPortabilityMap.md` — L0/L1+ classification
- `surfer.md` — this file

### Key Findings
- **Heavily obfuscated** decompiled codebase (GUPS.Obfuscator)
- **Clean DI architecture** — Zenject throughout, no FindObjectOfType, 1 singleton
- **Core mechanic**: Voxel-based destructible humanoid NPCs with ragdoll physics
- **Entity framework**: Deep abstract hierarchy (`bgb → g → bcx → bcz → concrete`)
- **VoxelMesh**: Burst-compiled voxel body system with runtime separation (dismemberment)
- **13 phases** identified with clear dependency ordering
- **God objects** to split: `fo.cs` (1420 lines), `bcx.cs` (940 lines)

---

## Coupling Hotspots

### 1. FindObjectOfType — **ZERO** instances (clean)
The entire codebase uses singleton access patterns exclusively. No `FindObjectOfType` or `FindObjectsOfType` calls exist.

### 2. Static Instance Access (Singleton.Instance)
Every manager is accessed globally via `ManagerName.Instance`. The heaviest consumers:
- **Player.cs** → reads 15+ singletons
- **Customer.cs** → reads ProductManager, NPCManager, QuestManager, MoneyManager, TimeManager
- **Station objects** → read ProductManager, StorageManager, ManagementMode
- **UI classes** → read nearly every manager

### 3. Direct Cross-Domain References
| Source | Target | Type |
|--------|--------|------|
| Player | LandVehicle | Direct field (`CurrentVehicle`) |
| Player | Skateboard | Direct field + events |
| NPC | LandVehicle | Direct field + events |
| Customer | Dealer | AssignedDealer reference |
| Customer | Supplier | Supplier recommendation chain |
| Dealer | Customer | List\<Customer> AssignedCustomers |
| Employee | Property/Business | Direct assignment |
| PoliceOfficer | Player | Pursuit target |
| Station objects | ProductManager | Product/recipe lookup |
| Station objects | StorageManager | Item transit |
| TransitRoute | ITransitEntity | Source/Destination |
| GrowContainer | TimeManager | Time event subscription |

### 4. Static Registry Lists
| Class | Static List | Purpose |
|-------|-------------|---------|
| Player | `PlayerList`, `Local` | All players + local reference |
| Customer | `LockedCustomers`, `UnlockedCustomers` | Customer progression |
| Dealer | `AllPlayerDealers` | Recruited dealers |
| ProductManager | `DiscoveredProducts`, `ListedProducts`, `FavouritedProducts` | Product state |

---

## Event System

### Pattern Mix
The codebase uses three event patterns interchangeably:

1. **C# `Action<T>`** — Most common for inter-system communication
2. **`UnityEvent`** — Used for Inspector-configurable callbacks (stations, NPCs, UI)
3. **Custom `delegate`** — Rare, used in Player (VehicleEvent), NPCInventory (ItemFilter), Messaging (ResponseCallback), Noise (HearingEvent)

### Central Event Hubs

**TimeManager** (temporal events):
- `onHourPass`, `onDayPass`, `onWeekPass` — time progression
- `onUpdate`, `onFixedUpdate` — frame-rate callbacks (centralized)
- `onTimeSkip`, `onTimeChanged` — time manipulation
- `onSleepStart`, `onSleepEnd` — sleep cycle
- `onFirstNight` — tutorial trigger

**Player** (player lifecycle):
- `static onLocalPlayerSpawned` — local player ready
- `static onPlayerSpawned/onPlayerDespawned` — any player
- `onEnterVehicle/onExitVehicle` — vehicle state
- `onRagdoll/onRagdollEnd` — physics state
- `onArrested/onFreed/onTased/onTasedEnd` — law state
- `onPassedOut/onPassOutRecovery` — consciousness

**NPC** (NPC lifecycle):
- `onEnterVehicle/onExitVehicle`, `onVisibilityChanged`, `onConversationCreated`

**NPCAwareness** (crime detection):
- `onNoticedGeneralCrime/PettyCrime/DrugDealing/PlayerViolatingCurfew/SuspiciousPlayer`
- `onGunshotHeard/onExplosionHeard/onHitByCar`

**ItemSlot** (inventory changes):
- `onItemDataChanged`, `onItemInstanceChanged`, `onLocked/onUnlocked`, `onFilterChange`

**Economy events**:
- `Customer.onCustomerUnlocked` (static), `onDealCompleted`, `onContractAssigned`
- `Dealer.onDealerRecruited` (static), `onContractAccepted`
- `ProductManager.onProductDiscovered/Created/Listed/Delisted`
- `MoneyManager.onNetworthCalculation`
- `LevelManager.onRankUp/onRankChanged`

---

## Data Flow

### Product Creation Pipeline
```
StationRecipe (SO)
  → Player inserts ingredients into Station (ItemSlot)
  → Station validates recipe (DoIngredientsSuffice)
  → Station starts operation (SendCookOperation RPC)
  → Timer runs (CookTime from recipe)
  → Station creates output (ProductStationItem → StorableItemInstance)
  → Output goes to OutputSlot (IItemSlotOwner)
  → Player collects → PlayerInventory
```

### Product Value Pipeline
```
ProductDefinition (SO, base values)
  → PropertyItemDefinition (mix ingredient, adds EProperty effects)
  → MixerMap (maps ingredient → effect on product)
  → ProductManager.CalculateProductValue(properties, quality)
  → Customer.GetProductEnjoyment(affinity + quality + addiction)
  → Contract price = base value × quality multiplier × customer preference
```

### Save/Load Pipeline
```
SaveManager.Save()
  → Iterates ISaveable list (ordered by LoadOrder for IBaseSaveable)
  → Each saveable: GetSaveString() → JSON
  → WriteData() → disk (SaveGame_N/subfolder/file.json)
  → 15 saves per frame (batched)

LoadManager.StartGame()
  → Read SaveInfo (save slot metadata)
  → Load scene → Initialize IBaseSaveables (by LoadOrder)
  → For each saveable: Load(json) → restore state
  → Staggered replication queue for network sync
  → Fire onLoadComplete
```

### Transit (Item Automation) Pipeline
```
ITransitEntity.OutputSlots (source station)
  → TransitRoute (source → destination link)
  → Employee walks: source.OutputSlot → picks up → destination.InputSlot
  → ITransitEntity.InsertItemIntoInput() (destination station)
  → ConfigurationReplicator syncs field changes over network
```

### NPC Decision Pipeline
```
NPCScheduleManager → NPCEvent (current schedule event)
  → NPCBehaviour stack (priority-ordered)
  → NPCActions (action execution)
  → NPCMovement (A* pathfinding + physical movement)
  → NPCAwareness (vision cone + hearing)
  → NPCResponses (reaction to awareness events)
```

---

## Inheritance Chains

### Worth Preserving
```
NetworkBehaviour
  └── BuildableItem (abstract)
        ├── GridItem
        │     └── ToggleableItem
        └── SurfaceItem
              └── ToggleableSurfaceItem

ScriptableObject
  └── ItemDefinition
        └── StorableItemDefinition
              ├── QualityItemDefinition
              │     └── ProductDefinition (abstract)
              │           ├── WeedDefinition
              │           ├── CocaineDefinition
              │           ├── MethDefinition
              │           └── ShroomDefinition
              └── PropertyItemDefinition

NetworkBehaviour
  └── NPC
        ├── Dealer (: IItemSlotOwner)
        ├── Employee (: IConfigurable)
        │     ├── Botanist, Chemist, Packager, Cleaner
        └── (Customer is NOT a subclass — uses composition)

MonoBehaviour
  └── Singleton<T>
        └── PersistentSingleton<T>
NetworkBehaviour
  └── NetworkSingleton<T>
MonoBehaviour
  └── PlayerSingleton<T>

Quest (abstract)
  └── QuestEntry (many concrete types)
  └── Contract (deal-based quest)

Behaviour (abstract, NPCs.Behaviour)
  └── 54 concrete behaviour classes
```

### Worth Flattening
```
MonoBehaviour → StationItem → ProductStationItem/LiquidMeth_StationItem
  (shallow, could be interface-based)

MonoBehaviour → ItemModule → IngredientModule/CookableModule/PourableModule
  (already thin, keep as composition)
```

# Estimate — Schedule I (schedule-1)

## Methodology

Hours = file count × complexity tier multiplier

| Tier | Multiplier | Criteria |
|------|-----------|----------|
| **T1 Simple** | 0.25 hr/file | Data classes, enums, DTOs, thin wrappers |
| **T2 Standard** | 0.5 hr/file | Standard MonoBehaviours, UI screens, behaviours |
| **T3 Complex** | 1.0 hr/file | Networked systems, god-object splits, multi-interface classes |
| **T4 Critical** | 2.0 hr/file | God objects (>15 KB), framework foundations, cross-system coordinators |

## Naming Conventions

### Classes
| Pattern | Convention | Example |
|---------|-----------|---------|
| ScriptableObject data | `SO_` prefix | `SO_ProductDefinition` |
| Runtime wrapper | `W_` prefix | `W_ItemInstance` |
| Management config field | `Field_` prefix | `Field_Item`, `Field_Quality` |
| DataService | `___Service` suffix | `ProductValueService` |
| Interface | `I` prefix | `IItemSlotOwner` (existing convention) |
| Singleton manager | `___Manager` suffix | `TimeManager`, `ProductManager` |
| NPC behaviour | `___Behaviour` suffix | `IdleBehaviour`, `FleeBehaviour` |
| UI screen | `___Screen`/`___Canvas`/`___Interface` | `DeathScreen`, `VehicleCanvas` |
| Phone app | `App<T>` base class | Existing pattern |

### Files
| Pattern | Convention |
|---------|-----------|
| One class per file | File name = class name |
| System folder | `_SystemName/` with underscore prefix |
| Test file | `___Tests.cs` suffix |
| Data DTO | `___Data` suffix (e.g., `PlayerSaveData`) |
| Loader | `___Loader` suffix (e.g., `PlayerLoader`) |

### Fields & Properties
| Pattern | Convention | Example |
|---------|-----------|---------|
| Serialized fields | `[SerializeField]` with camelCase | `[SerializeField] private float maxHealth` |
| Public fields | PascalCase | `public float Health` |
| Private fields | `_` prefix camelCase | `private float _currentHealth` |
| Constants | UPPER_SNAKE | `MAX_CUSTOMERS = 8` |
| Static events | `on` prefix | `static Action onPlayerSpawned` |
| Instance events | `on` prefix | `Action onDie` |
| SyncVar | PascalCase property | `public float CurrentAddiction` |

---

## Class Responsibilities

### Singleton
- **Owns:** Global state for its domain
- **Does NOT:** Directly reference other singletons in constructors (use lazy access)
- **Access:** `ManagerName.Instance`
- **Variants:** `Singleton<T>` (scene), `PersistentSingleton<T>` (cross-scene), `NetworkSingleton<T>` (networked), `PlayerSingleton<T>` (per-player)

### NetworkBehaviour (FishNet)
- **Owns:** Networked state via SyncVars
- **RPCs:** `_Server` suffix for ServerRpc, `_Client` for ObserversRpc/TargetRpc
- **Pattern:** Request→Authorize→Broadcast (Server validates, then broadcasts to clients)
- **Ownership:** Use `PredictedOwner` for physics objects, `NetworkTransform` for position sync

### BuildableItem (Entity)
- **Owns:** GUID, placement data, save state
- **Lifecycle:** Spawn → Initialize → Place on Grid/Surface → Operate → Destroy
- **Variants:** GridItem (tile-based), SurfaceItem (free-placed)
- **Always:** IGUIDRegisterable + ISaveable

### StationItem (Crafting)
- **Owns:** Physical station item in world
- **Composition:** ItemModule system (Ingredient, Cookable, Pourable)
- **Pattern:** Create → ActivateModules → Interact → Destroy

### DataService (Pure Logic)
- **No MonoBehaviour** — pure C# class
- **No Unity dependencies** — only data types
- **Stateless:** All methods are static or take explicit parameters
- **Testable:** Can be unit tested without Unity runtime

---

## Decoupling Patterns

### 1. Event-Based Communication
```csharp
// Publisher (TimeManager)
public Action onHourPass;

// Subscriber (GrowContainer)
void OnEnable() => TimeManager.Instance.onHourPass += OnHourPass;
void OnDisable() => TimeManager.Instance.onHourPass -= OnHourPass;
```

### 2. Interface-Based Contracts
```csharp
// Station implements ITransitEntity
public interface ITransitEntity {
    List<ItemSlot> InputSlots { get; }
    List<ItemSlot> OutputSlots { get; }
    bool IsAcceptingItems { get; }
    void InsertItemIntoInput(ItemInstance item);
}

// Employee references ITransitEntity, not concrete station
ITransitEntity source = transitRoute.Source;
source.InsertItemIntoInput(item);
```

### 3. Singleton Access (Existing Pattern)
```csharp
// Access via Instance property
ProductManager.Instance.DiscoverProduct(definition);
TimeManager.Instance.onDayPass += OnDayPass;
```

### 4. ScriptableObject Data Pipeline
```csharp
// SO defines data (Inspector-editable)
SO_ProductDefinition → SO_StationRecipe → SO_MixerMap

// Runtime wrapper holds instance state
W_ItemInstance wraps SO_ItemDefinition with Quantity, Quality
```

### 5. Configuration Replication
```csharp
// EntityConfiguration holds ConfigField list
// ConfigurationReplicator syncs each field type via RPCs
// IConfigurable provides the bridge
```

---

## Lifecycle Rules

### Initialization Order
1. PersistentSingletons (Awake, DontDestroyOnLoad)
2. NetworkSingletons (after FishNet connection)
3. Regular Singletons (scene Awake)
4. ISaveable.InitializeSaveable() (after managers ready)
5. IBaseSaveable.Load() (ordered by LoadOrder property)
6. Player.Activate() (after load complete)

### Save Order
1. SaveManager.Save() called (manual or auto)
2. ISaveable list iterated (IBaseSaveable first, by LoadOrder)
3. Each: GetSaveString() → JSON → WriteData() → disk
4. 15 saves per frame (batched via SaveRequest queue)
5. SaveManager fires onSaveComplete

### Destruction Order
1. BuildableItem.Destroy() → Destroy_Server RPC → Destroy_Client
2. NPC.OnDestroy() → unregister from NPCManager
3. Player.OnDespawn() → remove from PlayerList
4. Singleton.OnDestroy() → set Destroyed flag

---

## C# Features in Use

| Feature | Usage |
|---------|-------|
| Generics | `Singleton<T>`, `NetworkSingleton<T>`, `App<T>`, `SerializableDictionary<K,V>` |
| Interfaces | 16+ cross-cutting interfaces |
| Abstract classes | BuildableItem, ItemInstance, ItemModule, Quest, Behaviour, GrowContainer, Plant |
| Events (Action) | 100+ event declarations |
| UnityEvent | 80+ Inspector-configurable events |
| Delegates | VehicleEvent, HearingEvent, ResponseCallback, BoolCheck |
| Enums | EDrugType, EProperty, EQuality, EMapRegion, ERank, ECrimeType, EItemCategory, etc. |
| ScriptableObjects | ItemDefinition hierarchy, StationRecipe, MixerMap, DialogueContainer |
| Coroutines | CoroutineService centralizes StartCoroutine |
| Nullable | Not widely used (legacy C# style) |
| LINQ | Limited usage (mostly manual iteration) |
| Attributes | [SerializeField], [RequireComponent], [DisallowMultipleComponent], [SyncVar] |

---

## Testing Strategy

### Unit Testable (DataServices)
| Service | Test Focus |
|---------|-----------|
| ProductValueService | Property combination → value calculation |
| MixResolverService | Ingredient + product → output product |
| ContractEvaluationService | Quality, affinity, addiction → success chance |
| ItemSlotService | Insert, capacity, filtering, stacking |
| ConditionEvaluationService | Variable conditions → bool |
| NPCBehaviourPriorityService | Behaviour priority → active behaviour |

### Integration Testable (requires Unity)
| System | Test Focus |
|--------|-----------|
| Save/Load | Round-trip: save → load → verify state |
| ItemSlot | Network replication of slot changes |
| Station operations | Recipe input → timer → output |
| NPC schedule | Time advance → schedule event transition |
| Transit routing | Source slot → employee → destination slot |

### Manual Test Scenarios
| Scenario | Covers |
|----------|--------|
| Full drug production chain | Growing → Harvest → Station → Package → Store |
| Deal completion | Customer unlock → Contract → Deliver → Pay |
| Police encounter | Crime → Detection → Pursuit → Arrest/Escape |
| Building mode | Purchase property → Place stations → Configure → Automate |
| Multiplayer | Host → Client join → Shared world state |

---

## Project-Specific Notes

### Drug Types (EDrugType)
`Weed`, `Cocaine`, `Meth`, `Shroom` + 2 variants

### Property Effects (EProperty — 17 effects)
Modify product value and customer experience. Applied via mixing ingredients at stations.

### Map Regions (EMapRegion — 6 regions)
Rank-gated progression. Higher regions unlock at higher ranks.

### Quality System (EQuality)
Affects product value, customer satisfaction, and contract success.

### Tags/Layers (from source)
- NPC detection layers for vision/hearing
- Ground detection masks for player/NPC movement
- Vehicle layers for physics interactions

### Utility Extensions
- `CircularQueue<T>` — fixed-size circular buffer
- `RollingAverage` — windowed average calculation
- `SmoothedVelocityCalculator` — velocity smoothing
- `SerializableDictionary<K,V>` — Unity-serializable dictionary
- `PackingAlgorithm` — bin-packing for storage grids

### Key Constants (from source)
| Constant | Value | Location |
|----------|-------|----------|
| SAVE_SLOT_COUNT | 5 | SaveManager |
| SAVES_PER_FRAME | 15 | SaveManager |
| MAX_CUSTOMERS (per dealer) | 8 | Dealer |
| COCA_LEAF_REQUIRED | 20 | Cauldron |
| DEAL_COOLDOWN | varies | Customer |
| AFFINITY_MAX_EFFECT | varies | Customer |

- `SaveInfo.cs`, `SaveRequest.cs`, `LoadRequest.cs`, `SavePoint.cs`
- `SerializableDictionary.cs`

### What It Looks Like When Running
Game boots, singletons initialize in order, save/load system ready, network lobby available. No visible gameplay yet — this is the skeleton.

### Difficulty: ★★☆ Medium
Singleton and persistence patterns are well-understood. Main challenge is NetworkSingleton + FishNet integration and ensuring save/load ordering is correct.

176 files with 54 behaviour classes, 78+ character classes, and the NPC.cs god-object. The behaviour priority stack and schedule system are complex. A* pathfinding integration adds technical depth.

All crafting stations functional. Players mix products at MixingStation, cook at LabOven/ChemistryStation/Cauldron, dry at DryingRack, press at BrickPress, package at PackagingStation. Multi-step physical interactions (pouring, smashing, stirring). Recipes produce new items.

### Difficulty: ★★★ Hard
Each station (7 major ones) is a mini god-object (13-16 KB) implementing the same 4-interface pattern. High interaction complexity with physical objects, animations, and multi-step workflows.

## Cross-Phase Modification Table

| Phase | Modifies (Backward) | Modified By (Forward) |
|-------|---------------------|-----------------------|
| P0 | — | P1 (registers saveables), P3 (GameManager refs) |
| P1 | — | P5 (ProductDefinition extends ItemDefinition), P6 (stations use ItemSlot) |
| P2 | — | P4 (NPC schedules use TimeManager), P8 (Law uses TimeManager) |
| P3 | — | P4 (NPC references Player), P8 (combat targets Player) |
| P4 | — | P5 (Customer/Dealer extend NPC), P8 (PoliceOfficer extends NPC), P9 (Employee extends NPC) |
| P5 | P1 (product extends item defs) | P6 (stations use recipes/products), P9 (delivery uses contracts) |
| P6 | P1 (stations use ItemSlot/GridItem) | P7 (management configures stations), P9 (employees operate stations) |
| P7 | P6 (management configures stations) | P9 (transit routes for employees) |
| P8 | P3 (combat targets Player), P4 (Police extends NPC) | P10 (UI for law/vehicles) |
| P9 | P4 (Employee extends NPC), P6 (operates stations) | P10 (UI for storage/tools) |
| P10 | All previous phases | — |
| P11 | P3 (effects target Player) | — |
| P12 | P4 (Cartel uses NPC), P3 (Skating uses Player) | — |

### Critical Cross-Phase Interfaces
| Interface | Defined In | Implemented By |
|-----------|-----------|----------------|
| `ISaveable` | P0 | P1–P12 (everything saves) |
| `IItemSlotOwner` | P1 | P5 (Dealer), P6 (all stations), P9 (StorageEntity) |
| `ITransitEntity` | P7 | P6 (all stations), P9 (StorageEntity) |
| `IConfigurable` | P7 | P6 (all stations), P9 (Employee) |
| `ICombatTargetable` | P8 | P3 (Player), P4 (NPC) |
| `IGUIDRegisterable` | P0 | P1 (BuildableItem), P4 (NPC), P8 (LandVehicle) |

<!-- ==== FILE: LEARN/schedule-1/StructureMap.md ==== -->
# StructureMap — Schedule I (schedule-1)

## Naming Conventions

| Prefix/Suffix | Meaning | Example |
|---------------|---------|---------|
| `SO_` | ScriptableObject data container | `SO_ProductDefinition`, `SO_StationRecipe` |
| `Field_` | Management config field | `Field_Item`, `Field_NPC`, `Field_Quality` |
| `W_` | Runtime wrapper (SO → runtime) | `W_ItemInstance`, `W_ProductInstance` |
| `_System/` | Folder for 3+ tightly coupled files | `_NPCSystem/`, `_StationSystem/` |
| `DataService` | Pure C# logic extracted from MonoBehaviour | `ProductValueService`, `ContractEvaluationService` |
| `I_` | Interface | `I_Saveable`, `I_ItemSlotOwner` (already exist without prefix) |

---

## Phase 6 — Crafting & Stations

### `_StationFramework/` (18 files)
| Current | Becomes | Role |
|---------|---------|------|

| Fillable.cs | Fillable.cs | Liquid container |
| BoilingFlask.cs | BoilingFlask.cs | Chemistry flask |

### `_CraftingStations/` (55 files → shared pattern extraction)

All 7 major stations follow identical pattern: `GridItem : IUsable, IItemSlotOwner, ITransitEntity, IConfigurable`

**Shared extraction:**
| Extract To | Responsibility |
|------------|---------------|
| StationBase.cs | Common station logic: Open/Close, Hovered/Interacted, User tracking, IItemSlotOwner impl, ITransitEntity impl, IConfigurable impl |
| StationOperation.cs | Common operation lifecycle: Start → Timer → Complete |

Then each station only needs its unique logic:
| Station | Unique Logic |
|---------|-------------|
| LabOven | Hammer smashing, shard spawning, liquid pour |
| MixingStation | Product+Mixer→Output, discovery box |
| Cauldron | 4 ingredient + liquid + output, coca leaf dragging |
| ChemistryStation | 9-step enum workflow, explosion |
| DryingRack | Multiple concurrent drying operations |
| BrickPress | Brick pressing animation |
| PackagingStation | Package sealing, label |
| MushroomSpawnStation | Syringe interaction, grain bag |

**Interface candidates:**
- `IStation` — Already exists as quartet (IUsable + IItemSlotOwner + ITransitEntity + IConfigurable). Consider formalizing as a composite interface.

<!-- ==== FILE: LEARN/schedule-1/SystemPortabilityMap.md ==== -->
# SystemPortabilityMap — Schedule I (schedule-1)

## Classification

- **L0** — Fully portable: pure logic, no Unity/FishNet dependencies, can be extracted as-is
- **L1** — Mostly portable: light Unity dependency (ScriptableObject, MonoBehaviour), minimal refactor needed
- **L2** — Partially portable: significant Unity dependency (NetworkBehaviour, physics, rendering), needs adaptation layer
- **L3** — Engine-bound: deeply coupled to Unity/FishNet runtime (RPCs, SyncVars, physics, rendering), not portable

---

## Per-System Classification

### Phase 0 — Core Infrastructure
| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| Singleton\<T> | L3 | MonoBehaviour-based, Unity lifecycle |
| NetworkSingleton\<T> | L3 | FishNet NetworkBehaviour |
| PlayerSingleton\<T> | L3 | MonoBehaviour + FishNet client hooks |
| PersistentSingleton\<T> | L3 | DontDestroyOnLoad (Unity-specific) |
| SaveManager | L2 | File I/O is portable; Unity event hooks are not |
| LoadManager | L2 | Scene loading is Unity-specific; data loading is portable |
| GenericSaveablesManager | L2 | Interface-based but Unity singleton |
| ISaveable/IBaseSaveable | L0 | Pure interfaces |
| SaveInfo, SaveRequest, LoadRequest | L0 | Pure DTOs |
| SerializableDictionary | L1 | ISerializationCallbackReceiver is Unity-specific |
| GameManager | L3 | NetworkSingleton + FishNet RPCs |
| Settings | L2 | Unity PlayerPrefs-dependent |
| Registry | L2 | GUID tracking, light Unity dependency |
| CoroutineService | L3 | Unity coroutine system |
| PackingAlgorithm | L0 | Pure math/logic |

### Phase 1 — Data Frameworks
| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| ItemDefinition (SO hierarchy) | L1 | ScriptableObject base, but data is pure |
| ItemInstance | L0 | Abstract C# class, no Unity dependency |
| ItemSlot | L1 | Action events (portable), but SlotOwner ties to Unity |
| IItemSlotOwner | L0 | Pure interface |
| BuildableItem | L3 | NetworkBehaviour + RPCs + GUID + physics |
| GridItem | L3 | Tile system + NetworkBehaviour |
| SurfaceItem | L3 | Surface placement + NetworkBehaviour |
| ToggleableItem/Surface | L3 | NetworkBehaviour + RPCs |
| Tile, Grid, Coordinate | L1 | Mostly math, light MonoBehaviour for scene presence |
| FootprintTile, ProceduralTile | L1 | Geometry calculations |

### Phase 2 — World Foundation
| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| TimeManager | L2 | Time logic is portable; NetworkSingleton is not |
| Map, POI, MapRegion | L2 | Data model portable; Unity Transform/Singleton not |
| VariableDatabase | L2 | Data portable; NetworkSingleton wrapper not |
| BaseVariable, Condition | L0 | Pure data + logic |
| LevelManager | L2 | Rank math portable; NetworkSingleton not |
| Noise system | L1 | Event model portable; spatial queries use Unity physics |

### Phase 3 — Player Core
| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| Player | L3 | NetworkBehaviour, CharacterController, physics, FishNet RPCs |
| PlayerCamera | L3 | Unity Camera, Transform, InputSystem |
| PlayerMovement | L3 | CharacterController, Unity physics |
| PlayerInventory | L2 | ItemSlot logic portable; PlayerSingleton not |
| PlayerHealth/Energy | L1 | Value tracking portable; Unity events not |
| PlayerCrimeData | L0 | Pure data tracking |

### Phase 4 — NPC Core
| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| NPC | L3 | NetworkBehaviour, A* pathfinding, physics |
| NPCMovement | L3 | A* Pathfinding Project, Unity NavMesh |
| NPCAwareness | L2 | Vision cone logic portable; Physics.Raycast not |
| NPCBehaviour (base) | L1 | Priority stack logic portable; MonoBehaviour lifecycle not |
| 54 Behaviour classes | L2 | Logic portable; Unity references (Transform, etc.) not |
| NPCScheduleManager | L1 | Schedule logic portable |
| NPCRelationData | L0 | Pure data + math |
| 78+ Character classes | L2 | Character data portable; Unity/FishNet hooks not |

### Phase 5 — Economy & Product
| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| Customer | L2 | Economy logic portable; NetworkBehaviour not |
| Dealer | L2 | Business logic portable; NPC base not |
| Supplier | L2 | Same pattern |
| Contract, ContractReceipt | L0 | Pure data |
| ProductManager | L2 | Product logic portable; NetworkSingleton not |
| ProductDefinition (SO) | L1 | ScriptableObject wrapper on portable data |
| MixerMap | L0 | Pure data mapping |
| EDrugType, EProperty, EQuality | L0 | Pure enums |
| **ProductValueService** | L0 | Pure calculation — fully portable |
| **ContractEvaluationService** | L0 | Pure calculation — fully portable |
| **MixResolverService** | L0 | Pure calculation — fully portable |

### Phase 6 — Crafting & Stations
| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| StationRecipe (SO) | L1 | ScriptableObject, data is pure |
| StationItem | L2 | MonoBehaviour + module composition |
| ItemModule hierarchy | L1 | Logic portable; MonoBehaviour base not |
| Fillable, BoilingFlask | L3 | Liquid rendering, physics |
| LabOven, MixingStation, etc. | L3 | GridItem + 4 interfaces + physics + animation |

### Phase 7 — Property & Management
| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| Property, Business | L2 | Data model portable; Unity references not |
| BuildManager | L3 | Unity physics raycasting, grid placement |
| EntityConfiguration | L1 | ConfigField data portable; Unity events not |
| ConfigurationReplicator | L3 | Pure FishNet RPCs |
| TransitRoute | L1 | Routing logic portable; visual line not |
| ConfigField hierarchy | L1 | Data portable; UnityEvent not |
| **TransitRoutingService** | L0 | Pure validation logic — fully portable |

### Phase 8 — Gameplay Systems
| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| CombatManager | L3 | NetworkSingleton + physics explosions |
| ICombatTargetable, IDamageable | L0 | Pure interfaces |
| LawManager, LawController | L1 | Crime data + settings mostly portable |
| CurfewManager | L2 | Time-based logic portable; NetworkSingleton not |
| PoliceOfficer | L3 | NPC base + A* + pursuit AI |
| LandVehicle | L3 | WheelColliders, Rigidbody, NetworkBehaviour |
| VehicleAgent | L3 | A* + Unity physics |

### Phase 9 — Tools & Operations
| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| Equippable hierarchy | L3 | Unity physics, animation, rendering |
| GrowContainer, Plant | L2 | Growth logic portable; GridItem base not |
| StorageEntity, StorageGrid | L2 | Grid logic portable; NetworkBehaviour not |
| Employee | L3 | NPC base + pathfinding |
| TrashManager | L2 | Tracking portable; NetworkSingleton not |
| **ItemSlotService** | L0 | Pure slot logic — fully portable |

### Phase 10 — UI & Communication
| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| All UI (273 files) | L3 | Unity UI (Canvas, UGUI, TMP) |
| DialogueManager | L2 | Dialogue logic portable; Unity UI not |
| DialogueContainer | L1 | Data model portable |
| MessagingManager | L2 | Message logic portable; NetworkSingleton not |
| QuestManager | L2 | Quest logic portable; NetworkSingleton not |
| Quest, QuestEntry | L1 | Quest data/logic mostly portable |

### Phase 11 — Effects & Polish
| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| AudioManager, SFXManager | L3 | Unity AudioSource |
| Drug effects (17) | L2 | Effect logic portable; post-processing not |
| FXManager | L3 | Unity particle systems |
| Lighting | L3 | Unity Light, URP rendering |
| VoiceOver | L3 | Unity AudioSource |

### Phase 12 — Side Systems
| System | Level | Rationale |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| Casino (Blackjack, RTB, Slots) | L1 | Game logic portable; UI not |
| Graffiti | L3 | Texture painting, Unity rendering |
| Skating | L3 | Unity physics, animation |
| Cartel | L2 | Event logic portable; NPC base not |
| TV | L3 | Unity VideoPlayer |
| AvatarFramework | L3 | Unity SkinnedMeshRenderer, animation |

---

## Summary

| Level | Count | Percentage |
|-------|-------|-----------|
| **L0** — Fully portable | ~120 files | ~7% |
| **L1** — Mostly portable | ~280 files | ~16% |
| **L2** — Partially portable | ~450 files | ~26% |
| **L3** — Engine-bound | ~900 files | ~51% |

### Most Portable Subsystems (L0/L1)
1. All DataServices (9 services) — pure calculation logic
2. Contract/ContractReceipt — pure data
3. All enums (EDrugType, EProperty, EQuality, EMapRegion, etc.)
4. All interfaces (ISaveable, IItemSlotOwner, etc.)
5. ItemInstance hierarchy — abstract data wrappers
6. NPCRelationData — pure data + math
7. BaseVariable, Condition — pure logic
8. StationRecipe, MixerMap — pure data
9. Casino game logic — card/dice/slot math
10. LawSettings, crime type data — pure configuration
