# Schedule One — Domain Analysis Batch 2 (16 Domains)

## 1. ROOT-LEVEL FILES (ScheduleOne/)

### Registry : PersistentSingleton\<Registry>
- **Purpose**: Central item registry; maps string IDs → `ItemDefinition` via hashed dictionary
- **Key fields**: `ItemRegistry`, `ItemDictionary`, `itemIDAliases`
- **Methods**: `GetItem(ID)`, `AddToRegistry()`, `GetAllItems()`

### GameInput : PersistentSingleton\<GameInput>
- **Enums**: `ButtonCode` (33 values: PrimaryClick..SkateboardMount), `InputDeviceType` (KeyboardMouse/Gamepad)
- **Key fields**: `PlayerInput`, `MotionAxis`, `CameraAxis`, `exitListeners`
- **Inner class**: `ExitListener` with priority-based exit delegation

### Console : Singleton\<Console>
- **Inner abstract**: `ConsoleCommand { CommandWord, CommandDescription, Execute(args) }`
- **~15 concrete commands**: SetTime, SpawnVehicle, AddItemToInventory, ClearInventory, ChangeCash, ChangeOnlineBalance, SetMoveSpeed, etc.

### AchievementManager : PersistentSingleton\<AchievementManager>
- **Enum**: `EAchievement` (13 values: COMPLETE_PROLOGUE, DEALER_RECRUITED, MASTER_CHEF, BUSINESSMAN, MAGNATE, etc.)

### CommandListScreen : MainMenuScreen
- Simple UI container for displaying console commands

### IGUIDRegisterable (interface)
- `Guid GUID { get; }`, `SetGUID(string/Guid)` — used throughout for persistence

### TransformData (struct)
- Position/Rotation/Scale container with Lerp and Apply methods

### TransformExtensions (static)
- Extension methods for Transform ↔ TransformData conversion

### XPAmounts (static constants)
- `PLAYER_COMPLETED_DEAL=20`, `DEALER_COMPLETED_DEAL=10`, `SUCCESSFUL_SAMPLE=50`, `HARVESTED_PLANT=5`, `ESCAPED_ARREST=20/40/60`

---

## 2. NPCs/ Domain

### Class Hierarchy
```
NetworkBehaviour
├── NPC : NetworkBehaviour, IGUIDRegisterable, ISaveable, ICombatTargetable, IDamageable, ISightable
│   ├── Employee (Employees/)
│   │   ├── Botanist : Employee, IConfigurable
│   │   ├── Chemist : Employee, IConfigurable
│   │   ├── Cleaner : Employee, IConfigurable
│   │   └── Packager : Employee, IConfigurable
│   ├── Dealer : NPC, IItemSlotOwner (Economy/)
│   ├── Supplier : NPC (Economy/)
│   ├── PoliceOfficer : NPC (Police/)
│   ├── Fixer : NPC (CharacterClasses/)
│   ├── SewerKing : NPC (CharacterClasses/)
│   └── 78+ named CharacterClasses (Albert→Wei) — most extend Supplier/Customer
├── NPCMovement : NetworkBehaviour
├── NPCBehaviour : NetworkBehaviour
├── NPCActions : NetworkBehaviour
├── NPCHealth : NetworkBehaviour
├── NPCInventory : NetworkBehaviour, IItemSlotOwner
└── NPCScheduleManager : MonoBehaviour
```

### NPC (core entity)
- **Implements**: `IGUIDRegisterable`, `ISaveable`, `ICombatTargetable`, `IDamageable`, `ISightable`
- **Key component refs**: Movement, DialogueHandler, Avatar, Awareness, Responses, Actions, Behaviour, Inventory, Health, VoiceOverEmitter, Visibility
- **Key fields**: FirstName, LastName, ID, MugshotSprite, Region(EMapRegion), Aggression(0-1), IsImportant
- **Relationship**: `NPCRelationData RelationData`, `NPCUnlockedVariable`
- **Messaging**: `MSGConversation`, `ConversationCategories`
- **Summoning**: `CanBeSummoned`
- **Vehicle**: `CurrentVehicle`, `onEnterVehicle/onExitVehicle`

### NPCMovement : NetworkBehaviour
- **Enums**: `EAgentType` (Humanoid/BigHumanoid/IgnoreCosts), `EStance`, `WalkResult` (Failed/Interrupted/Stopped/Partial/Success)
- **Uses**: NavMeshAgent, CapsuleCollider, NPCAnimation, SmoothedVelocityCalculator
- **Key settings**: WalkSpeed, RunSpeed, MoveSpeedMultiplier, SlipperyMode
- **Threshold constants**: VEHICLE_RUNOVER=10, LIGHT_FLINCH=50, HEAVY_FLINCH=100, RAGDOLL=150

### NPCAwareness : MonoBehaviour
- **Refs**: VisionCone, Listener(Noise), NPCResponses
- **Events**: onNoticedGeneralCrime, onNoticedPettyCrime, onNoticedDrugDealing, onNoticedPlayerViolatingCurfew, onGunshotHeard, onHitByCar
- **Cross-refs**: Vision, Noise, PlayerScripts, Vehicles

### NPCResponses : MonoBehaviour (base)
- **Constants**: ASSAULT_RELATIONSHIPCHANGE=-0.25, DEADLYASSAULT=-1, AIMED_AT=-0.5, PICKPOCKET=-0.25
- **Virtual methods**: GunshotHeard, ExplosionHeard, NoticedPettyCrime, NoticedVandalism, SawPickpocketing, NoticedDrugDeal, HitByCar, ImpactReceived, RespondToFirstNonLethalAttack, RespondToLethalAttack
- **Subclasses**: `NPCResponses_Civilian` (with EAttackResponse: None/Panic/Flee/CallPolice/Fight), `NPCResponses_Police`, `NPCResponses_Employee`, `NPCResponses_CartelGoon`

### NPCBehaviour : NetworkBehaviour
- **Default behaviours** (all type `Behaviour`): Cowering, Ragdoll, CallPolice, GenericDialogue, HeavyFlinch, FaceTarget, Dead, Unconscious, Summon, ConsumeProduct, Combat, Flee, Stationary, RequestProduct
- **behaviourStack**: priority-sorted list; highest priority active behaviour wins
- **Cross-refs**: NPCScheduleManager, Product (ConsumeProduct)

### Behaviour (base) : NetworkBehaviour
- **Key fields**: Name, Priority, BehaviourIndex, Enabled, Started, Active
- **Lifecycle**: Enable→Activate→BehaviourUpdate→Deactivate→Disable
- **Pause/Resume** support
- **54 concrete behaviours** in Behaviour/ folder (AddSoil, ApplyAdditive, BagTrash, BodySearch, BrickPress, Checkpoint, ConsumeProduct, Cowering, Dead, DealerAttendDeal, DisposeTrash, EmptyTrashGrabber, FaceTarget, FinishLabOven, Flee, FootPatrol, GenericDialogue, GrowContainer, HarvestMushroom, HarvestPot, HeavyFlinch, Idle, MistMushroom, MoveItem, NPCBehaviour, PackagingStation, Pursuit, Ragdoll, RequestProduct, Schedule, Sentry, SewerGoblinRetrieve, SmokeBreak, SowSeed, StartCauldron, StartChemistryStation, StartDryingRack, StartLabOven, StartMixingStation, Stationary, StopDryingRack, Unconscious, UseSpawnStation, VehiclePatrol, VehiclePursuit, WaterPot)

### NPCManager : NetworkSingleton\<NPCManager>, ISaveable
- **Static**: `NPCRegistry` (all NPCs), NPCWarpPoints
- **Methods**: GetNPC(id), GetNPCsInRegion(region)

### NPCScheduleManager : MonoBehaviour
- **Manages**: ActionList (NPCAction[]), ActiveAction, PendingActions
- **CurfewMode**: EnabledDuringCurfew/NoCurfew GameObjects
- **Tick-driven**: processes actions by time, supports enable/disable schedule

### Schedules/
- **NPCAction** (abstract, NetworkBehaviour): StartTime, priority, IsEvent/IsSignal flags; lifecycle: Started→JumpTo→End→Interrupt
  - **NPCEvent** : NPCAction — has Duration/EndTime
    - Subclasses: NPCEvent_CartelGoonExit, NPCEvent_Conversate, NPCEvent_LocationBasedAction, NPCEvent_LocationDialogue, NPCEvent_Sit, NPCEvent_StayInBuilding
  - **NPCSignal** : NPCAction (implied)
    - Subclasses: NPCSignal_DriveToCarPark, NPCSignal_UseATM, NPCSignal_UseVendingMachine, NPCSignal_WaitForDelivery, NPCSignal_WalkToLocation

### Relation/
- **NPCRelationData**: RelationDelta (0-5, default 2), Unlocked, UnlockType (Recommendation/DirectApproach), Connections (mutual NPCs)
- **ERelationshipCategory**: Hostile/Unfriendly/Neutral/Friendly/Loyal

### NPCHealth : NetworkBehaviour
- SyncVar Health, MaxHealth, Invincible, CanRevive
- Events: onDie, onKnockedOut, onRevive, onTakeDamage
- REVIVE_DAYS = 3

### NPCInventory : NetworkBehaviour, IItemSlotOwner
- SlotCount, CanBePickpocketed, PickpocketDifficultyMultiplier
- RandomCash, RandomItems support
- ClearInventoryEachNight

### Character Classes (78+ files)
- Most named characters (Albert, Beth, Brad, etc.) extend either `Supplier` or `Customer` (via NPC chain)
- Special characters: `Fixer : NPC` (signing fee logic), `SewerKing : NPC` (SewerOffice ref), `SewerGoblin`, `SchizoGoblin`

- **Static lists**: DiscoveredProducts, ListedProducts, FavouritedProducts
- **Default products**: DefaultWeed, DefaultCocaine, DefaultMeth, DefaultShroom
- **Mix maps**: WeedMixMap, MethMixMap, CokeMixMap, ShroomMixMap
- **Mix operations**: CurrentMixOperation, onMixCompleted, onNewProductCreated
- **Constants**: MIN_PRICE=1, MAX_PRICE=999, CONTRACT_RECEIPT_MAX_COUNT=50
- **Cross-refs**: Economy (ContractReceipt), Effects, StationFramework

### Other Product files

## 14. Tiles/ Domain

- Width/Height auto-calculated
- Temperature system: cosmeticTemperatureEmitters, temperatureEmitters
- Methods: RegisterTile, DeregisterTile, IsTileValidAtCoordinate, GetTile

### Tile : MonoBehaviour
- x, y coordinates; AvailableOffset; OwnerGrid
- BuildableOccupants (List\<GridItem>), OccupantTiles
- Temperature: CosmeticTileTemperature, TileTemperature
- Events: onTileChanged, onTileTemperatureChanged
- Virtual: CanBeBuiltOn, IsIndoorTile

### Coordinate
- x, y; supports +, -, Equals, GetHashCode
- Cantor pairing for hash

### FootprintTile : MonoBehaviour
- X, Y, RequiredOffset, Corners(CornerObstacle[])
- MatchedStandardTile; Initialize(Tile)

### Supporting
- IndoorTile : Tile (implied), ProceduralTile
- TileAppearance, TileDetector, ETileColor, ETileDetectionMode
- CoordinatePair, CoordinateTilePair, CoordinateFootprintTilePair, CoordinateProceduralTilePair

---

## 15. Growing/ Domain

### GrowContainer (abstract) : GridItem, IUsable, ITransitEntity
- **Key settings**: SoilCapacity, MoistureCapacity, MoistureDrainPerHour
- **Allowed**: AllowedSoils, AllowedAdditives
- **State**: NormalizedSoilAmount, NormalizedMoistureAmount, IsFullyFilledWithSoil
- **SyncVars**: NPCUserObject, PlayerUserObject
- **References**: CameraHandler, TemperatureDisplay, SurfaceCover
- **Cross-refs**: Tiles(GridItem), Management, Property, Lighting

### Plant (abstract) : MonoBehaviour
- **Key fields**: SeedDefinition, GrowthTime, BaseYieldQuantity, GrowthStages(PlantGrowthStage[])
- **State**: NormalizedGrowthProgress, IsFullyGrown, YieldMultiplier, QualityLevel
- **Pot** reference (parent container)
- **Methods**: Initialize(pot, growthProgress), MinPass, AdditiveApplied, SetHarvestableActive
- **Constants**: BaseQualityLevel=0.5

### WeedPlant : Plant
- BranchPrefab (PlantHarvestable)

### CocaPlant : Plant (implied)

### Supporting
- Additive, PourableAdditive, SeedDefinition, FunctionalSeed
- SoilChunk, VialCap, GrowingMushroom, ShroomColony
- GrowContainerInteraction, GrowContainerCameraHandler, GrowContainerMoistureDisplay, GrowContainerSurfaceCover
- MushroomBedInteraction, MushroomBedMoistureDisplay
- PotInteraction, PotMoistureDisplay
- PlantGrowthStage, PlantHarvestable

---

## 16. Employees/ Domain

### Employee : NPC
- **Key fields**: Type(EEmployeeType), SigningFee, DailyWage, AssignedProperty, EmployeeIndex
- **SyncVar**: PaidForToday
- **State**: Fired, IsWaitingOutside, TimeSinceLastWorked, IsMale, AppearanceIndex
- **Behaviours**: WaitOutside(IdleBehaviour), MoveItemBehaviour
- **Dialogue**: BedNotAssigned, NotPaid, WorkIssue, Fire, Transfer
- **WorkIssues**: List\<NoWorkReason> (Reason, Fix, Priority)

### EEmployeeType
- Botanist=0, Handler=1, Chemist=2, Cleaner=3

### Concrete Employee Types
| Type | Base | Key Feature | Implements |
|------|------|-------------|------------|
| Botanist | Employee, IConfigurable | Manages pots, soil, water, additives, harvesting, drying racks | MaxAssignedPots, ~8 behaviour refs |
| Chemist | Employee, IConfigurable | Manages chemistry stations, lab ovens, cauldrons, mixing stations | MAX_ASSIGNED_STATIONS=4 |
| Packager | Employee, IConfigurable | Manages packaging stations, brick press | MaxAssignedStations, PackagingSpeedMultiplier |
| Cleaner | Employee, IConfigurable | Trash grabbing, emptying, bagging, disposing | MAX_ASSIGNED_BINS=6, TrashGrabberDef |

### EmployeeManager : NetworkSingleton\<EmployeeManager>
- **Prefabs**: BotanistPrefab, PackagerPrefab, ChemistPrefab, CleanerPrefab
- **Appearance system**: Male/FemaleAppearances, Voices, Names
- **Constants**: MALE_EMPLOYEE_CHANCE=0.67
- **Methods**: CreateNewEmployee(property, type), GenerateRandomName

### NPCResponses_Employee (in Employees/)
- Employee-specific response overrides

```
    │    Combat            │   │      Law              │    │    Tiles           │

    │  CombatBehaviour     │   │  LawController        │    │  Coordinate        │
    │  ICombatTargetable   │   │  Crime (30 types)     │    │  FootprintTile     │

    └──────────────────────┘   └──────────────────────┘
                                                            ┌────────────────────┐
    ┌──────────────────────┐   ┌──────────────────────┐    │    Variables       │
    │    Storage           │   │      UI               │    │  VariableDatabase  │
    │  StorageEntity       │   │  HUD, StorageMenu     │    │  BaseVariable      │
    │  WorldStorageEntity  │   │  HandoverScreen       │    │  Condition(s)      │
    │  StorageGrid         │   │  Phone, ShopManager   │    │  Bool/NumberVariable│
    │  StoredItem          │   │  ShopInterface        │    └────────────────────┘
    └──────────────────────┘   └──────────────────────┘
```

### Key Cross-Domain Relationships

1. **NPC is the central entity** — Customer, Dealer, Supplier, PoliceOfficer, Employee all extend NPC
2. **Economy↔Quests**: Contract extends Quest; Customer generates contracts; Dealer fulfills them
3. **Economy↔Product**: Customer has preferences (EDrugType, EProperty); ProductManager manages discovery/listing
4. **Property↔Tiles↔Building**: Property owns Grids, Grids contain Tiles, BuildManager creates GridItems/SurfaceItems
5. **Growing↔Tiles**: GrowContainer extends GridItem (from EntityFramework), lives on Grid tiles
6. **Employees↔Property**: Employee assigned to Property; Botanist manages GrowContainers, Chemist manages Stations
7. **Law↔Police↔NPCs**: PoliceOfficer is an NPC; LawManager dispatches officers; Crime hierarchy defines offenses
8. **Storage↔Economy**: DeadDrop uses WorldStorageEntity; StorageMenu opens StorageEntity
9. **Variables**: Used throughout for quest conditions, NPC unlock tracking, progress gating
10. **Map↔Everything**: EMapRegion used by NPC, Customer, DeliveryLocation, DeadDrop, MapRegionData

### Singleton Pattern Summary
| Pattern | Classes |
|---------|---------|
| PersistentSingleton\<T> | Registry, GameInput, AchievementManager |
| Singleton\<T> | Console, Map, HUD, StorageMenu, HandoverScreen, BuildManager, PropertyManager, BusinessManager, LawManager, LawController |
| NetworkSingleton\<T> | NPCManager, ProductManager, QuestManager, CombatManager, DarkMarket, VariableDatabase, EmployeeManager, ShopManager |
| PlayerSingleton\<T> | Phone, AppsCanvas, HomeScreen |

# Surfer — Schedule I (schedule-1)

## Prompt 1: Initial source analysis

**Date:** 2026-05-16

**Actions performed:**
1. Selected project: `schedule-1`
2. Verified `MAIN-SOURCE/schedule-1/` exists with `Scripts/Assembly-CSharp/` containing 2,041 .cs files
3. Read `MAIN-SOURCE/entire-schedule-1.stub` — 24,139 files, 10.242 GB total project
4. Created `LEARN/schedule-1/` folder structure
5. Identified 1,752 ScheduleOne namespace files across 66 domain folders
6. Read top 10 god-objects (Player, NPC, Customer, ProductManager, LandVehicle, Dealer, LabOven, MixingStation, Cauldron, ChemistryStation) — full analysis
7. Extracted all class declarations, singleton patterns, event patterns via grep scan across all 1,752 files
8. Read core frameworks: EntityFramework, ItemFramework, StationFramework, Persistence, DevUtilities (Singleton hierarchy), Management
9. Read all remaining domains via subagent: NPCs (176 files), UI (273), Product (45), Economy (20), Map (35), Quests (37), Property (14), Variables (12), Storage (24), Combat (11), Law (30), Building (21), Growing (22), Employees (9), Vehicles (44), plus all root files
10. Zero FindObjectOfType usage confirmed — clean singleton access throughout

- `ARCHITECTURE.md` — full dependency graph, 100+ singletons, god objects, event system, data flow, inheritance chains, asset inventory
- `PhaseMap.md` — 13 phases (P0–P12), 1,752 files mapped, cross-phase modification table
- `StructureMap.md` — system folders, DataService candidates, interface candidates, SO/Field/W prefixes
- `GOAL.md` — folder structure, naming conventions, class responsibilities, decoupling patterns, lifecycle, testing strategy
- `Estimate.md` — ~708 hours total, per-phase breakdown by complexity tier
- `SystemPortabilityMap.md` — L0–L3 classification, ~7% fully portable, ~51% engine-bound
- `surfer.md` — this file

**Key findings:**
- Game: Drug dealing simulation (Schedule I) in Unity 2022.x with FishNet multiplayer
- 4 drug types (Weed, Cocaine, Meth, Shroom) with mixing/crafting pipeline
- 6 god-objects need splitting: Player (40 KB), NPC (24 KB), Customer (22 KB), ProductManager (22 KB), LandVehicle (17 KB), Dealer (16 KB)
- 7 major crafting stations share identical 4-interface pattern (IUsable+IItemSlotOwner+ITransitEntity+IConfigurable)
- 100+ singletons (25 NetworkSingleton, 35+ Singleton, 11 PersistentSingleton, 7 PlayerSingleton, 40+ UI)
- Zero FindObjectOfType — clean architecture
- 9 DataService extraction candidates identified
- 78+ named NPC characters, 54 behaviour classes, 30 crime types, 22 quest types

## Coupling Hotspots

### FindObjectOfType / GetComponent Patterns
- `OnlineOrderInteraction` → `Camera.main` cached as `m_MainCamera`
- `BoxInteraction` → raycast-based interaction with multiple target types
- `FurniturePlacer` → raycast-based placement with layermask filtering
- Most singletons accessed via `NoktaSingleton<T>.Instance` (static accessor)

### Static Instance Access (Singleton.Instance)
Every manager-to-manager call goes through `ManagerName.Instance.Method()`:
- `MoneyManager.Instance.MoneyTransition()`
- `CustomerManager.Instance.m_ActiveCustomers`
- `InventoryManager.Instance.ProductCount()`
- `PriceManager.Instance.SellingPrice()`
- `CheckoutManager.Instance.GetAvailableCheckout()`
- `DayCycleManager.Instance.CurrentHour`
- etc.

### Direct Cross-Domain References
| Script | References Outside Its Domain |
|--------|------------------------------|
| BoxInteraction | DisplaySlot, RackSlot, VendingSlot, TrashBin, MissionSystem, PlayerInstance |
| Customer | DisplaySlot, Checkout, CustomerQueue, WeightedProductSO, Product |
| Restocker | RestockerManager, DisplaySlot, Box, RackSlot, Dirt, TrashBin |
| Checkout | Customer, PlayerInstance, CheckoutBelt, Product, CashRegister |
| SecurityGuard | Crate, Restocker, Shoplifter, Product |
| Baker | Box, DisplaySlot, Oven, Crate |
| Scale | CustomerQueue, BarcodeSpawner, ProductPaperBag, Numpad |
| NPC | VendingMachine, VendingSlot, Product |
| PlayerInstance | 15+ interaction classes, PhotonView, CinemachineVirtualCamera |

## Event System

### Pattern: C# Action Delegates (primary)
Most inter-system communication uses `Action` / `Action<T>`:

| Manager | Key Events |
|---------|------------|
| **PlayerInteraction** | `onUse`, `onTake`, `onDrop`, `onThrow`, `onSell`, `onClose`, `onRotate`, `onHoldingStateChanged`, `onMap`, `onOnlineOrder` (20+ events) |
| **MoneyManager** | `onMoneyTransition`, `onDisabled` |
| **DayCycleManager** | `OnTimeChanged`, `OnFullHour`, `OnDayFinished`, `OnStartedNewDay` |
| **EmployeeManager** | `onCashierHired`, `onRestockerHired`, `onIceCreamHelperHired`, `onRestockerFired` |
| **VehicleManager** | `onVehicleBought`, `onVehicleReset`, `onEnterVehicle`, `onExitVehicle`, `VehicleRemoved` |
| **PriceManager** | `onPriceSet`, `onSaleSignSet`, `onCostsChanged` |
| **SectionManager** | `onSectionPositionChanged`, `onSectionPurchased`, `onSectionPurchasedAnimated` |
| **ProductLicenseManager** | `onLicensePurchased` |
| **InventoryManager** | `OnProductPurchased`, `OnInventoryChanged`, `OnPurchaseCompleted` |
| **CheckoutManager** | `onCheckoutCompleted`, `onSelfCheckoutCountChanged` |
| **StoreLevelManager** | `onPointChanged`, `onLevelChanged` |
| **ExpensesManager** | `OnBillDataChanged` |
| **BankManager** | `onTakenLoan`, `onCompletedLoan`, `OnLoanBillDataChanged` |
| **OrderManager** | `OrderIssued`, `OrderRemoved`, `OrderDelivered` |
| **BakeryManager** | `OnOvenAdded`, `OnOvenRemoved`, `OnOvenBakeFinished` |
| **ScaleManager** | `ScaleRemoved`, `ScaleCountChanged`, `ScaleBarcodeCreated/Applied` |
| **CCTVManager** | `OnShoplifterDeteched`, `OnSecurityGuardFired` |
| **WholeSaleManager** | `onWholesaleOfferWarningRaised`, `onWholesaleOfferAccepted/Declined` |
| **ScannerDevice** | `onTabletOpened`, `onTabletClosed`, `OnAddedItem`, `OnRemoveItem` |
| **FurniturePlacer** | `OnFurniturePlaced`, `OnFurnitureBoxUp`, `OnFurnitureStartPlacingMode` |

### Pattern: EventHandler (C# standard)
- `ScaleManager` uses `EventHandler` delegates for scale-related events

### Pattern: Photon RPC
- Network sync uses `[PunRPC]` methods across most managers
- Common pattern: `MethodName_RPC()` or `MethodName_Broadcast()`
- `PriceManager`, `CartManager`, `DayCycleManager`, `NetworkManager` are multiplayer-first

---

## Data Flow

```
ScriptableObjects (ProductSO, FurnitureSO, DisplaySO, RackSO, CheckoutSO, BoxSO)
        │
        ▼
Runtime Data Containers (BoxData, DisplayData, RackData, CartData, VendingData, etc.)
        │
        ▼
Manager Singletons (InventoryManager, DisplayManager, RackManager, etc.)
        │
        ├──► SaveManager (ES3 persistence)
        ├──► Network (Photon RPC sync)
        └──► UI (Canvas, TMP_Text, Sliders)
```

### SO → Runtime → Manager Pattern
1. `ProductSO` defines product properties (price, icon, grid layout, category)
2. `Product` MonoBehaviour instances created at runtime from SO data
3. `InventoryManager` tracks product counts in displays/vending
4. `PriceManager` manages per-product pricing (player-set + dynamic)
5. `SaveManager.ProgressionContainer` serializes runtime state to disk

### Player Input Flow
```
InputActions (Unity InputSystem) → PlayerInteraction (20+ Action delegates)
    → Specific Interaction classes (BoxInteraction, CheckoutInteraction, etc.)
        → Target IInteractable → Game state changes → Manager updates
```

---

## Inheritance Chains

### Worth Preserving
```
ScriptableObject
├── ProductSO
├── FurnitureSO
│   ├── DisplaySO
│   ├── RackSO
│   └── CheckoutSO
├── BoxSO
├── ProductLicenseSO
├── CustomerStrategySO
├── CustomerSpawnSettingSO
├── ExpensesSO
├── LightingPresetsSO
└── BankCreditSO

MonoBehaviour
├── NoktaSingleton<T> → (39+ managers)
├── NoktaSingletonPunCallbacks<T> → (PriceManager, CartManager, NetworkManager, MissionSystem)
├── Interaction (abstract)
│   ├── BoxInteraction
│   ├── CheckoutInteraction
│   ├── DisplayInteraction
│   ├── FurnitureInteraction
│   ├── OnlineOrderInteraction
│   └── (others)
└── MonoBehaviourPunCallbacks
    ├── PlayerInteraction
    ├── NPC
    └── PlayerInstance
```

### Consider Flattening
- `ShoplifterTutorialCustomer` duplicates most of `Customer` behavior — candidate for composition
- Multiple character customization classes (`BWomanCustomise`, `BmanCustomize`, `BigGuy_CharCustomize`, etc.) share identical patterns

## Summary

| Metric | Value |
|--------|-------|
| **Total game code files** | ~1,025 |
| **Files requiring rebuild** | ~635 (excluding third-party mirrors) |
| **Estimated hours** | ~453 |
| **Estimated weeks (40h/wk)** | ~11.3 |
| **Highest risk phases** | Phase 8 (Customer AI), Phase 9 (Employee AI), Phase 19 (Multiplayer) |
| **Most complex files** | Restocker.cs, Customer.cs, Checkout.cs, OnboardingManager.cs, MissionSystem.cs |

### Risk Factors
- **Multiplayer**: 50+ Network* wrappers make every change potentially break sync
- **Customer AI**: Shopping behavior is the core loop — most breakage risk
- **God Objects**: 10 files > 6 KB need splitting before rebuild
- **Singleton Coupling**: 39 singletons with direct Instance calls — gradual decoupling needed

# GOAL — smarket (Supermarket Simulator)

> Target architecture for the rebuilt project. All new code follows these rules.

---

## 1. Project Identity

- **Project**: smarket (Supermarket Simulator)
- **Engine**: Unity 6+ (URP)
- **Language**: C# 12+ (latest Unity-supported)
- **Phases**: 20 (see PhaseMap.md)
- **Networking**: Photon PUN 2 (preserve existing — no migration)
- **Save System**: Easy Save 3 (preserve existing)

---

## 2. Folder Structure

```
Assets/
├── _smarket/
│   ├── _-PlayerSystem/
│   ├── _-EconomySystem/
│   ├── _-StoreSystem/
│   ├── _-DayCycleSystem/
│   ├── _-ProductSystem/
│   ├── _-InventorySystem/
│   ├── _-FurnitureSystem/
│   ├── _-DisplaySystem/
│   ├── _-RackSystem/
│   ├── _-CheckoutSystem/
│   ├── _-CustomerSystem/
│   ├── _-EmployeeSystem/
│   ├── _-BakerySystem/
│   ├── _-IceCreamSystem/
│   ├── _-ScaleSystem/
│   ├── _-VendingSystem/
│   ├── _-SecuritySystem/
│   ├── _-OrderSystem/
│   ├── _-MissionSystem/
│   ├── _-VehicleSystem/
│   ├── _-AudioSystem/
│   ├── _-NetworkSystem/
│   ├── _-UISystem/
│   ├── _Core/
│   │   ├── Singletons/
│   │   ├── Interfaces/
│   │   ├── Math/
│   │   ├── Grid/
│   │   ├── Data/
│   │   └── Util/
│   └── _ThirdParty/
│       ├── Gley/
│       ├── Pathfinding/
│       ├── PG/
│       ├── VLB/
│       ├── Gadd420/
│       ├── NodeCanvas/
│       ├── Koenigz/
│       ├── LayerLab/
│       ├── ShellanderGames/
│       └── Photon/
├── Resources/
├── Scenes/
└── StreamingAssets/
```

### Rules
- Each `_-*System/` is self-contained with its own scripts, SOs, prefabs
- Cross-system communication goes through interfaces or events, never direct singleton references (target state)
- Third-party code stays untouched in `_ThirdParty/`

---

## 3. Naming Conventions

| Category | Prefix | Example |
|----------|--------|---------|
| ScriptableObject definition | `SO_` | `SO_Product`, `SO_Furniture`, `SO_Checkout` |
| Runtime data wrapper | `W_` | `W_BoxData`, `W_DisplayData` |
| Serialized field class | `Field_` | `Field_SpawnSettings` |
| Interface | `I` | `IInteractable`, `IEmployee`, `IBoostable` |
| Abstract base | no prefix | `Interaction`, `NoktaSingleton<T>` |
| Manager (singleton) | `*Manager` | `MoneyManager`, `CustomerManager` |
| Network wrapper | `Network*` | `NetworkBox`, `NetworkCheckout` |
| Enum | PascalCase | `CheckoutType`, `DisplayType`, `ExpenseType` |
| Event field | `On*` or `on*` | `OnDayFinished`, `onMoneyTransition` |

---

## 4. Class Responsibilities

### MonoBehaviour — Scene presence only
- Holds `[SerializeField]` references to scene objects
- Calls into DataService for logic
- Subscribes to events in `OnEnable`, unsubscribes in `OnDisable`
- Never contains business logic > 20 lines

### DataService — Pure C# logic
- No MonoBehaviour, no Unity lifecycle
- Receives data, returns results
- Testable without Unity runtime
- Examples: `PriceCalculationService`, `InventoryTrackingService`, `OrderGenerationService`

### ScriptableObject — Configuration
- Immutable at runtime (read-only definitions)
- Prefixed with `SO_`
- Contains: IDs, names, costs, prefab refs, curves, layout data

### Singleton Manager — System orchestration
- Extends `NoktaSingleton<T>` (preserve existing pattern)
- Owns system-wide state
- Dispatches events for cross-system communication
- **Target**: Reduce from 39 singletons toward event-bus decoupling

---

## 5. Decoupling Patterns

### Current State (problems to address)
- 39 singletons with direct `Instance.Method()` calls everywhere
- `Customer.cs` (18 KB) directly references `DisplaySlot`, `Checkout`, `Product`
- `BoxInteraction.cs` references 6+ different systems
- `PlayerInteraction.cs` holds 20+ Action delegates (god event hub)

### Target Patterns

#### Event Bus (phase-local)
```csharp
// Instead of: MoneyManager.Instance.MoneyTransition(amount, type)
// Use: EventBus<MoneyTransactionEvent>.Raise(new MoneyTransactionEvent { ... })
```

#### Interface-based Cross-System
```csharp
// Instead of: Restocker directly referencing DisplaySlot
// Use: IRestockTarget interface implemented by DisplaySlot, RackSlot, VendingSlot
public interface IRestockTarget {
    bool NeedRefill();
    void PlaceProduct(Product product);
    Transform InteractionPosition { get; }
}
```

#### Service Locator for Managers (migration path)
Gradually replace `Singleton.Instance` with registered services while preserving existing `NoktaSingleton` as fallback.

---

## 6. Lifecycle Rules

### Initialization Order
1. `NoktaSingleton` instances created (Awake)
2. SaveManager loads data (Start)
3. Managers subscribe to events (OnEnable)
4. DayCycleManager starts time progression
5. CustomerManager begins spawning

### Day Cycle
```
DayCycleManager.OnStartedNewDay → all systems reset daily state
DayCycleManager.OnTimeChanged → lighting updates, spawn rate changes
DayCycleManager.OnDayFinished → DailyStatisticsManager tallies, ExpensesManager bills, SaveManager auto-save
```

### Network Lifecycle
- Master client: authoritative for customer spawning, time sync, pricing
- Non-master: receives RPC updates, can interact locally
- `_Order()` suffix = authoritative method (master only)
- `_RPC()` suffix = network broadcast
- `_Broadcast()` suffix = notify all clients

---

## 7. C# Features to Use

| Feature | Usage |
|---------|-------|
| `record` | Immutable data transfer objects (event payloads) |
| `init` properties | SO data that shouldn't change after creation |
| `switch` expressions | State machine transitions, enum mapping |
| `pattern matching` | Type checking in interaction systems |
| `nullable reference types` | Prevent null reference issues in manager lookups |
| `string interpolation` | Money formatting, debug logging |
| `ValueTuple` | Multi-return from service methods |
| `Span<T>` | Performance-critical array operations (grid calculations) |
| `readonly struct` | Grid positions, transform data |

---

## 8. Testing Strategy

### Unit Tests (DataService layer)
- `PriceCalculationService` — profit rate, purchase chance
- `InventoryTrackingService` — product count, occupation
- `OrderGenerationService` — fee calculation, item selection
- `LoanCalculationService` — repayment, late fees
- `GridCalculationService` — layout positions

### Integration Tests (MonoBehaviour)
- Customer shopping flow: spawn → pick products → queue → checkout → leave
- Box flow: delivery → open → place products → dispose
- Day cycle: time progression → lighting → statistics → new day

### Manual Verification
- Each phase has "What It Looks Like When Running" in PhaseMap.md
- Use as acceptance criteria

---

## 9. Project-Specific Details

### Enums Found in Source
- `CheckoutType` — Regular, Self
- `DisplayType` — Product display categories
- `DisplaySubType` — Furniture sub-categories
- `ExpenseType` — Bills, Rent, Staff, etc.
- `BoxSize` — Box dimensions
- `CustomerGender` — Male, Female
- `CustomerSpeechType` — Speech bubble categories
- `InteractionType` — Instant, Holding, Custom, Repair
- `InteractactableType` — Object interaction categories
- `LoanStatus` — Active, Completed, Overdue
- `PlayerPaymentType` — Cash, Card
- `PlayerState` — Player state machine
- `CheckoutGridSize` — Belt grid dimensions
- `SortState` / `SortResult` — Box sorting
- `MoneyManager.TransitionType` — CHECKOUT_INCOME, SUPPLY_COSTS, UPGRADE_COSTS, RENT, BILLS, LOAN_INCOME, LOAN_PAYMENT, STAFF, FURNITURE_SALE, CUSTOMIZATION, FURNITURE_SELL, GAS, VENDING_MACHINE

### Tags & Layers
- InteractableLayer (PlayerInteraction raycast)
- FurniturePlacingLayer (FurniturePlacer raycast)
- BoxInteractionLayer (BoxInteraction raycast)
- Various collision layers for vehicles, NPCs, player

### Utility Extensions (from Extensions.cs)
- `string.RandomString()` — random name generation
- `float.ToMoneyText()` — currency formatting
- `string.Raw()` — raw localization string
- `List<T>.AddUnique()` — safe add
- `List<T>.SafeRemove()` — null-safe remove
- `CanvasGroup.OpenAnimation()` — fade in/out
- `DisplayType.Localize()` — localized display names
- `InteractionType.Has*Interaction()` — interaction type checks

---

## 10. Key Architecture Decisions

### Preserve
- `NoktaSingleton<T>` pattern (used by 35+ managers — migration cost too high)
- Photon PUN 2 networking (deeply integrated, 50+ Network* wrappers)
- Easy Save 3 for persistence
- `IInteractable` interface contract (InstantInteract, HoldingInteract, CustomInteract, RepairInteract)
- ScriptableObject data architecture (ProductSO, FurnitureSO hierarchy)
- Abstract `Interaction` base class pattern

### Refactor
- Split god objects: `Restocker.cs` (22.4 KB), `Customer.cs` (18 KB), `Checkout.cs` (11.3 KB)
- Extract business logic from MonoBehaviours into DataServices
- Consolidate 8+ duplicate character customization classes into shared `ICharacterModel`
- Standardize event naming (mix of `on*`, `On*`, no prefix)
- Add `IEmployee` interface to unify Cashier/Restocker/Janitor/SecurityGuard/Baker patterns

### Avoid
- Do NOT migrate away from Photon PUN (too deeply embedded)
- Do NOT replace NoktaSingleton with DI container (incremental improvement instead)
- Do NOT refactor third-party code (Gley, Pathfinding, VLB, PG, Gadd420)
- Do NOT change save format (ES3 compatibility critical for existing saves)

## Cross-Phase Modification Table

| Phase Modified | Triggered By Phase | Modification |
|----------------|-------------------|-------------|
| Phase 3 (Economy) | Phase 7 (Checkout) | MoneyManager receives checkout income |
| Phase 3 (Economy) | Phase 9 (Employee) | ExpensesManager adds staff wages |
| Phase 5 (Products) | Phase 6 (Display) | Product instances placed on DisplaySlots |
| Phase 5 (Products) | Phase 8 (Customer) | Customer takes products from display |
| Phase 6 (Display) | Phase 9 (Employee) | Restocker fills DisplaySlots from Boxes |
| Phase 7 (Checkout) | Phase 8 (Customer) | Customer queues and pays at Checkout |
| Phase 7 (Checkout) | Phase 9 (Employee) | Cashier scans at Checkout |
| Phase 4 (Store) | Phase 8 (Customer) | DayCycleManager triggers customer spawn |
| Phase 4 (Store) | Phase 3 (Economy) | Day end → daily statistics + expenses |
| Phase 5 (Products) | Phase 10 (Bakery) | Baked products added to inventory |
| Phase 5 (Products) | Phase 13 (Vending) | Products placed in VendingSlots |
| Phase 8 (Customer) | Phase 14 (Security) | Shoplifter detected by SecurityCamera/Antenna |
| Phase 9 (Employee) | Phase 14 (Security) | SecurityGuard chases Shoplifter |
| Phase 5 (Products) | Phase 15 (Orders) | Online orders reference ProductSO |
| Phase 3 (Economy) | Phase 15 (Orders) | Wholesale affects MoneyManager |
| Phase 1-20 | Phase 19 (Network) | Every system gets Network* wrapper for multiplayer |

<!-- ==== FILE: LEARN/smarket/StructureMap.md ==== -->
# StructureMap — smarket (Supermarket Simulator)

> For each phase: which scripts become `_-Systems/` folders, DataService candidates, interface candidates, and prefix assignments.

---

## Phase 1 — Core Infrastructure

### Systems
No `_-Systems/` folders — these are foundational utilities.

### Structure
```
_Core/
├── Singletons/
│   ├── NoktaSingleton.cs           → kept as-is (generic base)
│   └── NoktaSingletonPunCallbacks.cs → kept as-is (network base)
├── Interfaces/
│   ├── IInteractable.cs
│   ├── IPlacingMode.cs
│   ├── IPlacementArea.cs
│   ├── IPlacementAreaObject.cs
│   ├── IPlacementAreaPhysicsBody.cs
│   ├── IPurchasable.cs
│   ├── IPurchaser.cs
│   ├── ILoader.cs
│   ├── IHoldDuration.cs
│   ├── IAimHint.cs
│   ├── IAttachment.cs
│   └── ITutorial.cs
├── Math/
│   ├── FMath.cs
│   ├── CriticallyDamped.cs
│   ├── Spring.cs
│   └── Slerp.cs
├── Grid/
│   ├── GridPoint.cs
│   ├── GridLayout3D.cs
│   ├── BoxGridLayout3D.cs
│   └── TransformCalculators (Default, Display, ProduceStall, VendingMachine)
├── Data/
│   ├── TransformData.cs
│   ├── InstanceData.cs
│   └── InstanceBoundsData.cs
└── Util/
    ├── Extensions.cs
    ├── IDManager.cs
    ├── CustomTypeCodes.cs
    └── EditorPrefsStrings.cs
```

### DataService Candidates
- **GridCalculationService** — Extract grid/transform calculations into pure C# (no MonoBehaviour)
- **MathService** — `FMath`, `CriticallyDamped`, `Spring`, `Slerp` already pure C#

### Interface Candidates
All interfaces already defined. No new interfaces needed.

### Prefix Assignments
- No SO_ prefixes (no ScriptableObjects)
- No Field_ prefixes (no serialized data wrappers)
- No W_ prefixes (no runtime wrappers)

---

## Phase 2 — Input & Player Foundation

### Systems → `_-PlayerSystem/`
3+ tightly coupled files: PlayerInstance, PlayerController, PlayerInteraction, FirstPersonController, PlayerObjectHolder, PlayerAnimation, InputActions

```
_-PlayerSystem/
├── PlayerInstance.cs
├── PlayerController.cs
├── PlayerInteraction.cs
├── FirstPersonController.cs
├── PlayerObjectHolder.cs
├── PlayerAnimation.cs
├── PlayerIKHandler.cs
├── PlayerManager.cs            (singleton)
├── PlayerScaleController.cs
├── PlayerState.cs
├── InputActions.cs
├── InputActionID.cs
├── InputActionName.cs
├── InputSystemUtil.cs
├── Skin/
│   ├── PlayerSkin.cs
│   ├── PlayerSkinController.cs
│   └── PlayerSkinNetwork.cs
└── UI/
    ├── PlayerAimCanvas.cs
    ├── PlayerCrosshairManager.cs
    └── CrosshairReference.cs
```

### DataService Candidates
- **InputMappingService** — Pure C# input action name→ID mapping (currently in `InputActionID`, `InputActionName`)

### Interface Candidates
- `IPushable` — already on FirstPersonController, could be extracted for reuse

### Prefix Assignments
- None needed — player system uses MonoBehaviour-based architecture

---

## Phase 3 — Economy & Data Layer

### Systems → `_-EconomySystem/`

```
_-EconomySystem/
├── MoneyManager.cs             (singleton)
├── Money.cs
├── MoneyPack.cs
├── MoneyGenerator.cs
├── MoneyText.cs
├── MoneyInputRestrictor.cs
├── Pricing/
│   ├── PriceManager.cs         (singleton)
│   ├── PriceTag.cs
│   ├── Pricing.cs
│   ├── PricingItem.cs
│   ├── PricingInteraction.cs
│   ├── PricingProductViewer.cs
│   ├── PricingSorting*.cs
│   ├── PriceChangeNotification.cs
│   ├── PriceEvaluationManager.cs  (singleton)
│   ├── DynamicPriceProduct.cs
│   ├── DiscountManager.cs      (singleton)
│   └── DiscountPanel.cs
├── Bank/
│   ├── BankManager.cs          (singleton)
│   ├── SO_BankCredit.cs        (was BankCreditSO)
│   ├── LoanData.cs
│   ├── LoanItem.cs
│   ├── LoanStatus.cs
│   ├── BankruptcyManager.cs    (singleton)
│   └── BankruptcyCanvas.cs
├── Expenses/
│   ├── ExpensesManager.cs      (singleton)
│   ├── SO_Expenses.cs          (was ExpensesSO)
│   ├── ExpenseType.cs
│   ├── BillItem.cs
│   ├── BillsTab.cs
│   ├── AutoPaymentManager.cs
│   └── AutoPaidBillsCanvas.cs
├── Statistics/
│   ├── DailyStatisticsManager.cs  (singleton)
│   ├── DailyStatisticsData.cs
```

## Phase 17–20 — Remaining Phases

Phase 17 (Vehicle), Phase 18 (Audio), Phase 19 (Multiplayer), Phase 20 (UI) follow the same pattern:
- Tightly coupled files (3+) → `_-Systems/` folder
- Pure logic → DataService extraction
- Cross-system contracts → Interface candidates
- ScriptableObjects → `SO_` prefix

### Key System Folders
- `_-VehicleSystem/` — VehicleManager + controllers + gas + traffic
- `_-AudioSystem/` — SFXManager + MusicPlayerManager + Speaker
- `_-NetworkSystem/` — All Network* wrappers + Photon sync
- `_-UISystem/` — Menus, popups, settings, computer/tablet, minimap, warnings

<!-- ==== FILE: LEARN/smarket/SystemPortabilityMap.md ==== -->
# SystemPortabilityMap — smarket (Supermarket Simulator)

> Classification of each system's portability level for extraction and reuse.

## Portability Levels

| Level | Definition |
|-------|-----------|
| **L0** | Unity-independent. Pure C# logic. Can compile outside Unity. |
| **L1** | Unity-dependent but project-independent. Reusable across Unity projects. |
| **L2** | Project-coupled. Depends on smarket-specific types, singletons, or data shapes. |
| **L3** | Deeply entangled. Requires significant refactoring before extraction. |

---

## System Classifications

### Phase 1 — Core Infrastructure

| File/Module | Current | Target | Notes |
|-------------|---------|--------|-------|
| `NoktaSingleton<T>` | L1 | L1 | Already generic. Unity-only (MonoBehaviour). |
| `NoktaSingletonPunCallbacks<T>` | L2 | L1 | Photon dependency. Extractable with interface. |
| `Extensions.cs` utility methods | L0/L2 | L0 | `RandomString`, `AddUnique`, `SafeRemove` are L0. `ToMoneyText`, `OpenAnimation` are L2. Split. |
| `Grid*` classes | L1 | L0 | Math-heavy. Extract pure calculation to L0. |
| Interfaces (`IInteractable`, etc.) | L1 | L0 | Pure contracts. Move to L0 DataService layer. |

### Phase 2 — Input & Player

| File/Module | Current | Target | Notes |
|-------------|---------|--------|-------|
| `PlayerInteraction` | L3 | L2 | 20+ event delegates, 6+ system refs. God object. |
| `PlayerMovement` | L2 | L1 | Standard FPS controller. Decouple from smarket-specific. |
| `PlayerNetwork` | L3 | L2 | Photon PUN specific. |

### Phase 3 — Economy

| File/Module | Current | Target | Notes |
|-------------|---------|--------|-------|
| Price calculation logic | L3 | L0 | Currently in `MoneyManager`. Extract to `PriceCalculationService`. |
| Profit rate formulas | L3 | L0 | In `ProductSO` + `PriceManager`. Extract to service. |
| `LoanData` / loan math | L2 | L0 | Basic financial math. |
| `MoneyManager` | L3 | L2 | Singleton orchestrator. Keep as L2, extract logic to L0 services. |

### Phase 4 — Store & Day Cycle

| File/Module | Current | Target | Notes |
|-------------|---------|--------|-------|
| Day/time math | L3 | L0 | Currently baked in `DayCycleManager`. |
| Weather system | L2 | L1 | ScriptableObject driven. |
| Lighting transitions | L2 | L1 | URP-specific but project-independent. |

### Phase 5 — Products & Inventory

| File/Module | Current | Target | Notes |
|-------------|---------|--------|-------|
| `ProductSO` data model | L2 | L1 | SO definition. Generic enough. |
| Inventory counting logic | L3 | L0 | Extract from managers to `InventoryTrackingService`. |
| Box system | L3 | L2 | `BoxInteraction` references 6+ systems. |
| Product label generation | L2 | L1 | Text formatting logic. |

### Phase 6 — Furniture, Display & Rack

| File/Module | Current | Target | Notes |
|-------------|---------|--------|-------|
| Placement system (grid snapping) | L3 | L1 | Grid math extractable. Placement logic Unity-bound. |
| `FurnitureSO` hierarchy | L2 | L1 | SO definitions. |
| Display slot logic | L3 | L2 | Tightly coupled to product + customer systems. |
| Rack slot logic | L3 | L2 | Similar to display. |

### Phase 7 — Checkout

| File/Module | Current | Target | Notes |

| Level | Current Count | Target Count |
|-------|--------------|-------------|
| L0 (Pure C#) | ~5% | ~25% |
| L1 (Unity-generic) | ~15% | ~30% |
| L2 (Project-coupled) | ~25% | ~35% |
| L3 (Entangled) | ~55% | ~10% |

# surfer — smarket (Supermarket Simulator)

> Prompt log. Each entry records what was done and what changed.

---

## Prompt 1 — Initial Source Analysis

**Action**: Full project analysis via `init.prompt.md` workflow.

**Read**:
- `entire-smarket.stub` (22,598 files, 10.234 GB)
- 80+ .cs files across all systems (managers, customer, employee, checkout, display, network, etc.)
- Assembly definitions, third-party code identification

**Generated**:
- `ARCHITECTURE.md` — Dependency graph, god objects, singleton registry, coupling hotspots, event system, data flow, inheritance chains, external packages, asset inventory
- `PhaseMap.md` — 20 phases ordered by dependency with file lists, difficulty ratings, visual acceptance criteria
- `StructureMap.md` — Per-phase _-System/ folder layouts, DataService candidates, interface candidates, SO_ prefix assignments
- `GOAL.md` — Architecture rules, naming conventions, class responsibilities, decoupling patterns, lifecycle rules, C# features, testing strategy
- `Estimate.md` — ~453 hours across 20 phases (~11.3 weeks at 40h/wk)
- `SystemPortabilityMap.md` — L0-L3 classification per system, priority extractions to pure C#
- `surfer.md` — This file

**Key Findings**:
- 1,025 game code files + 571 third-party = 1,596 total .cs files
- 39 singletons (NoktaSingleton pattern)
- 10 god objects > 6 KB (Restocker 22.4 KB, Customer 18 KB, Checkout 11.3 KB largest)
- 50+ Network* Photon wrappers
- 25+ external packages (A* Pathfinding, Gley Traffic, PG Car Physics, VLB, DOTween, etc.)
- 55% of codebase currently L3 (entangled) — target 10%

# ARCHITECTURE — twFactory (Tower Factory)

## Source Overview

| Metric | Value |
|---|---|
| **Game Scripts** | 554 `.cs` files |
| **Total Lines** | ~49,000 |
| **Engine** | Unity 6 (URP, Input System, Addressables, Localization) |
| **Code Folder** | `Scripts/Assembly-CSharp/` |
| **Sub-Folders** | `HighlightPlus/` (third-party), `TMPro/` (third-party), `LayerLab/` (third-party), `LightTower/` (game namespace), `Properties/` |
| **Scenes** | GameScene, LoadingScreen, MainMenu, Tutorial |

### Folder Structure (Assembly-CSharp)
```
Assembly-CSharp/
├── (root)          — 500+ game scripts (flat, no sub-grouping)
├── HighlightPlus/  — Third-party highlight/selection plugin (~25 files)
├── TMPro/          — TextMeshPro examples (1 file)
├── LayerLab/       — Third-party UI theme plugin (2 files)
├── LightTower/     — Game namespace: Tile, PathTile, Path, EnemyMovement, EnemyController (5 files)
└── Properties/     — AssemblyInfo.cs
```

## Singleton Registry

| Singleton | What It Owns | Who Reads It |
|---|---|---|
| **GameManager.instance** | Player character/controller refs, pause state | LTFunctionLibrary, AudioSystem, SettingsElement_keyRebind, LevelController |
| **AudioSystem.Instance** | Audio source pool, mixer volumes, pause state | ~50+ classes (towers, enemies, UI, buildings) |
| **SaveSystem.instance** | Save profiles, serialized data, file I/O | LevelsProgressionManager, PlayerUpgradesManager, GameplayEffectsComponent, SessionChecker, SpawnersManager |
| **SpawnersManager.instance** | Active round/wave spawners, enemy tracking | CycleTimeUI, GE_GiveEffectToEnemy, LTFunctionLibrary |
| **FogOfWarController.instance** | FOW render texture, camera, visibility checks | PlacementComponent, CombatComponent, TooltipManager, Grid, EnemyController, Beacon, AreaExtractor |
| **SettingsController.instance** | All game settings (resolution, volume, controls) | LTPlayerController, AudioSystem, many UI classes |
| **PlayerUpgradesManager.instance** | Player upgrades, money, unlock state | LTFunctionLibrary, PlayerData, LevelsProgressionManager, EnvironmentGenerator |
| **LevelsProgressionManager.instance** | Level completion/unlock state, boss rewards | LTHUD, LTGameManager_Campaign, NewGameMenuUI |
| **GameStatsManager.instance** | Damage reports, kill counts, resource stats | EndGameInfoUI, SteamAchievements |
| **MatchInfo.instance** | Current match settings, level data, match mode | LTPlayerController, SpawnerConfig, Spawner, many UI/game classes |
| **ConveyorBeltSystem.instance** | All belt groups, resource tick coroutine | ConveyorBelt, ConveyorBeltGroup |
| **LTAssetsReferences.instance** | ID→asset lookups (objects, resources, gems, effects, enemies) | Storage_ResourceData, GameplayEffectsComponent, GemsComponent |

---

## Coupling Hotspots

### Service Locator Pattern — LTFunctionLibrary
`LTFunctionLibrary` is a static class that wraps singleton access for ~20 managers. Nearly every game class calls it instead of directly accessing singletons. This centralizes coupling but makes the locator itself a dependency magnet.

**References (accessed through LTFunctionLibrary):**
- `GetLTGameManager()` → `GameManager.instance as LTGameManager`
- `GetPlayerData()` → `LTGameManager.PlayerData`
- `GetPlayerInventory()` → `PlayerData.Inventory`
- `GetGrid()` → `LTLevelController.Grid`
- `GetSpawnersManager()` → `SpawnersManager.instance`
- `GetFogOfWarController()` → `FogOfWarController.instance`
- `GetPlayerUpgradesManager()` → `PlayerUpgradesManager.instance`
- `GetLevelsProgressionManager()` → `LevelsProgressionManager.instance`
- `GetTimeManager()`, `GetCyclesManager()`, `GetGameStatsManager()`, etc.

### Direct Cross-Domain References
| From | To | Via |
|---|---|---|
| Tower | Enemy | TowerCombatComponent damage events |
| Extractor | Source | Direct reference + event subscription |
| ConveyorBelt | Grid | PlacementComponent + GridCell lookup |
| GE_ effects | TowerCombatComponent | onDamageEnemy event subscription |
| PlayerTower | ConveyorBelt_storage | Belt resource forwarding |
| Beacon | FogOfWarController | Direct instance access for area reveal |
| Obelisk | Tower | Applies GE when tower placed adjacent |
| SpawnersManager | Enemy | Tracks spawned enemies, death events |

### Static Instance Access (not through LTFunctionLibrary)
- `AudioSystem.Instance` — called directly by ~50+ classes
- `FogOfWarController.instance` — direct access by PlacementComponent, CombatComponent, Grid
- `SaveSystem.instance` — direct access by persistence classes
- `ConveyorBeltSystem.instance` — direct access by ConveyorBelt

---

## Event System

### Pattern: C# Delegates/Actions (primary pattern — no UnityEvents in game logic)

**Major Event Hubs:**

| Hub | Events | Subscribers |
|---|---|---|
| **LTGameManager** | `onGameStarted`, `onGameEnded`, `onGameOver`, `onVictoryAnimationStarted`, `onGameOverAnimationStarted`, `onShowGridChanged`, `onPause`, `onResume` | MusicManager, CyclesManager, TimeManager, PlayerTower, PlayerData, Trader, SpawnersManager, DayNightCycle, AudioSystem |
| **CyclesManager** | `onCycleChanged(int, ECycleMode)` | SpawnersManager, MusicManager, DayNightCycle, Trader, CycleTimeUI, SnowfallController, SteamAchievements |
| **StatsComponent** | `onStatChanged(EStats, float, float)` | Processor, Extractor, ConveyorBelt, CombatComponent, Tower, PlayerTower, PlayerData, ActiveAbility |
| **PlacementComponent** | `onPlace`, `onUnplace`, `onChangePosition`, `onDestroyAndSubstitute`, `onBecomeVisible` | Tower, Extractor, Processor, ConveyorBelt, Beacon, CrystalFinder, ResourceActivatedBuilding, LightBomb |
| **CombatComponent** | `onDamageTaken`, `onHealthChanged`, `onDie` | Enemy, WaveSpawner, SpawnersManager, AbilityManager, PlayerTower |
| **TowerCombatComponent** | `onPreDamageEnemy`, `onDamageEnemy` | GE_Splash, GE_ProjectileBounce, GE_ProjectileSplit, GE_DirectDamageChain, GE_GameplayEffectApplier, GE_StacksConsumer, GE_LifeBasedDamage, GE_AreaEffectSpawner, GameStatsManager |
| **PlayerData** | `onPlayerBuildingAdded/Removed`, `onPlayerTowerAdded/Removed`, `onEnemyEssenceAdded` | LTPlayerController, GameStatsManager, IdleManager |
| **SpawnersManager** | `onEnemySpawned`, `onBossSpawned`, `onEnemyDies` | GE_GiveEffectToEnemy, GameStatsManager |
| **LTPlayerController** | `onInputModeChanged`, `onPlayerInputLocked`, `onHotbarBankChanged`, `onHotbarActionChanged` | LTHUD, TooltipManager, many UI classes |
| **GameplayEffectsComponent** | `onEffectAdded`, `onEffectRemoved` | Processor, Extractor, Tower, SelectableUI |
| **SaveSystem** | `onSave`, `onPreLoad`, `onLoad`, `onProfilesChanged`, `onActiveProfileChanged` | All ISavable implementers |

---

## Data Flow

```
ScriptableObject (config) → Runtime Instance → Manager → UI

Examples:
  GameplayObjectData (SO) → GameplayObject (MonoBehaviour) → PlayerData.availableBuildings → StoreUI
  GameplayEffectData (SO) → GameplayEffect (runtime) → GameplayEffectsComponent → SelectableUI_tower
  SpawnerConfig (SO) → Spawner (MonoBehaviour) → SpawnersManager → CycleTimeUI
  LevelData (SO) → MatchInfo → LTGameManager → NewGameMenuUI
  ResourceData (SO) → Storage_ResourceData → PlayerData.Inventory → InventoryUI
  
Resource Flow:
  Source → Extractor → ConveyorBelt → Processor → ConveyorBelt → Storage_ResourceData (player inventory)
  Storage_ResourceData → Cost checks → Building/Tower placement
  
Combat Flow:
  TowerController.PerceptionAI → TowerTargetProvider → AbilityManager.UseAutoAttack →
  AutoAttack variant → Projectile/DirectDamage → TowerCombatComponent.DoDamageToEnemy →
  GE_ effects trigger (splash, bounce, DoT, etc.) → Enemy.CombatComponent.DoDamage
```

---

## Inheritance Chains

### Worth Preserving
```
MonoBehaviour
├── Character
│   ├── Enemy          (+ ISelectable, ISavable)
│   └── Tower          (+ ISelectable, ISampleableData, ISavable)
├── GameplayObject     (+ ISavable)
│   ├── Extractor
│   │   └── AreaExtractor (+ ISelectable)
│   ├── Processor
│   │   └── EssenceFactory
│   ├── ConveyorBelt
│   │   ├── ConveyorBelt_straight
│   │   ├── ConveyorBelt_curve
│   │   ├── ConveyorBelt_storage
│   │   ├── ConveyorBeltCombiner
│   │   ├── ConveyorBeltSplitter
│   │   ├── ConveyorBeltCrossing
│   │   └── ConveyorBeltUnderground
│   ├── Source
│   ├── PlayerTower
│   ├── EnemyTower     (+ ISelectable)
│   ├── LightBomb      (+ ISelectable)
│   └── ResourceActivatedBuilding (+ ISelectable, ISavable)
│       ├── PerkBeacon
│       └── SnowfallBeacon
├── Controller
│   ├── PlayerController
│   │   └── LTPlayerController
│   ├── TowerController
│   └── EnemyController (LightTower namespace)
├── CombatComponent
│   └── TowerCombatComponent
│       └── EnemyCombatComponent
├── InputMode
│   ├── StandardInputMode
│   ├── EditModeInputMode
│   └── BuyModeInputMode
├── MapObject (+ ISelectable)
│   ├── CrystalAltar
│   ├── Obelisk
│   └── Trader

ScriptableObject
├── GameplayObjectData (+ ISavable)
├── GameplayEffectData (+ ISavable) [abstract]
│   ├── GE_StatModifierData, GE_SlowData, GE_DotData, GE_SplashData, ...
│   └── (25+ concrete effect data classes)
├── SpawnerConfig
├── WaveSpawnerConfig
├── LevelData
├── LevelSpawners
├── CycleSpawners
├── MatchSettings
├── PlayerUpgrade
└── EnemyData

GameplayEffect [abstract]
├── GE_StatModifier, GE_Slow, GE_Dot
├── GE_Splash → GE_SplashDamage, GE_SplashGameplayEffectApplier
├── GE_StacksConsumer → GE_StacksConsumerDamage
└── (20+ concrete effect classes)

Ability [abstract, SerializedMonoBehaviour]
├── ActiveAbility [abstract]
│   ├── AutoAttack [abstract]
│   │   ├── TowerAutoAttack [abstract]
│   │   │   ├── AutoAttack_collisionCheck
│   │   │   ├── AutoAttack_directDamage
│   │   │   ├── AutoAttack_overTime → AutoAttack_overTime_laser
│   │   │   └── AutoAttack_projectile → AutoAttack_projectile_splash
│   │   └── EnemyAbility [abstract]
│   │       ├── EnemyAbility_applyGE
│   │       ├── EnemyAbility_spawnEnemies
│   │       └── EnemyAbility_targeting
│   └── (other active abilities)
└── PassiveAbility

Beacon (+ ISelectable, ISavable) → CircleBeacon, ConeBeacon, SquaredBeacon
├── Beacon_01 (: CircleBeacon)
├── Beacon_02 (: CircleBeacon)
├── Beacon_03 (: ConeBeacon)
└── Beacon_04 (: CircleBeacon)

SelectableUI [abstract]
├── SelectableUI_tower, SelectableUI_enemy, SelectableUI_processor
├── SelectableUI_extractor, SelectableUI_trader, SelectableUI_perkBeacon
├── SelectableUI_chest, SelectableUI_gemsChest, SelectableUI_goldenCoinsChest
├── SelectableUI_crystalAlatar, SelectableUI_crystalFinder
├── SelectableUI_enemyTower, SelectableUI_obelisk, SelectableUI_snowfallBeacon
└── SelectableUI_tower_gemUI

HUD → InGameHUD → LTHUD
HUD → MainMenuHUD → LTMainMenuHUD
HUDMenu → InGameUI, StoreUI, SettingsUI, etc.
```

### Consider Flattening
- `EssenceFactory` : `Processor` — only adds sound/particle on recipe completion; could be config
- `EnemyCombatComponent` : `TowerCombatComponent` : `CombatComponent` — 3-deep chain, EnemyCombatComponent adds nothing
- `AutoAttack_projectile_splash` : `AutoAttack_projectile` — minor override, could be config flag

| **Audio Mixer** | 5 groups | Master → Music, SFX, UI, Ambience |

### Key Enemy Types (from mesh/audio assets)
Skeleton, Mushroom, SoldierMushroom, Boss_mushroom, Bat, Bee, BeeWarrior, BattleBee, Boss_bee, Fishman, CrabMesh, HermitCrab, MantaRay, Salamander, BigPenguin, FlyingPenguin, Boss_penguin, BigSnowman, Boss_snowman, Yeti, BlackKnight, LizardWarrior, RatAssasin, Specter, Werewolf, Boss_naga, Boss_orc

### Key Tower Types (from mesh assets)
Ballista (3 tiers), Catapult (3 tiers), Bombard (3 tiers), Rockets (3 tiers), SawThrower (3 tiers), LightRay (3 tiers), TeslaCoil (3 tiers), Shockwave (3 tiers), Spikes (3 tiers), AcornCannon (3 tiers), ResinBarrel (3 tiers), SporeCannon (2 tiers), FlyingCannon (3 tiers)

### Building Types (from mesh assets)
Extractors: Wood (T1/T2), Stone (T1/T2)
Processors: Sawmill, Stonemason, KilnFurnace, Forge, Workshop, EssenceFactory
Conveyor Belts: Straight, Curve, Splitter, Combiner, Crossing, Underground (all T1/T2)
Special: Beacon (4 variants), PerkBeacon, SnowfallBeacon, CrystalAltar, CrystalFinder, Obelisk, MainTower, EnemyTower

# Estimate — Tower Factory (twFactory)

## Estimation Method

**Formula:** `Hours = FileCount × ComplexityTier × BaseHoursPerFile`

| Complexity Tier | Multiplier | Description |
|-----------------|-----------|-------------|
| Tier 1 (Simple) | 0.5h | Enums, data containers, small wrappers, one-liners |
| Tier 2 (Moderate) | 1.0h | Standard MonoBehaviours, clear single responsibility |
| Tier 3 (Complex) | 2.0h | Multi-responsibility, event-heavy, 200-500 lines |
| Tier 4 (God Object) | 4.0h | >500 lines, 3+ responsibilities, deep coupling |
| Tier 5 (Extreme) | 8.0h | >700 lines, cross-system orchestration, must split |

<!-- ==== FILE: LEARN/twFactory/GOAL.md ==== -->
# GOAL — Tower Factory (twFactory)

## Project Identity

- **Project Name:** Tower Factory
- **Engine:** Unity 6 (URP, Input System, Addressables, Localization, Cinemachine)
- **Genre:** Tower Defense + Factory Automation hybrid
- **Phases:** 12 (Core → Grid → Character → Tower → Effects → Enemy → Factory → Buildings → Flow → Player → UI → Audio)

---

## Target Architecture Rules

### 1. Folder Structure

```
twFactory-reimpl/
├── _-StatsSystem/           # Stat, StatModifier, StatsComponent
├── _-StorageSystem/         # Storage<T>, Storage_ResourceData
├── _-GameplayObjectBase/    # GameplayObject, GameplayObjectData, PlacementComponent
├── _-GridSystem/            # Grid, GridCell, Tile, PathTile, Path
├── _-MapGeneratorSystem/    # MapGenerator, PathGenerator, GroundGenerator, EnvironmentGenerator
├── _-FogOfWarSystem/        # FogOfWarController, FogOfWarArea
├── _-CharacterSystem/       # Character, Controller, MovementComponent, AnimationComponent
├── _-CombatSystem/          # CombatComponent, TowerCombatComponent, EnemyCombatComponent
├── _-AbilitySystem/         # Ability, ActiveAbility, AutoAttack, AbilityManager, AbilityQueue
├── _-FSMSystem/             # FSMComponent, FSMState, FSMCondition, FSMTask, FSMTransition
├── _-PerceptionSystem/      # PerceptionAI, PerceptionSense variants
├── _-GameplayEffectBase/    # GameplayEffect, GameplayEffectData, GameplayEffectsComponent
├── _-TowerSystem/           # Tower, TowerController, TowerAutoAttack, PlayerTower
├── _-AttackVariants/        # AutoAttack_directDamage, _projectile, _overTime, etc.
├── _-TargetProviderSystem/  # TowerTargetProvider + 10 concrete strategies
├── _-ProjectileSystem/      # Projectile, ProjectileMovement variants
├── _-AreaEffectSystem/      # AreaEffect, AreaEffectModule variants
├── _-GameplayEffects/       # All GE_ pairs (30+ files, flat folder)
├── _-GemSystem/             # GemsComponent, GemData, GemUI
├── _-EnemySystem/           # Enemy, EnemyData, EnemyMovement, EnemyController
├── _-EnemyAbilitySystem/    # EnemyAbility variants, EnemyAICondition variants
├── _-SpawnerSystem/         # Spawner, WaveSpawner, LTSpawner, CycleSpawners, SpawnersManager
├── _-ExtractorSystem/       # Extractor, AreaExtractor, audio, UI
├── _-ProcessorSystem/       # Processor, EssenceFactory, Recipe
├── _-ConveyorSystem/        # ConveyorBelt variants, ConveyorBeltGroup, ConveyorBeltSystem
├── _-IdleSystem/            # IdleDetector variants, IdleManager
├── _-BeaconSystem/          # Beacon hierarchy (Circle, Cone, Squared, Beacon_01-04)
├── _-SnowfallSystem/        # SnowfallController, SnowfallBeacon, VFX
├── _-GameManagerSystem/     # GameManager, LTGameManager variants, LTFunctionLibrary
├── _-SaveSystem/            # SaveSystem, SaveProfile, SessionChecker
├── _-ProgressionSystem/     # PlayerUpgrade, PlayerUpgradesManager, LevelsProgressionManager
├── _-InputModeSystem/       # InputMode, Standard/Edit/BuyModeInputMode
├── _-CameraSystem/          # Isometric, Top, SpringArm, Cinemachine, CameraShake
├── _-HotbarSystem/          # HotbarController, HotbarAction variants
├── _-HUDSystem/             # HUD, InGameHUD, LTHUD, MainMenuHUD
├── _-StoreSystem/           # StoreUI, StoreElementUI, info panels
├── _-SelectableUISystem/    # SelectableUI + 15 concrete variants
├── _-TooltipSystem/         # TooltipManager, TooltipUI/Component variants
├── _-MenuSystem/            # MainMenu, Pause, Settings, Profile, Credits
├── _-AudioSystem/           # AudioSystem, MusicManager, AmbienceManager
├── DataServices/            # Pure C# logic services (no MonoBehaviour)
├── Interfaces/              # Cross-system interfaces
├── SO/                      # ScriptableObject definitions
└── Enums/                   # All shared enums
```

### 2. Naming Conventions

| Prefix | Type | Example |
|--------|------|---------|
| `SO_` | ScriptableObject asset | `SO_GameplayObjectData`, `SO_LevelData` |
| `Field_` | Serialized data field | `Field_EStats`, `Field_ResourceType` |
| `W_` | Runtime wrapper | `W_GameplayEffect`, `W_SpawnerConfig` |
| `DS_` | DataService (pure C#) | `DS_ConveyorTransport`, `DS_Economy` |
| `I` | Interface | `ISelectable`, `ISavable`, `IDamageable` |
| `_-` | System folder | `_-TowerSystem/`, `_-ConveyorSystem/` |
| `GE_` | Gameplay effect | `GE_Splash`, `GE_Dot`, `GE_ProjectileBounce` |
| `TTP_` | Tower target provider | `TTP_Nearest`, `TTP_HighestHealth` |

### 3. Class Responsibilities

**MonoBehaviour classes:**
- Unity lifecycle only (Awake, Start, Update, OnDestroy)
- Delegate logic to DataServices
- Wire events in OnEnable, unwire in OnDisable
- No business logic in Update — call DataService methods

**DataService classes:**
- Pure C# (no MonoBehaviour inheritance)
- Stateless where possible, or explicitly manage state
- Testable without Unity runtime
- Injected via constructor or singleton registry

**ScriptableObject assets:**
- Configuration data only
- No runtime state
- Shared across instances via asset references

### 4. Decoupling Patterns

**Current Problem → Target Solution:**

| Current Pattern | Count | Target Pattern |
|-----------------|-------|---------------|
| `LTFunctionLibrary.GetXxx()` (service locator) | ~100+ calls | Keep as central accessor — acceptable pattern for this scale |
| `AudioSystem.Instance` (direct singleton) | ~50+ calls | Route through `LTFunctionLibrary.GetAudioSystem()` for consistency |
| `FogOfWarController.instance` (direct singleton) | ~10 calls | Route through `LTFunctionLibrary` |
| `ConveyorBeltSystem.instance` (direct singleton) | ~5 calls | Route through `LTFunctionLibrary` |
| `SaveSystem.instance` (direct singleton) | ~8 calls | Keep direct — persistence is cross-cutting |
| God objects >400 lines | 10 files | Split into DataService + thin MonoBehaviour |

**Acceptable static access (keep as-is):**
- `LTFunctionLibrary` service locator — centralized facade is the intended pattern
- `SaveSystem.instance` — persistence is legitimately cross-cutting
- `MatchInfo.instance` — match config is globally relevant

**Must decouple:**
- God objects: `LTPlayerController` (844 lines), `EnvironmentGenerator` (786 lines), `CycleSpawners` (737 lines), `SaveSystem` (692 lines), `LTGameManager` (666 lines)
- Direct cross-domain references that bypass LTFunctionLibrary

### 5. Lifecycle Rules

**Game Session Lifecycle (critical path):**

```
1. MainMenu → SelectLevel → MatchInfo configured
2. GameScene loaded
3. LTGameManager.Awake() → register singletons
4. MapGenerator.Generate() → PathGenerator → GroundGenerator → EnvironmentGenerator
5. PlayerData initialized (buildings, inventory, upgrades)
6. LTPlayerController.Start() → StandardInputMode active
7. LTGameManager.onGameStarted fires
8. CyclesManager begins (cycle 1, day mode)
9. [GAMEPLAY LOOP]:
   a. Day phase: build towers, place extractors/processors, connect conveyors
   b. CyclesManager.onCycleChanged → night phase
   c. SpawnersManager activates spawners
   d. Enemies spawn, walk paths, attack PlayerTower
   e. Towers detect, target, fire, apply GE effects
   f. Factory loop: Source → Extractor → Belt → Processor → Inventory
   g. Cycle ends → day phase → repeat
10. Victory: all waves cleared → VictoryAnimation → BossReward
11. Game Over: PlayerTower HP ≤ 0 → GameOverAnimation
12. SaveSystem persists progression
```

**Building Placement Lifecycle:**
```
1. Player selects building from Hotbar/Store
2. BuyModeInputMode activates preview ghost
3. Grid cell validation (occupancy, adjacency, resources)
4. Conveyor auto-connection check (if belt type)
5. Cost deducted via LTGameManager.Pay()
6. GameplayObject instantiated
7. PlacementComponent.Place() → onPlace fires
8. Subscribers react: Tower enables combat, Extractor finds sources, etc.
```

**Tower Combat Lifecycle:**
```
1. TowerController.PerceptionAI detects enemies in range
2. TowerTargetProvider selects best target (e.g., nearest, highest HP)
3. AbilityManager.UseAutoAttack() queues attack
4. AutoAttack variant executes (projectile, direct, over-time)
5. TowerCombatComponent.DoDamageToEnemy() applies damage
6. onDamageEnemy fires → GE_ subscribers trigger (splash, bounce, DoT, etc.)
7. Enemy.CombatComponent.DoDamage() reduces HP
8. If HP ≤ 0: onDie fires → SpawnersManager tracks, resources awarded
```

### 6. C# Feature Guidelines

**Use:**
- `readonly` for fields set once
- `sealed` on classes not intended for inheritance
- Pattern matching for type checks
- String interpolation over concatenation
- `using` declarations for IDisposable
- `Dictionary<K,V>` over `Hashtable`
- `List<T>` over `ArrayList`
- Generic `Storage<T>` pattern (already in source)

**Avoid:**
- `public` fields on MonoBehaviours (use `[SerializeField] private`)
- Allocation in Update/FixedUpdate (pool objects)
- String concatenation in hot paths (use StringBuilder)
- `BinaryFormatter` for new code (security risk — replace with JSON or custom binary)
- `foreach` on non-generic collections in tight loops

**Existing patterns to preserve:**
- `Storage<T>` generic container — clean and reusable
- `GameplayEffect` + `GameplayEffectData` paired pattern — all 25+ effects follow it
- `StatsComponent` + `StatModifier` event-driven stats — well-designed
- `PlacementComponent` event bus — `onPlace`/`onUnplace` is the building lifecycle hook
- `TowerTargetProvider` strategy pattern — clean extension point
- `ProjectileMovement` strategy pattern — clean extension point
- `ConveyorBeltGroup` chain management — complex but well-isolated

### 7. Project-Specific Elements

**Tower Types (13 types × 3 tiers):**
Ballista, Catapult, Bombard, Rockets, SawThrower, LightRay, TeslaCoil, Shockwave, Spikes, AcornCannon, ResinBarrel, SporeCannon, FlyingCannon

**Enemy Types (~27):**
Skeleton, Mushroom, SoldierMushroom, Boss_mushroom, Bat, Bee, BeeWarrior, BattleBee, Boss_bee, Fishman, CrabMesh, HermitCrab, MantaRay, Salamander, BigPenguin, FlyingPenguin, Boss_penguin, BigSnowman, Boss_snowman, Yeti, BlackKnight, LizardWarrior, RatAssasin, Specter, Werewolf, Boss_naga, Boss_orc

**Resource Types:**
Wood, Stone, Iron, Gold (and processed variants via recipes)

**Building Types:**
- Extractors: Wood (T1/T2), Stone (T1/T2)
- Processors: Sawmill, Stonemason, KilnFurnace, Forge, Workshop, EssenceFactory
- Conveyors: Straight, Curve, Splitter, Combiner, Crossing, Underground (all T1/T2)
- Special: 4 Beacon variants, PerkBeacon, SnowfallBeacon, CrystalAltar, CrystalFinder, Obelisk

**Gameplay Effects (25+ types):**
GE_StatModifier, GE_Slow, GE_SlowResistance, GE_Dot, GE_Splash, GE_SplashDamage, GE_ProjectileBounce, GE_ProjectileSplit, GE_DirectDamageChain, GE_GameplayEffectApplier, GE_SplashGameplayEffectApplier, GE_StacksConsumer, GE_StacksConsumerDamage, GE_DisableTower, GE_LifeBasedDamage, GE_Heal, GE_HealLightTower, GE_GiveResources, GE_GiveEffectToBuilding, GE_GiveEffectToEnemy, GE_AddGemSlot, GE_UnlockBuilding, GE_AreaEffectSpawner, GE_Descriptor

**Input Modes:**
Standard (select/inspect/sell), Edit (rearrange), Buy (place new buildings)

**Match Modes:**
Campaign, Endless

### 8. Testing Strategy

**Unit Testable (DataServices):**
- `DS_StatCalculator` — modifier stacking, operation order (Add → Multiply → Override)
- `DS_ConveyorTransport` — belt chain traversal, resource distribution, loop detection
- `DS_SpawnerBalance` — LpS auto-balancing formula correctness
- `DS_Economy` — cost evaluation, refund calculation, resource sufficiency
- `DS_RecipeEvaluator` — input matching, output quantity
- `DS_TowerExperience` — XP thresholds, stat scaling per level
- `DS_PlacementValidator` — grid occupancy, adjacency rules
- `DS_Serializer` — save/load round-trip (replace BinaryFormatter with testable format)
- `DS_EffectStacking` — stack count, duration refresh, max cap
- `DS_PathLayout` — procedural path generation determinism

**Integration Testable (MonoBehaviour):**
- Tower place → detect enemy → fire → damage → GE trigger chain
- Extractor → Conveyor belt chain → Processor → Inventory
- Spawner cycle → wave composition → enemy spawn → path follow → die
- Building placement → cost deduction → grid occupation → PlacementComponent events
- Save → load → verify all ISavable state restored

**Manual Test Scenarios:**
- Build complete factory: extract wood → belt → sawmill → belt → inventory
- Tower upgrade path: place ballista → level up → tier 2 → tier 3
- Full combat cycle: day build → night defend → boss fight → victory
- Snowfall mechanic: controller intensity increases → beacon placement counters
- Fog of war: beacon placement → area reveal → enemy tower discovery
- Trader interaction: wait for trader → buy item → resources deducted

### 9. Key Metrics

| Metric | Current | Target |
|--------|---------|--------|
| God objects (>400 lines) | 10 | 0 (split into DataService + thin MonoBehaviour) |
| Direct singleton access (bypass LTFunctionLibrary) | ~70+ | ≤10 (AudioSystem, SaveSystem acceptable) |
| Public fields on MonoBehaviour | Hundreds | All `[SerializeField] private` |
| Untested business logic | ~100% | DataServices: 80%+ unit test coverage |
| `BinaryFormatter` usage | 1 (SaveSystem) | 0 (replace with JSON or custom binary) |
| FindObjectOfType calls | 0 | 0 (maintain clean pattern) |

## Phase 0 — Core Framework & Data (~75 files)

### File List

**Enums & Constants (~20 files)**
- `EStats.cs`, `DamageType.cs`, `EDamageMultiplier.cs`, `EOrientation.cs`
- `EGameplayObjectType.cs`, `EComparison.cs`, `ECycleMode.cs`, `EInputMode.cs`
- `EMatchMode.cs`, `ENotificationType.cs`, `EValueMode.cs`, `EGameDifficulty.cs`
- `ModifierOperation.cs`, `ETargetProviderType.cs`, `EProjectileMovementType.cs`
- `ECombatState.cs`, `EControllerState.cs`, `ETowerUpgradeState.cs`, `EResourceType.cs`

**Stats System (~8 files)**
- `Stat.cs`, `StatConfig.cs`, `StatModifier.cs`, `StatsComponent.cs`
- `StatConfigVariable.cs`, `StatConfigObject.cs`, `ISampleableData.cs`

**Data Types & Containers (~12 files)**
- `Cost.cs`, `ResourceData.cs`, `FDamageData.cs`, `FDamageReport.cs`
- `RandomizableFloat.cs`, `RandomizableInt.cs`, `WeightedRandomSelector.cs`
- `Timer.cs`, `StorableData.cs`, `Storable.cs`
- `GameplayObjectData.cs`, `GameplayObjectDataGroup.cs`

**Base Classes (~8 files)**
- `GameplayObject.cs`, `Storage.cs` (generic), `Storage_ResourceData.cs`
- `PlacementComponent.cs`, `ISelectable.cs`, `ISavable.cs`

**Utility Libraries (~12 files)**
- `FunctionLibrary.cs` (586 lines — GOD OBJECT), `ExtensionMethods.cs`, `RectExtensions.cs`
- `LTAssetsReferences.cs`, `SavableAttribute.cs`, `SaveComponent.cs`
- Serialization surrogates (`Vector2`, `Vector3`, `Quaternion`)

**Serialization (~5 files)**
- Serialization surrogate selectors, custom formatters

**Third-Party Wrappers (~10 files)**
- `DOTween/` references (external DLL — no source), `HighlightPlus/` (~25 files — read-only third-party)

### What It Looks Like When Running
Stats can be created, modified, and queried. Resources and costs can be evaluated. Storage containers hold typed data. Gameplay objects have placement and serialization. Utility functions available. No visible game yet — pure data backbone.

### Difficulty: ★★☆ Medium
Well-defined data types and enums. `FunctionLibrary` (586 lines) is the only god object here. Stats system (`StatsComponent` + `StatModifier`) is event-heavy but cleanly designed with `onStatChanged` delegates.

## Phase 1 — Grid & Map Generation (~25 files)

### File List

**Grid Core (~6 files)**
- `Grid.cs`, `GridCell.cs`
- `LightTower/Tile.cs`, `LightTower/PathTile.cs`, `LightTower/Path.cs`
- `PathChunk.cs`

**Map Generation (~8 files)**
- `MapGenerator.cs`, `PathGenerator.cs`, `GroundGenerator.cs`, `GroundChunk.cs`
- `EnvironmentGenerator.cs` (786 lines — GOD OBJECT)
- `LevelData.cs`, `LevelController.cs`, `LTLevelController.cs`

**Fog of War (~4 files)**
- `FogOfWarController.cs`, `FogOfWarArea.cs`

**Placement (~3 files)**
- `PlacementComponent.cs` (if not in P0), `PlacementDirectionArrow.cs`

**Map Objects base (~4 files)**
- `MapObject.cs`, `Source.cs`, `Resource.cs`

### What It Looks Like When Running
Procedurally generated map with tiles, paths, and terrain. Grid visible with placeable cells. Fog of war obscures unexplored areas. Sources (wood, stone) scattered on the map. No buildings or enemies yet — empty world with resources.

### Difficulty: ★★★ Hard
`EnvironmentGenerator` (786 lines) spawns all map objects and is the most complex god object in this phase. `PathGenerator` creates procedural paths that enemies will follow. Grid system is the spatial foundation everything builds on.

## Phase 2 — Character & Combat Framework (~35 files)

### File List

**Character Base (~6 files)**
- `Character.cs`, `Controller.cs`, `MovementComponent.cs`
- `AnimationComponent.cs`, `TeamComponent.cs`

**Combat Core (~5 files)**
- `CombatComponent.cs`, `TowerCombatComponent.cs`, `EnemyCombatComponent.cs`

**Ability Framework (~12 files)**
- `Ability.cs` (abstract), `ActiveAbility.cs` (abstract), `PassiveAbility.cs`
- `AutoAttack.cs` (abstract), `AbilityManager.cs`, `AbilityQueue.cs`
- `QueuedAbility.cs`, `FActiveAbilityInputData.cs`
- `AbilityUnlockCondition.cs`, `AUC_LocalAbilityUsed.cs`

**FSM (~5 files)**
- `FSMComponent.cs`, `FSMState.cs`, `FSMCondition.cs`, `FSMTask.cs`, `FSMTransition.cs`

**Perception (~5 files)**
- `PerceptionAI.cs`, `PerceptionSense.cs`
- `PerceptionSense_Sight.cs`, `PerceptionSense_Hearing.cs`, `PerceptionSense_Proximity.cs`
- `PerceptionNoise.cs`

**Gameplay Effect Base (~2 files)**
- `GameplayEffect.cs` (abstract), `GameplayEffectData.cs` (abstract, ScriptableObject)
- `GameplayEffectsComponent.cs`

### What It Looks Like When Running
Characters can be instantiated with stats, take/deal damage, die. FSM drives state transitions. Perception system detects targets within range. Ability queue processes attack commands. No specific tower or enemy behavior yet — generic character skeleton.

### Difficulty: ★★★ Hard
The ability pipeline (`AbilityManager` → `AbilityQueue` → `ActiveAbility` → `AutoAttack`) is the critical chain. `TowerCombatComponent` extends `CombatComponent` with tower-specific damage events (`onDamageEnemy`) that 10+ GE_ classes subscribe to. Getting this event wiring right is essential.

---

## Phase 3 — Tower System (~45 files)

### File List

**Tower Core (~6 files)**
- `Tower.cs` (409 lines — complex), `TowerController.cs`
- `TowerAnimationComponent.cs`, `TowerAutoAttack.cs` (abstract)
- `PlayerTower.cs`, `PlayerTowerHealthBar.cs`

**Auto-Attack Variants (~8 files)**
- `AutoAttack_collisionCheck.cs`, `AutoAttack_directDamage.cs`
- `AutoAttack_overTime.cs`, `AutoAttack_overTime_laser.cs`
- `AutoAttack_projectile.cs`, `AutoAttack_projectile_splash.cs`

**Target Providers (~10 files)**
- `TowerTargetProvider.cs` (abstract)
- `TTP_Nearest.cs`, `TTP_HighestHealth.cs`, `TTP_LowestHealth.cs`
- `TTP_FastestSpeed.cs`, `TTP_SlowestSpeed.cs`
- `TTP_NearestToPosition.cs`, `TTP_FarthestFromTower.cs`
- `TTP_FirstTarget.cs`, `TTP_LastTarget.cs`, `TTP_Random.cs`

**Projectile System (~10 files)**
- `Projectile.cs`, `ProjectileMovement.cs` (abstract)
- `ProjectileMovement_Forward.cs`, `ProjectileMovement_Homing.cs`
- `ProjectileMovement_Parable.cs`, `ProjectileMovement_ToTarget.cs`
- `DirectDamageParticles.cs`

**Area Effects (~6 files)**
- `AreaEffect.cs`, `AreaEffectModule.cs` (abstract)
- `AreaEffectModule_damage.cs`, `AreaEffectModule_effect.cs`
- `AreaEffectModule_slow.cs`

**Tower Data (~5 files)**
- `TowerData.cs` (ScriptableObject), `TowerUpgradeData.cs`
- `TowerLevelUpData.cs`

### What It Looks Like When Running
Towers placed on grid, detect enemies via perception, select targets using priority strategies (nearest, highest HP, etc.), fire projectiles or deal direct damage. Projectiles fly using various movement patterns. Area effects splash damage. Towers level up and can be upgraded to new tiers.

### Difficulty: ★★★ Hard
Tower system is the primary gameplay mechanic. `TowerController` orchestrates perception → targeting → ability use. 10 target provider variants and 6 attack variants make this phase the most variant-heavy. `Tower.cs` (409 lines) manages experience, obelisk buffs, and upgrade chains.

- `GE_ProjectileSplit.cs`, `GE_ProjectileSplitData.cs`
- `GE_DirectDamageChain.cs`, `GE_DirectDamageChainData.cs`

**Applicator Effects (~6 files)**
- `GE_GameplayEffectApplier.cs`, `GE_GameplayEffectApplierData.cs`
- `GE_SplashGameplayEffectApplier.cs`, `GE_SplashGameplayEffectApplierData.cs`
- `GE_StacksConsumer.cs`, `GE_StacksConsumerData.cs`

- `GE_DisableTower.cs`, `GE_DisableTowerData.cs`

**Building/Tower Effects (~4 files)**
- `GE_GiveEffectToBuilding.cs`, `GE_GiveEffectToBuildingData.cs`
- `GE_GiveEffectToEnemy.cs`, `GE_GiveEffectToEnemyData.cs`
- `GE_AddGemSlot.cs`, `GE_AddGemSlotData.cs`

**Misc (~3 files)**
- `GE_AreaEffectSpawner.cs`, `GE_AreaEffectSpawnerData.cs`
- `GE_Descriptor.cs`, `GE_DescriptorData.cs`
- `ResourceActivatedGEData.cs`

**Gems (~3 files)**
- `GemsComponent.cs`, `GemData.cs`, `GemUI.cs`

### What It Looks Like When Running
Towers apply gameplay effects when hitting enemies: slows, DoTs, splash damage, projectile bounces/splits, chain lightning. Stacking effects accumulate and can be consumed for burst damage. Gems add GE slots to towers. Buildings can receive/give effects. Visual feedback for heals, damage chains, splashes.

### Difficulty: ★★☆ Medium
Each GE_ pair (runtime + data) follows a consistent abstract pattern: `GameplayEffectData` (ScriptableObject config) → `GameplayEffect` (runtime behavior). Most are 50-150 lines. The challenge is the event subscription wiring — many GE_ classes subscribe to `TowerCombatComponent.onDamageEnemy`.
